File: main.go

package main

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"strings"

	"crawler/pkg/config"
	"crawler/pkg/crawler"
	"crawler/pkg/scraper"
)

const version = "2.0.0"

func main() {
	if len(os.Args) < 2 {
		printHelp()
		os.Exit(0)
	}

	command := os.Args[1]

	switch strings.ToLower(command) {
	case "crawl":
		if len(os.Args) < 3 {
			fmt.Println("Error: Missing config name")
			fmt.Println("Usage: scraper crawl <config-name>")
			fmt.Println("Example: scraper crawl brooklinen")
			os.Exit(1)
		}
		configName := os.Args[2]
		if err := runCrawl(configName); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
			os.Exit(1)
		}

	case "scrape":
		if len(os.Args) < 3 {
			fmt.Println("Error: Missing config name")
			fmt.Println("Usage: scraper scrape <config-name>")
			fmt.Println("Example: scraper scrape brooklinen")
			os.Exit(1)
		}
		configName := os.Args[2]
		if err := runScrape(configName); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
			os.Exit(1)
		}

	case "init":
		if err := runInit(); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
			os.Exit(1)
		}

	case "list":
		if err := runList(); err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("✗ Error: %v\n", err)
			os.Exit(1)
		}

	case "help", "--help", "-h":
		printHelp()

	case "version", "--version", "-v":
		fmt.Printf("Web Scraper v%s\n", version)

	default:
		fmt.Printf("Unknown command: %s\n\n", command)
		printHelp()
		os.Exit(1)
	}
}

func printHelp() {
	fmt.Println(`
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Web Scraper - Crawl websites and extract data         │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

USAGE:
  scraper <command> <config-name>

COMMANDS:
  crawl <name>    Crawl website and discover URLs
  scrape <name>   Scrape products from discovered URLs
  init [name]     Create config in configs/ directory (default: configs/default.json)
  list            List available configs
  help            Show this help message
  version         Show version information

EXAMPLES:
  # First time setup
  scraper init                   # Creates configs/default.json
  scraper init mysite            # Creates configs/mysite.json

  # Edit the config file with your site details, then:
  scraper crawl default          # Uses configs/default.json
  scraper scrape default         # Uses configs/default.json

  # Or use named configs:
  scraper crawl brooklinen       # Uses configs/brooklinen.json
  scraper scrape brooklinen      # Uses configs/brooklinen.json

  # List all available configurations:
  scraper list

CONFIG LOCATION:
  All configs are stored in: configs/<name>.json

WORKFLOW:
  1. scraper init mysite         # Create configs/mysite.json
  2. Edit configs/mysite.json    # Set domain, selectors, etc.
  3. scraper crawl mysite        # Discover product URLs
  4. scraper scrape mysite       # Extract product data

OUTPUT:
  Crawler: Saves URLs to path specified in config (output.crawler_path)
  Scraper: Saves products to path specified in config (output.scraper_path)

Need help? Check README.md or visit: github.com/yourusername/scraper
`)
}

func runCrawl(configName string) error {
	fmt.Printf("Loading config '%s'...\n", configName)

	cfg, err := config.Load(configName)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("✓ Config loaded: %s\n", cfg.Name)
	fmt.Printf("  Domain: %s\n", cfg.Domain)
	fmt.Printf("  Output: %s\n", cfg.Output.CrawlerPath)
	fmt.Println()

	// Run the crawler
	return crawler.Run(cfg)
}

func runScrape(configName string) error {
	fmt.Printf("Loading config '%s'...\n", configName)

	cfg, err := config.Load(configName)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("✓ Config loaded: %s\n", cfg.Name)
	fmt.Printf("  Domain: %s\n", cfg.Domain)
	fmt.Printf("  Brand: %s\n", cfg.Scraper.Brand)
	fmt.Printf("  Output: %s\n", cfg.Output.ScraperPath)
	fmt.Println()

	// Run the scraper
	return scraper.Run(cfg)
}

func runInit() error {
	// Get config name from user or use default
	configName := "default"
	if len(os.Args) > 2 {
		configName = os.Args[2]
	}

	// Ensure configs directory exists
	if err := os.MkdirAll("configs", 0755); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create configs directory: %w", err)
	}

	configFile := fmt.Sprintf("configs/%s.json", configName)

	// Check if config already exists
	if _, err := os.Stat(configFile); err == nil {
		fmt.Printf("⚠ Warning: %s already exists\n", configFile)
		fmt.Print("Overwrite? (y/N): ")
		var response string
		fmt.Scanln(&response)
		if strings.ToLower(response) != "y" {
			fmt.Println("Cancelled.")
			return nil
		}
	}

	// Create example config
	exampleConfig := config.Config{
		Name:   configName,
		Domain: "https://example.com",
		Output: config.OutputConfig{
			CrawlerPath: "output/urls",
			ScraperPath: "output/products",
		},
		Crawler: config.CrawlerConfig{
			MaxDepth:       10,
			Parallelism:    4,
			BatchSize:      100,
			DelayMS:        500,
			RandomDelayMS:  500,
			TimeoutMinutes: 5,
			Async:          true,
			UserAgent:      "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36",
			DatabaseName:   "urls.csv",
		},
		Scraper: config.ScraperConfig{
			RateLimitMs:    500,
			BatchSize:      10,
			TimeoutSeconds: 30,
			Brand:          "My Brand",
			Country:        "USA",
			Currency:       "USD",
			Selectors: config.Selectors{
				Title:        []string{"meta[property='og:title']", "h1"},
				Description:  []string{"meta[property='og:description']", ".description"},
				MainImage:    []string{"meta[property='og:image']", ".product-image img"},
				Price:        []string{"meta[property='product:price:amount']", ".price"},
				SalePrice:    []string{".sale-price"},
				Sizes:        []string{"select[name*='size'] option"},
				Availability: []string{"button.add-to-cart"},
			},
			ExtractionRules: config.ExtractionRules{
				ProductPaths: []string{"/products/", "/item/"},
			},
		},
	}

	// Set defaults
	exampleConfig.SetDefaults()

	// Write to file
	file, err := os.Create(configFile)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create config file: %w", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	encoder := json.NewEncoder(file)
	encoder.SetIndent("", "  ")
	if err := encoder.Encode(exampleConfig); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write config: %w", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("✓ Created %s\n\n", configFile)
	fmt.Println("Next steps:")
	fmt.Printf("  1. Edit %s\n", configFile)
	fmt.Println("  2. Set 'domain' to your target website")
	fmt.Println("  3. Customize selectors for your site")
	fmt.Printf("  4. Run: scraper crawl %s\n", configName)
	fmt.Println()
	fmt.Println("See configs/example.json for a fully documented template")

	return nil
}

func runList() error {
	configs, err := config.ListAvailableConfigs()
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if len(configs) == 0 {
		fmt.Println("No configurations found.")
		fmt.Println()
		fmt.Println("Create one with:")
		fmt.Println("  scraper init                  # Creates config.json")
		fmt.Println("  cp config.json configs/mysite.json  # Create named config")
		return nil
	}

	fmt.Println()
	fmt.Println("Available configurations:")
	fmt.Println()

	for _, name := range configs {
		cfg, err := config.Load(name)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("  • %s (error loading)\n", name)
			continue
		}
		fmt.Printf("  • %-20s (%s)\n", name, cfg.Domain)
	}

	fmt.Println()
	fmt.Println("Usage: scraper crawl <name>")
	fmt.Println("       scraper scrape <name>")

	return nil
}

File: insert.go

package main

import (
	"database/sql"
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"

	_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"
)

func main() {
	// Get arguments
	args := os.Args
	if len(args) < 2 {
		fmt.Println("Usage: go run main.go <folder_path> [dbname]")
		return
	}

	root := args[1]
	dbname := "justdata.db"
	if len(args) > 2 {
		dbname = args[2]
	}

	// Open SQLite DB
	db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dbname)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	defer db.Close()

	// Create table if not exists
	createTable := `
	CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS urls (
		id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
		url TEXT,
		timestamp TEXT
	);`
	_, err = db.Exec(createTable)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}

	// Walk through all folders for CSV
	err = filepath.Walk(root, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		if !info.IsDir() && filepath.Ext(path) == ".csv" {
			fmt.Println("Processing:", path)
			if err := processCSV(db, path); err != nil {
				log.Println("Error processing", path, ":", err)
			}
		}
		return nil
	})
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
}

func processCSV(db *sql.DB, filename string) error {
	file, err := os.Open(filename)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	records, err := reader.ReadAll()
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	for i, row := range records {
		if i == 0 {
			continue // skip header
		}
		if len(row) < 2 {
			continue
		}
		url := row[0]
		timestamp := row[1]

		_, err := db.Exec("INSERT INTO urls (url, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?)", url, timestamp)
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
	}
	return nil
}

File: config.go

package config

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"
)

// Config represents the unified configuration for both crawler and scraper
type Config struct {
	Name   string       `json:"name"`
	Domain string       `json:"domain"`
	Output OutputConfig `json:"output"`

	Crawler CrawlerConfig `json:"crawler"`
	Scraper ScraperConfig `json:"scraper"`
}

// OutputConfig defines where to save crawler and scraper outputs
type OutputConfig struct {
	CrawlerPath string `json:"crawler_path"` // Where to save discovered URLs
	ScraperPath string `json:"scraper_path"` // Where to save product data
}

// CrawlerConfig holds crawler-specific settings
type CrawlerConfig struct {
	MaxDepth       int    `json:"max_depth"`
	Parallelism    int    `json:"parallelism"`
	BatchSize      int    `json:"batch_size"`
	DelayMS        int    `json:"delay_ms"`
	RandomDelayMS  int    `json:"random_delay_ms"`
	TimeoutMinutes int    `json:"timeout_minutes"`
	Async          bool   `json:"async"`
	UserAgent      string `json:"user_agent"`
	DatabaseName   string `json:"database_name"` // "urls.csv" or "urls.db"
	MaxOpenConns   int    `json:"max_open_conns,omitempty"`
	MaxIdleConns   int    `json:"max_idle_conns,omitempty"`
	WriteBufferSize int   `json:"write_buffer_size,omitempty"`
}

// ScraperConfig holds scraper-specific settings
type ScraperConfig struct {
	RateLimitMs    int    `json:"rate_limit_ms"`
	BatchSize      int    `json:"batch_size"`
	TimeoutSeconds int    `json:"timeout_seconds"`
	Brand          string `json:"brand"`
	Country        string `json:"country"`
	Currency       string `json:"currency"`

	Selectors          Selectors          `json:"selectors"`
	ExtractionRules    ExtractionRules    `json:"extraction_rules"`
	FallbackExtraction FallbackExtraction `json:"fallback_extraction,omitempty"`
}

// Selectors defines CSS selectors for extracting product data
type Selectors struct {
	Title        []string `json:"title"`
	Description  []string `json:"description"`
	MainImage    []string `json:"main_image"`
	ImageGallery []string `json:"image_gallery,omitempty"`
	Price        []string `json:"price"`
	Currency     []string `json:"currency,omitempty"`
	SalePrice    []string `json:"sale_price,omitempty"`
	Sizes        []string `json:"sizes,omitempty"`
	Availability []string `json:"availability,omitempty"`
	SKU          []string `json:"sku,omitempty"`
	Category     []string `json:"category,omitempty"`
}

// ExtractionRules defines rules for URL filtering and data extraction
type ExtractionRules struct {
	CollectionPaths      []string `json:"collection_paths,omitempty"`
	ProductPaths         []string `json:"product_paths"`
	CollectionFromURL    string   `json:"collection_from_url,omitempty"`
	ProductURLFilter     string   `json:"product_url_filter,omitempty"`
	AvailabilityKeywords []string `json:"availability_keywords,omitempty"`
	SizeFilters          []string `json:"size_filters,omitempty"`
	PriceCleanup         struct {
		RemoveChars  []string `json:"remove_chars"`
		ParseAsFloat bool     `json:"parse_as_float"`
	} `json:"price_cleanup,omitempty"`
}

// FallbackExtraction configures fallback extraction methods
type FallbackExtraction struct {
	EnableJSONLD         bool `json:"enable_json_ld"`
	EnableMicrodata      bool `json:"enable_microdata"`
	EnableTextExtraction bool `json:"enable_text_extraction,omitempty"`
}

// Load loads a configuration from file
// It searches in configs/ directory
func Load(name string) (*Config, error) {
	// Search path: configs/<name>.json
	searchPaths := []string{
		filepath.Join("configs", name+".json"),
	}

	for _, path := range searchPaths {
		cfg, err := loadFromFile(path)
		if err == nil {
			// Validate required fields
			if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
				return nil, fmt.Errorf("invalid config '%s': %w", path, err)
			}
			// Set defaults
			cfg.SetDefaults()
			return cfg, nil
		}
	}

	// Config not found, provide helpful error
	return nil, fmt.Errorf(
		"config not found for '%s'\n\nSearched in:\n  • %s\n\nRun 'scraper init' to create a template config",
		name,
		strings.Join(searchPaths, "\n  • "),
	)
}

// loadFromFile loads config from a specific file path
func loadFromFile(path string) (*Config, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(path)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	var cfg Config
	decoder := json.NewDecoder(file)
	if err := decoder.Decode(&cfg); err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse JSON: %w", err)
	}

	return &cfg, nil
}

// Validate checks if all required fields are present
func (c *Config) Validate() error {
	var missing []string

	if c.Name == "" {
		missing = append(missing, "name")
	}
	if c.Domain == "" {
		missing = append(missing, "domain")
	}
	if c.Crawler.MaxDepth == 0 {
		missing = append(missing, "crawler.max_depth")
	}
	if c.Scraper.Brand == "" {
		missing = append(missing, "scraper.brand")
	}

	if len(missing) > 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("missing required fields: %s", strings.Join(missing, ", "))
	}

	return nil
}

// SetDefaults sets default values for optional fields
func (c *Config) SetDefaults() {
	// Output paths
	if c.Output.CrawlerPath == "" {
		c.Output.CrawlerPath = "output/urls"
	}
	if c.Output.ScraperPath == "" {
		c.Output.ScraperPath = "output/products"
	}

	// Crawler defaults
	if c.Crawler.Parallelism == 0 {
		c.Crawler.Parallelism = 4
	}
	if c.Crawler.BatchSize == 0 {
		c.Crawler.BatchSize = 100
	}
	if c.Crawler.DelayMS == 0 {
		c.Crawler.DelayMS = 500
	}
	if c.Crawler.TimeoutMinutes == 0 {
		c.Crawler.TimeoutMinutes = 5
	}
	if c.Crawler.UserAgent == "" {
		c.Crawler.UserAgent = "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36"
	}
	if c.Crawler.DatabaseName == "" {
		c.Crawler.DatabaseName = "urls.csv"
	}
	if c.Crawler.MaxOpenConns == 0 {
		c.Crawler.MaxOpenConns = 20
	}
	if c.Crawler.MaxIdleConns == 0 {
		c.Crawler.MaxIdleConns = 10
	}
	if c.Crawler.WriteBufferSize == 0 {
		c.Crawler.WriteBufferSize = 1000
	}

	// Scraper defaults
	if c.Scraper.RateLimitMs == 0 {
		c.Scraper.RateLimitMs = 500
	}
	if c.Scraper.BatchSize == 0 {
		c.Scraper.BatchSize = 10
	}
	if c.Scraper.TimeoutSeconds == 0 {
		c.Scraper.TimeoutSeconds = 30
	}
	if c.Scraper.Currency == "" {
		c.Scraper.Currency = "USD"
	}
	if c.Scraper.Country == "" {
		c.Scraper.Country = "Global"
	}

	// Price cleanup defaults
	if len(c.Scraper.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.RemoveChars) == 0 {
		c.Scraper.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.RemoveChars = []string{",", "$", "₹", "€", "£"}
		c.Scraper.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.ParseAsFloat = true
	}

	// Availability keywords defaults
	if len(c.Scraper.ExtractionRules.AvailabilityKeywords) == 0 {
		c.Scraper.ExtractionRules.AvailabilityKeywords = []string{
			"sold out", "out of stock", "unavailable",
		}
	}
}

// ListAvailableConfigs lists all available configuration files
func ListAvailableConfigs() ([]string, error) {
	var configs []string

	// Check configs/ directory
	entries, err := os.ReadDir("configs")
	if err == nil {
		for _, entry := range entries {
			if !entry.IsDir() && strings.HasSuffix(entry.Name(), ".json") {
				name := strings.TrimSuffix(entry.Name(), ".json")
				configs = append(configs, name)
			}
		}
	}

	// Check for default config.json
	if _, err := os.Stat("config.json"); err == nil {
		configs = append(configs, "default")
	}

	return configs, nil
}

File: crawler.go

package crawler

import (
	"context"
	"database/sql"
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/url"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"sync/atomic"
	"time"

	"crawler/pkg/config"

	"github.com/gocolly/colly"
	_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"
)

// URLData represents a discovered URL with metadata
type URLData struct {
	URL       string
	TimeStamp time.Time
	SiteName  string
}

// CrawlStats tracks crawling performance and errors
type CrawlStats struct {
	URLsProcessed int64
	URLsWritten   int64
	ErrorCount    int64
	StartTime     time.Time
	mu            sync.RWMutex
	errors        []string
}

// NewCrawlStats creates a new stats tracker
func NewCrawlStats() *CrawlStats {
	return &CrawlStats{
		StartTime: time.Now(),
		errors:    make([]string, 0),
	}
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementProcessed() {
	atomic.AddInt64(&cs.URLsProcessed, 1)
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementWritten() {
	atomic.AddInt64(&cs.URLsWritten, 1)
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementErrors() {
	atomic.AddInt64(&cs.ErrorCount, 1)
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) AddError(err string) {
	cs.mu.Lock()
	defer cs.mu.Unlock()
	cs.errors = append(cs.errors, fmt.Sprintf("[%s] %s", time.Now().Format("15:04:05"), err))
	if len(cs.errors) > 100 {
		cs.errors = cs.errors[1:]
	}
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) GetStats() (int64, int64, int64, time.Duration, []string) {
	cs.mu.RLock()
	defer cs.mu.RUnlock()
	return atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.URLsProcessed),
		atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.URLsWritten),
		atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.ErrorCount),
		time.Since(cs.StartTime),
		append([]string{}, cs.errors...)
}

func (cs *CrawlStats) PrintStats() {
	processed, written, errorCount, duration, errors := cs.GetStats()
	log.Printf("=== CRAWL STATISTICS ===")
	log.Printf("URLs Processed: %d", processed)
	log.Printf("URLs Written: %d", written)
	log.Printf("Error Count: %d", errorCount)
	log.Printf("Duration: %v", duration.Truncate(time.Second))
	if processed > 0 {
		log.Printf("Processing Rate: %.2f URLs/second", float64(processed)/duration.Seconds())
	}
	if len(errors) > 0 {
		log.Printf("Recent Errors:")
		for i, err := range errors {
			if i >= 10 {
				log.Printf("... and %d more errors", len(errors)-10)
				break
			}
			log.Printf("  %s", err)
		}
	}
	log.Printf("========================")
}

// BatchWriter writes URLs to CSV files in batches
type BatchWriter struct {
	results     []URLData
	batchSize   int
	mu          sync.Mutex
	fileCounter int
	baseDir     string
	siteName    string
	stats       *CrawlStats
}

// Asset URL filtering
var blockedExtensions = []string{
	".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".gif", ".webp", ".bmp", ".svg",
	".ico", ".css", ".js", ".json", ".pdf", ".mp4", ".avi",
	".mov", ".zip", ".rar", ".woff", ".ttf",
}

var blockedPathPatterns = []string{
	"/image/upload/", "/images/", "/static/", "/assets/",
	"/media/", "/fonts/", "/js/", "/css/",
}

var blockedHostKeywords = []string{
	"cdn.", "assets.", "media.",
}

func isAssetURL(u string) bool {
	parsed, err := url.Parse(u)
	if err != nil {
		return false
	}

	urlLower := strings.ToLower(u)
	for _, ext := range blockedExtensions {
		if strings.HasSuffix(urlLower, ext) {
			return true
		}
	}

	for _, pattern := range blockedPathPatterns {
		if strings.Contains(parsed.Path, pattern) {
			return true
		}
	}

	hostLower := strings.ToLower(parsed.Hostname())
	for _, kw := range blockedHostKeywords {
		if strings.Contains(hostLower, kw) {
			return true
		}
	}

	return false
}

func hasBlockedExtension(u string) bool {
	lower := strings.ToLower(u)
	for _, ext := range blockedExtensions {
		if strings.HasSuffix(lower, ext) {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

func NewBatchWriter(siteName string, cfg *config.Config, stats *CrawlStats) (*BatchWriter, error) {
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	baseDir := filepath.Join(cfg.Output.CrawlerPath, siteName, fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s", siteName, timestamp))

	if err := os.MkdirAll(baseDir, 0755); err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create directory %s: %w", baseDir, err)
	}

	return &BatchWriter{
		results:   make([]URLData, 0, cfg.Crawler.BatchSize),
		batchSize: cfg.Crawler.BatchSize,
		baseDir:   baseDir,
		siteName:  siteName,
		stats:     stats,
	}, nil
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Add(data URLData) {
	bw.mu.Lock()
	defer bw.mu.Unlock()
	bw.results = append(bw.results, data)
	bw.stats.IncrementProcessed()
	if len(bw.results) >= bw.batchSize {
		bw.writeBatch()
	}
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) writeBatch() {
	if len(bw.results) == 0 {
		return
	}

	filename := fmt.Sprintf("%s/batch%d.csv", bw.baseDir, bw.fileCounter)
	log.Printf("Writing batch %d with %d URLs to %s", bw.fileCounter, len(bw.results), filename)

	if err := writeToCSV(filename, bw.results); err != nil {
		errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Error writing CSV batch %d: %v", bw.fileCounter, err)
		log.Printf(errMsg)
		bw.stats.AddError(errMsg)
		bw.stats.IncrementErrors()
		return
	}

	bw.stats.IncrementWritten()
	bw.fileCounter++
	bw.results = make([]URLData, 0, bw.batchSize)
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Flush() {
	bw.mu.Lock()
	defer bw.mu.Unlock()
	bw.writeBatch()
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Close() error {
	bw.Flush()
	return nil
}

// AsyncSQLiteWriter writes URLs to SQLite database asynchronously
type AsyncSQLiteWriter struct {
	db          *sql.DB
	ctx         context.Context
	cancel      context.CancelFunc
	dataChan    chan URLData
	flushChan   chan chan struct{}
	closeChan   chan chan error
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	batchSize   int
	siteName    string
	tableName   string
	stats       *CrawlStats
	writeBuffer []URLData
	bufferMu    sync.Mutex
}

func NewAsyncSQLiteWriter(siteName string, cfg *config.Config, stats *CrawlStats) (*AsyncSQLiteWriter, error) {
	dbDir := filepath.Join(cfg.Output.CrawlerPath, siteName)
	if err := os.MkdirAll(dbDir, 0755); err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create directory %s: %w", dbDir, err)
	}

	dbFileName := strings.TrimSuffix(cfg.Crawler.DatabaseName, ".db")
	dbPath := filepath.Join(dbDir, fmt.Sprintf("%s.db", dbFileName))

	dsn := fmt.Sprintf("%s?_journal_mode=WAL&_synchronous=NORMAL&_cache_size=100000&_temp_store=memory&_mmap_size=268435456", dbPath)
	db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dsn)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to open database: %w", err)
	}

	db.SetMaxOpenConns(cfg.Crawler.MaxOpenConns)
	db.SetMaxIdleConns(cfg.Crawler.MaxIdleConns)
	db.SetConnMaxLifetime(time.Hour)

	if err := db.Ping(); err != nil {
		db.Close()
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to ping database: %w", err)
	}

	ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())

	tableName := fmt.Sprintf("urls_%s", strings.ReplaceAll(cfg.Name, "-", "_"))

	writer := &AsyncSQLiteWriter{
		db:          db,
		ctx:         ctx,
		cancel:      cancel,
		dataChan:    make(chan URLData, cfg.Crawler.WriteBufferSize),
		flushChan:   make(chan chan struct{}, 1),
		closeChan:   make(chan chan error, 1),
		batchSize:   cfg.Crawler.BatchSize,
		siteName:    siteName,
		tableName:   tableName,
		stats:       stats,
		writeBuffer: make([]URLData, 0, cfg.Crawler.BatchSize),
	}

	if err := writer.initializeDatabase(); err != nil {
		writer.Close()
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize database: %w", err)
	}

	writer.wg.Add(1)
	go writer.writeWorker()

	return writer, nil
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) initializeDatabase() error {
	createTableSQL := fmt.Sprintf(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS %s (
		id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
		url TEXT NOT NULL,
		timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL,
		site_name TEXT NOT NULL,
		created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
		UNIQUE(url)
	);`, asw.tableName)

	if _, err := asw.db.ExecContext(asw.ctx, createTableSQL); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create table: %w", err)
	}

	indexes := []string{
		fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_url ON %s(url);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
		fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_site_name ON %s(site_name);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
		fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_timestamp ON %s(timestamp);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
	}

	for _, indexSQL := range indexes {
		if _, err := asw.db.ExecContext(asw.ctx, indexSQL); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Warning: Failed to create index: %v", err)
		}
	}

	return nil
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) writeWorker() {
	defer asw.wg.Done()
	ticker := time.NewTicker(5 * time.Second)
	defer ticker.Stop()

	for {
		select {
		case <-asw.ctx.Done():
			asw.flushBuffer()
			return

		case data := <-asw.dataChan:
			asw.bufferMu.Lock()
			asw.writeBuffer = append(asw.writeBuffer, data)
			shouldFlush := len(asw.writeBuffer) >= asw.batchSize
			asw.bufferMu.Unlock()

			if shouldFlush {
				asw.flushBuffer()
			}

		case respChan := <-asw.flushChan:
			asw.flushBuffer()
			respChan <- struct{}{}

		case respChan := <-asw.closeChan:
			asw.flushBuffer()
			respChan <- nil
			return

		case <-ticker.C:
			asw.bufferMu.Lock()
			hasData := len(asw.writeBuffer) > 0
			asw.bufferMu.Unlock()
			if hasData {
				asw.flushBuffer()
			}
		}
	}
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) flushBuffer() {
	asw.bufferMu.Lock()
	if len(asw.writeBuffer) == 0 {
		asw.bufferMu.Unlock()
		return
	}

	batch := make([]URLData, len(asw.writeBuffer))
	copy(batch, asw.writeBuffer)
	asw.writeBuffer = asw.writeBuffer[:0]
	asw.bufferMu.Unlock()

	if err := asw.writeBatch(batch); err != nil {
		errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Failed to write batch to SQLite: %v", err)
		log.Printf(errMsg)
		asw.stats.AddError(errMsg)
		asw.stats.IncrementErrors()
		return
	}

	asw.stats.IncrementWritten()
	log.Printf("Wrote batch of %d URLs to SQLite (Total processed: %d)",
		len(batch), atomic.LoadInt64(&asw.stats.URLsProcessed))
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) writeBatch(batch []URLData) error {
	if len(batch) == 0 {
		return nil
	}

	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(asw.ctx, 30*time.Second)
	defer cancel()

	tx, err := asw.db.BeginTx(ctx, &sql.TxOptions{
		Isolation: sql.LevelReadCommitted,
	})
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to begin transaction: %w", err)
	}

	insertSQL := fmt.Sprintf("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO %s (url, timestamp, site_name) VALUES (?, ?, ?)", asw.tableName)
	stmt, err := tx.PrepareContext(ctx, insertSQL)
	if err != nil {
		tx.Rollback()
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to prepare statement: %w", err)
	}
	defer stmt.Close()

	for _, data := range batch {
		if _, err := stmt.ExecContext(ctx, data.URL, data.TimeStamp, data.SiteName); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Warning: Failed to insert URL %s: %v", data.URL, err)
		}
	}

	if err := tx.Commit(); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to commit transaction: %w", err)
	}

	return nil
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Add(data URLData) {
	asw.stats.IncrementProcessed()
	select {
	case asw.dataChan <- data:
	case <-asw.ctx.Done():
	default:
		log.Printf("Warning: Write buffer full, may be blocking")
		select {
		case asw.dataChan <- data:
		case <-asw.ctx.Done():
		}
	}
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Flush() {
	respChan := make(chan struct{})
	select {
	case asw.flushChan <- respChan:
		<-respChan
	case <-time.After(10 * time.Second):
		log.Printf("Warning: Flush timeout")
	}
}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Close() error {
	asw.cancel()

	respChan := make(chan error)
	select {
	case asw.closeChan <- respChan:
		err := <-respChan
		asw.wg.Wait()
		asw.db.Close()
		return err
	case <-time.After(30 * time.Second):
		log.Printf("Warning: Close timeout, forcing shutdown")
		asw.wg.Wait()
		return asw.db.Close()
	}
}

type Writer interface {
	Add(URLData)
	Flush()
	Close() error
}

func writeToCSV(filename string, results []URLData) error {
	file, err := os.Create(filename)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create CSV file: %w", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	if err := writer.Write([]string{"URL", "Timestamp", "SiteName"}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write CSV header: %w", err)
	}

	for _, r := range results {
		if err := writer.Write([]string{r.URL, r.TimeStamp.Format(time.RFC3339), r.SiteName}); err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("failed to write CSV row: %w", err)
		}
	}
	return nil
}

func isValidURL(urlStr string) bool {
	u, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	return err == nil && (u.Scheme == "http" || u.Scheme == "https") && u.Host != ""
}

func cleanURL(urlStr string) string {
	u, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	if err != nil {
		return ""
	}
	u.Fragment = ""
	return u.String()
}

// isProductURL checks if a URL matches product path patterns from config
func isProductURL(urlStr string, cfg *config.Config) bool {
	if cfg == nil || len(cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths) == 0 {
		return true // If no product paths defined, accept all URLs
	}

	for _, path := range cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths {
		if strings.Contains(urlStr, path) {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

func isSQLiteDatabase(databaseName string) bool {
	return strings.HasSuffix(strings.ToLower(databaseName), ".db")
}

// Run starts the crawler with the given configuration
func Run(cfg *config.Config) error {
	log.Printf("Starting crawler for %s", cfg.Domain)

	// Parse domain
	parsed, err := url.Parse(cfg.Domain)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("invalid domain: %w", err)
	}

	startURL := strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")
	siteName := strings.Split(startURL, ".")[0]

	// Initialize statistics
	stats := NewCrawlStats()

	// Create collector
	c := colly.NewCollector(
		colly.MaxDepth(cfg.Crawler.MaxDepth),
		colly.Async(cfg.Crawler.Async),
		colly.IgnoreRobotsTxt(),
		colly.UserAgent(cfg.Crawler.UserAgent),
	)

	if err := c.Limit(&colly.LimitRule{
		DomainGlob:  "*",
		Parallelism: cfg.Crawler.Parallelism,
		Delay:       time.Duration(cfg.Crawler.DelayMS) * time.Millisecond,
		RandomDelay: time.Duration(cfg.Crawler.RandomDelayMS) * time.Millisecond,
	}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error setting rate limit: %w", err)
	}

	// Choose writer based on database_name extension
	var writer Writer
	if isSQLiteDatabase(cfg.Crawler.DatabaseName) {
		sqliteWriter, err := NewAsyncSQLiteWriter(siteName, cfg, stats)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("failed to create async SQLite writer: %w", err)
		}
		writer = sqliteWriter
		log.Printf("Using Async SQLite database for storage: %s", cfg.Crawler.DatabaseName)
	} else {
		csvWriter, err := NewBatchWriter(siteName, cfg, stats)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("failed to create CSV writer: %w", err)
		}
		writer = csvWriter
		log.Printf("Using CSV files for storage: %s", cfg.Crawler.DatabaseName)
	}
	defer writer.Close()

	visited := &sync.Map{}

	// Error handling
	c.OnError(func(r *colly.Response, err error) {
		errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Request error for %s: %v", r.Request.URL, err)
		log.Printf("%s", errMsg)
		stats.AddError(errMsg)
		stats.IncrementErrors()
	})

	// Performance monitoring
	go func() {
		ticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)
		defer ticker.Stop()
		for range ticker.C {
			stats.PrintStats()
		}
	}()

	// OnHTML callback
	c.OnHTML("a[href]", func(e *colly.HTMLElement) {
		link := e.Request.AbsoluteURL(e.Attr("href"))
		if link == "" || !isValidURL(link) {
			return
		}

		if isAssetURL(link) {
			return
		}

		cleanLink := cleanURL(link)
		if cleanLink == "" {
			return
		}

		if hasBlockedExtension(cleanLink) {
			return
		}

		if _, exists := visited.LoadOrStore(cleanLink, true); exists {
			return
		}

		// Only save URLs that match product path patterns
		if isProductURL(cleanLink, cfg) {
			writer.Add(URLData{
				URL:       cleanLink,
				TimeStamp: time.Now(),
				SiteName:  siteName,
			})
		}

		// Continue crawling all pages to discover more product URLs
		if strings.Contains(cleanLink, startURL) {
			if err := e.Request.Visit(cleanLink); err != nil {
				errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Failed to visit %s: %v", cleanLink, err)
				stats.AddError(errMsg)
			}
		}
	})

	log.Printf("Starting crawl for %s (max depth: %d, parallelism: %d)",
		cfg.Domain, cfg.Crawler.MaxDepth, cfg.Crawler.Parallelism)

	if err := c.Visit(cfg.Domain); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error starting crawl: %w", err)
	}

	done := make(chan bool)
	go func() {
		c.Wait()
		done <- true
	}()

	select {
	case <-done:
		log.Println("Crawl completed normally")
	case <-time.After(time.Duration(cfg.Crawler.TimeoutMinutes) * time.Minute):
		log.Println("Crawl timed out")
	}

	writer.Flush()
	stats.PrintStats()

	log.Println("✓ Crawl finished successfully")
	log.Printf("✓ Output saved to: %s", cfg.Output.CrawlerPath)

	return nil
}

File: scraper.go

package scraper

import (
	"database/sql"
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"crawler/pkg/config"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
	_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"
)

// ProductItem represents a scraped product
type ProductItem struct {
	URL          string
	Title        string
	Description  string
	Price        float64
	SalePrice    float64
	Currency     string
	MainImage    string
	ImageGallery []string
	Sizes        []string
	Availability bool
	Brand        string
	SiteName     string
	Country      string
	Collection   string
	Timestamp    string
	SKU          string
	Category     string
}

// GenericSpider scrapes product data from URLs
type GenericSpider struct {
	client    *http.Client
	cfg       *config.Config
	rateLimit <-chan time.Time
	wg        sync.WaitGroup
	mutex     sync.Mutex
}

// NewGenericSpider creates a new spider instance
func NewGenericSpider(cfg *config.Config) *GenericSpider {
	return &GenericSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: time.Duration(cfg.Scraper.TimeoutSeconds) * time.Second,
		},
		cfg:       cfg,
		rateLimit: time.Tick(time.Duration(cfg.Scraper.RateLimitMs) * time.Millisecond),
	}
}

// ScrapeURLs scrapes product data from a list of URLs
func (s *GenericSpider) ScrapeURLs(urls []string) error {
	if err := os.MkdirAll(s.cfg.Output.ScraperPath, 0755); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create output directory: %w", err)
	}

	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.cfg.Output.ScraperPath, fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s.csv", s.cfg.Name, timestamp))

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create output file: %w", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Write headers
	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "image_gallery", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	if err := writer.Write(headers); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write headers: %w", err)
	}

	batchSize := s.cfg.Scraper.BatchSize
	totalBatches := (len(urls) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	log.Printf("Starting to scrape %d URLs in %d batches", len(urls), totalBatches)

	for i := 0; i < len(urls); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(urls) {
			end = len(urls)
		}

		batch := urls[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		log.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
		log.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	s.wg.Wait()
	log.Printf("✓ Scraping completed")
	log.Printf("✓ Output saved to: %s", outputFile)

	return nil
}

func (s *GenericSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			log.Printf("Scraping: %s", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.ImageGallery, " | "),
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		if err := writer.Write(record); err != nil {
			log.Printf("Warning: Failed to write record: %v", err)
		}
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *GenericSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     s.cfg.Scraper.Brand,
		SiteName:  s.cfg.Scraper.Brand, // Use brand as site name
		Country:   s.cfg.Scraper.Country,
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
		Currency:  s.cfg.Scraper.Currency,
	}

	// Extract data using selectors
	product.Title = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Title, "content", "text")
	product.Description = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Description, "content", "text")
	product.MainImage = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.MainImage, "content", "src", "data-src")
	product.SKU = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.SKU, "content", "text", "data-sku")
	product.Category = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Category, "text", "content")

	// Extract currency
	if currency := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Currency, "content", "text"); currency != "" {
		product.Currency = currency
	}

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Price, "content", "text", "data-price"); priceStr != "" {
		product.Price = s.cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr)
	}

	// Extract sale price
	if salePriceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.SalePrice, "content", "text", "data-sale-price"); salePriceStr != "" {
		product.SalePrice = s.cleanAndParsePrice(salePriceStr)
	}

	// Extract sizes
	product.Sizes = s.extractSizes(doc)

	// Check availability
	product.Availability = s.checkAvailability(doc)

	// Extract collection from URL
	if s.cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL != "" {
		if parts := strings.Split(url, s.cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL); len(parts) > 1 {
			product.Collection = strings.Split(parts[1], "/")[0]
		}
	}

	// JSON-LD fallback extraction
	if s.cfg.Scraper.FallbackExtraction.EnableJSONLD {
		s.extractFromJSONLD(doc, product)
	}

	return product
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractWithSelectors(doc *goquery.Document, selectors []string, attrs ...string) string {
	for _, selector := range selectors {
		if selector == "" {
			continue
		}

		selection := doc.Find(selector)
		if selection.Length() > 0 {
			for _, attr := range attrs {
				var value string
				if attr == "text" {
					value = strings.TrimSpace(selection.First().Text())
				} else {
					value = selection.First().AttrOr(attr, "")
				}
				if value != "" {
					return value
				}
			}
		}
	}
	return ""
}

func (s *GenericSpider) cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr string) float64 {
	if priceStr == "" {
		return 0.0
	}

	// Remove configured characters
	for _, char := range s.cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.RemoveChars {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, char, "")
	}

	// Regex to find the first number that looks like a price
	// Handles 123, 123.45, 1,234.56
	re := regexp.MustCompile(`[0-9]{1,3}(?:[0-9,.]*[0-9])?`)
	match := re.FindString(priceStr)
	if match != "" {
		// Remove commas for parsing
		clean := strings.ReplaceAll(match, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(clean, 64); err == nil {
			return price
		}
	}

	return 0.0
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractSizes(doc *goquery.Document) []string {
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)

	for _, selector := range s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Sizes {
		doc.Find(selector).Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) {
			size := strings.TrimSpace(sel.Text())
			if size != "" {
				isValidSize := true
				for _, filter := range s.cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.SizeFilters {
					if strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), strings.ToLower(filter)) {
						isValidSize = false
						break
					}
				}
				if isValidSize {
					sizeMap[size] = true
				}
			}
		})
	}

	var sizes []string
	for size := range sizeMap {
		sizes = append(sizes, size)
	}
	return sizes
}

func (s *GenericSpider) checkAvailability(doc *goquery.Document) bool {
	for _, selector := range s.cfg.Scraper.Selectors.Availability {
		element := doc.Find(selector)
		if element.Length() > 0 {
			text := strings.ToLower(element.Text())
			for _, keyword := range s.cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.AvailabilityKeywords {
				if strings.Contains(text, strings.ToLower(keyword)) {
					return false
				}
			}
			return true
		}
	}
	return true
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractFromJSONLD(doc *goquery.Document, product *ProductItem) {
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := sel.Text()
		
		var data interface{}
		if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &data); err != nil {
			return
		}

		s.processJSONLDNode(data, product)
	})
}

func (s *GenericSpider) processJSONLDNode(data interface{}, product *ProductItem) {
	switch v := data.(type) {
	case map[string]interface{}:
		if typeVal, ok := v["@type"].(string); ok && (typeVal == "Product" || typeVal == "http://schema.org/Product") {
			s.extractProductFromMap(v, product)
		}
		for _, val := range v {
			s.processJSONLDNode(val, product)
		}
	case []interface{}:
		for _, item := range v {
			s.processJSONLDNode(item, product)
		}
	}
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractProductFromMap(v map[string]interface{}, product *ProductItem) {
	if name, ok := v["name"].(string); ok && product.Title == "" {
		product.Title = name
	}
	if desc, ok := v["description"].(string); ok && product.Description == "" {
		product.Description = desc
	}
	if sku, ok := v["sku"].(string); ok && product.SKU == "" {
		product.SKU = sku
	}
	if brandData, ok := v["brand"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
		if brandName, ok := brandData["name"].(string); ok {
			product.Brand = brandName
		}
	} else if brandName, ok := v["brand"].(string); ok {
		product.Brand = brandName
	}

	if offers, ok := v["offers"].([]interface{}); ok && len(offers) > 0 {
		if offer, ok := offers[0].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
			s.extractOfferFromMap(offer, product)
		}
	} else if offer, ok := v["offers"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
		s.extractOfferFromMap(offer, product)
	}
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractOfferFromMap(offer map[string]interface{}, product *ProductItem) {
	if price, ok := offer["price"].(float64); ok && product.Price == 0 {
		product.Price = price
	} else if priceStr, ok := offer["price"].(string); ok && product.Price == 0 {
		product.Price = s.cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr)
	}
	if currency, ok := offer["priceCurrency"].(string); ok {
		product.Currency = currency
	}
	if availability, ok := offer["availability"].(string); ok {
		if strings.Contains(availability, "OutOfStock") || strings.Contains(availability, "SoldOut") {
			product.Availability = false
		} else if strings.Contains(availability, "InStock") {
			product.Availability = true
		}
	}
}

// LoadURLsFromCrawlerOutput loads URLs from the latest crawler output
func LoadURLsFromCrawlerOutput(cfg *config.Config) ([]string, error) {
	// Find the latest site directory
	var latestDir string
	var latestTime time.Time

	siteName := strings.Split(strings.TrimPrefix(cfg.Domain, "https://"), "/")[0]
	siteName = strings.TrimPrefix(siteName, "www.")
	siteName = strings.Split(siteName, ".")[0]

	siteDir := filepath.Join(cfg.Output.CrawlerPath, siteName)
	if entries, err := os.ReadDir(siteDir); err == nil {
		for _, entry := range entries {
			if entry.IsDir() {
				info, _ := entry.Info()
				if info.ModTime().After(latestTime) {
					latestTime = info.ModTime()
					latestDir = filepath.Join(siteDir, entry.Name())
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if latestDir == "" {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("no crawler output found in %s", siteDir)
	}

	log.Printf("Loading URLs from: %s", latestDir)

	// Load all batch CSV files
	var allURLs []string
	entries, err := os.ReadDir(latestDir)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read output directory: %w", err)
	}

	for _, entry := range entries {
		if strings.HasSuffix(entry.Name(), ".csv") {
			csvPath := filepath.Join(latestDir, entry.Name())
			urls, err := loadURLsFromCSV(csvPath)
			if err != nil {
				log.Printf("Warning: Failed to load %s: %v", csvPath, err)
				continue
			}
			allURLs = append(allURLs, urls...)
		}
	}

	log.Printf("Loaded %d URLs from crawler output", len(allURLs))

	// Filter product URLs
	var productURLs []string
	for _, url := range allURLs {
		if isProductURL(url, cfg) {
			productURLs = append(productURLs, url)
		}
	}

	log.Printf("Filtered to %d product URLs", len(productURLs))

	return productURLs, nil
}

func loadURLsFromCSV(path string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(path)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)
	records, err := reader.ReadAll()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	var urls []string
	for i, record := range records {
		if i == 0 {
			continue // Skip header
		}
		if len(record) > 0 {
			urls = append(urls, record[0])
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

func isProductURL(url string, cfg *config.Config) bool {
	for _, path := range cfg.Scraper.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths {
		if strings.Contains(url, path) {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

// LoadURLsFromSQLite loads URLs from SQLite database
func LoadURLsFromSQLite(dbPath, table, field string) ([]string, error) {
	db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dbPath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer db.Close()

	rows, err := db.Query("SELECT " + field + " FROM " + table)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer rows.Close()

	var urls []string
	for rows.Next() {
		var url string
		if err := rows.Scan(&url); err == nil && strings.TrimSpace(url) != "" {
			urls = append(urls, url)
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

// Run starts the scraper with the given configuration
func Run(cfg *config.Config) error {
	log.Printf("Starting scraper for %s", cfg.Domain)

	// Load URLs from crawler output
	urls, err := LoadURLsFromCrawlerOutput(cfg)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to load URLs: %w", err)
	}

	if len(urls) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found to scrape")
	}

	// Create spider and scrape
	spider := NewGenericSpider(cfg)
	return spider.ScrapeURLs(urls)
}

package main

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"net/url"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"

    "database/sql"
    _ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"

func printHelp() {
	fmt.Println("Usage:")
	fmt.Println("  scraper <site> <config file> [urlfile]")
	fmt.Println("  scraper --genconfig <site>")
	fmt.Println("")
	fmt.Println("Example:")
	fmt.Println("  scraper nyandcompany.com nyandcompanyconfig.json urls.txt")
	fmt.Println("  scraper --genconfig nyandcompany.com")
	fmt.Println("")
	fmt.Println("If [urlfile] is not given, scraper will look for:")
	fmt.Println("  <site>_urls.txt")
	fmt.Println("  <site>_urls.csv")
	fmt.Println("  urls.txt")
	fmt.Println("  urls.csv")
	fmt.Println("")
	fmt.Println("Options:")
	fmt.Println("  -h, --help      Show this help message")
	fmt.Println("  --genconfig     Generate a default config file for a site")
}

var STARTURL string
var AllowedDomains []string

func genScraperConfig(siteURL string) error {
	// Parse the URL to get domain
	parsed, err := url.Parse(siteURL)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("invalid URL: %v", err)
	}

	domain := strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")

	// Create config with default values
	config := Config{
		SpiderConfig: SpiderConfig{
			Name:           strings.ReplaceAll(domain, ".", "_") + "_scraper",
			BaseURL:        "",
			OutputDir:      "./output",
			RateLimitMs:    500,
			BatchSize:      10,
			TimeoutSeconds: 30,
			ChannelBuffer:  100,
		},
		ScrapingConfig: ScrapingConfig{
			Brand:            "Generic Brand",
			SiteName:         domain,
			Country:          "Global",
			CurrencyFallback: "INR",
		},
		Selectors: Selectors{
			Title:        []string{"meta[property='og:title']", "meta[name='title']", "title", "h1"},
			Description:  []string{"meta[property='og:description']", "meta[name='description']", ".product-description", ".description"},
			MainImage:    []string{"meta[property='og:image:secure_url']", "meta[property='og:image']", ".product-image img", ".main-image img", "img[data-main-image]"},
			Price:        []string{"meta[property='product:price:amount']", ".price", ".current-price", "[data-price]"},
			Currency:     []string{"meta[property='product:price:currency']", "[data-currency]"},
			SalePrice:    []string{".sale-price", ".discounted-price", "[data-sale-price]"},
			Sizes:        []string{"select[name*='size'] option", "select[name*='Size'] option", ".size-selector option", ".sizes .size"},
			Availability: []string{"button[id*='AddToCart']", ".add-to-cart", ".buy-now"},
			SKU:          []string{"[data-sku]", ".sku"},
			Category:     []string{".breadcrumbs a:last-child", ".category"},
		},
		ExtractionRules: ExtractionRules{
			CollectionPaths:      []string{"/collections/", "/category/"},
			ProductPaths:         []string{"/products/", "/item/"},
			CollectionFromURL:    "/collections/",
			ProductURLFilter:     "/products/",
			AvailabilityKeywords: []string{"sold out", "out of stock", "unavailable"},
			SizeFilters:          []string{"select size", "choose size", "pick size"},
			PriceCleanup: struct {
				RemoveChars  []string `json:"remove_chars"`
				ParseAsFloat bool     `json:"parse_as_float"`
			}{
				RemoveChars:  []string{",", "$", "₹", "€", "£"},
				ParseAsFloat: true,
			},
		},
		FallbackExtraction: FallbackExtraction{
			EnableJSONLD:         true,
			EnableMicrodata:      true,
			EnableTextExtraction: true,
		},
	}

	// Generate filename
	filename := strings.ReplaceAll(domain, ".", "_") + "_config.json"

	// Convert to JSON with proper indentation
	jsonData, err := json.MarshalIndent(config, "", "  ")
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error marshaling config: %v", err)
	}

	// Write to file
	err = os.WriteFile(filename, jsonData, 0644)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error writing config file: %v", err)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Generated config file: %s\n", filename)
	return nil
}

func main() {
	if len(os.Args) < 2 {
		printHelp()
		os.Exit(1)
	}

	// Help flag
	if strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "-h") || strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "--help") {
		printHelp()
		return
	}
	// Generate config flag
	if strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "--genconfig") {
		if len(os.Args) < 3 {
			log.Fatal("Error: --genconfig requires a site URL")
		}
		rawInput := os.Args[2]
		if !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "http://") && !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "https://") {
			rawInput = "https://" + rawInput
		}
		err := genScraperConfig(rawInput)
		if err != nil {
			log.Fatal(err)
		}
		return
	}

	if len(os.Args) < 3 {
		log.Fatal("Error: Missing arguments. Run with --help for usage.")
	}

	// Normalize input URL
	rawInput := os.Args[1]
	if !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "http://") && !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "https://") {
		rawInput = "https://" + rawInput
	}

	parsed, err := url.Parse(rawInput)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Invalid URL: %v", err)
	}

	// Extract clean domain
	host := strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")

	// Store for scraper
	STARTURL = rawInput
	AllowedDomains = []string{host, "www." + host}

	log.Printf("Scraping site: %s (allowed domains: %v)\n", STARTURL, AllowedDomains)

	// Remaining arguments
	configFile := os.Args[2]
	var urlFile string
	if len(os.Args) >= 4 {
		urlFile = os.Args[3]
	}

	err = RunScraper(STARTURL, configFile, urlFile) // pass normalized URL
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
}
func RunScraper(siteName, configFile, urlFile string) error {
	fmt.Println("Starting scraper for", siteName, "with config", configFile)

	// Load config
	config, err := LoadConfig(configFile)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error loading config: %v", err)
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Loaded config for: %s\n", config.SpiderConfig.Name)

	// Load URLs
	var urls []string
	if urlFile != "" {
		urls, err = LoadURLsFromFile(urlFile)
		if err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("error loading URLs from %s: %v", urlFile, err)
		}
	} else {
		defaultFiles := []string{
			fmt.Sprintf("%s_urls.txt", siteName),
			fmt.Sprintf("%s_urls.csv", siteName),
			"urls.txt",
			"urls.csv",
		}
		for _, f := range defaultFiles {
			if fileUrls, err := LoadURLsFromFile(f); err == nil && len(fileUrls) > 0 {
				urls = fileUrls
				fmt.Printf("Loaded %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), f)
				break
			}
		}
	}

	if len(urls) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no URLs found. Provide a file or create one like %s_urls.txt", siteName)
	}

	// Filter product URLs
	var productURLs []string
	for _, url := range urls {
		if len(config.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths) > 0 {
			for _, path := range config.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths {
				if strings.Contains(url, path) {
					productURLs = append(productURLs, url)
					break
				}
			}
		} else if config.ExtractionRules.ProductURLFilter != "" {
			if strings.Contains(url, config.ExtractionRules.ProductURLFilter) {
				productURLs = append(productURLs, url)
			}
		}
	}

	if len(productURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no valid product URLs found")
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs\n", len(productURLs))
	fmt.Printf("Starting scraping with rate limit: %dms, batch size: %d\n",
		config.SpiderConfig.RateLimitMs, config.SpiderConfig.BatchSize)

	spider := NewGenericSpider(config)
	return spider.ScrapeURLs(productURLs)
}

func LoadURLsFromFile(path string) ([]string, error) {
	f, err := os.Open(path)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer f.Close()

	var urls []string
	if strings.HasSuffix(strings.ToLower(path), ".csv") {
		r := csv.NewReader(f)
		records, err := r.ReadAll()
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
		for _, rec := range records {
			if len(rec) > 0 && strings.TrimSpace(rec[0]) != "" {
				urls = append(urls, strings.TrimSpace(rec[0]))
			}
		}
	} else {
		buf, err := os.ReadFile(path)
		if err != nil {
			return nil, err
		}
		lines := strings.Split(string(buf), "\n")
		for _, line := range lines {
			if trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(line); trimmed != "" {
				urls = append(urls, trimmed)
			}
		}
	}
	return urls, nil
}

// Helper function
func contains(s, substr string) bool {
	if substr == "" {
		return true
	}
	for i := 0; i <= len(s)-len(substr); i++ {
		if s[i:i+len(substr)] == substr {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

// Updated structs to support arrays of selectors
type Selectors struct {
	Title        []string `json:"title"`
	Description  []string `json:"description"`
	MainImage    []string `json:"main_image"`
	Price        []string `json:"price"`
	Currency     []string `json:"currency"`
	SalePrice    []string `json:"sale_price"`
	Sizes        []string `json:"sizes"`
	Availability []string `json:"availability"`
	SKU          []string `json:"sku"`
	Category     []string `json:"category"`
}

type ExtractionRules struct {
	CollectionPaths      []string `json:"collection_paths"`
	ProductPaths         []string `json:"product_paths"`
	CollectionFromURL    string   `json:"collection_from_url"`
	ProductURLFilter     string   `json:"product_url_filter"`
	AvailabilityKeywords []string `json:"availability_keywords"`
	SizeFilters          []string `json:"size_filters"`
	PriceCleanup         struct {
		RemoveChars  []string `json:"remove_chars"`
		ParseAsFloat bool     `json:"parse_as_float"`
	} `json:"price_cleanup"`
}

type FallbackExtraction struct {
	EnableJSONLD         bool `json:"enable_json_ld"`
	EnableMicrodata      bool `json:"enable_microdata"`
	EnableTextExtraction bool `json:"enable_text_extraction"`
}

type Config struct {
	SpiderConfig       SpiderConfig       `json:"spider_config"`
	ScrapingConfig     ScrapingConfig     `json:"scraping_config"`
	Selectors          Selectors          `json:"selectors"`
	ExtractionRules    ExtractionRules    `json:"extraction_rules"`
	OutputFormat       OutputFormat       `json:"output_format"`
	FallbackExtraction FallbackExtraction `json:"fallback_extraction"`
}

// Rest of the structs remain the same...
type SpiderConfig struct {
	Name           string `json:"name"`
	BaseURL        string `json:"base_url"`
	OutputDir      string `json:"output_dir"`
	RateLimitMs    int    `json:"rate_limit_ms"`
	BatchSize      int    `json:"batch_size"`
	TimeoutSeconds int    `json:"timeout_seconds"`
	ChannelBuffer  int    `json:"channel_buffer"`
}

type ScrapingConfig struct {
	Brand            string `json:"brand"`
	SiteName         string `json:"site_name"`
	Country          string `json:"country"`
	CurrencyFallback string `json:"currency_fallback"`
}

type OutputFormat struct {
	Headers []string `json:"headers"`
}

type ProductItem struct {
	URL          string
	Title        string
	Description  string
	Price        float64
	SalePrice    float64
	Currency     string
	MainImage    string
	Sizes        []string
	Availability bool
	Brand        string
	SiteName     string
	Country      string
	Collection   string
	Timestamp    string
	SKU          string
	Category     string
}

type GenericSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	config      *Config
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
}

func NewGenericSpider(config *Config) *GenericSpider {
	return &GenericSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: time.Duration(config.SpiderConfig.TimeoutSeconds) * time.Second,
		},
		config:      config,
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Duration(config.SpiderConfig.RateLimitMs) * time.Millisecond),
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, config.SpiderConfig.ChannelBuffer),
	}
}

func (s *GenericSpider) ScrapeURLs(urls []string) error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.config.SpiderConfig.OutputDir, 0755)

	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.config.SpiderConfig.OutputDir, fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s.csv", s.config.SpiderConfig.Name, timestamp))

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Default headers if not specified
	headers := s.config.OutputFormat.Headers
	if len(headers) == 0 {
		headers = []string{
			"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
			"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
			"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
		}
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := s.config.SpiderConfig.BatchSize
	totalBatches := (len(urls) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(urls); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(urls) {
			end = len(urls)
		}

		batch := urls[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
		fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	fmt.Printf("Output saved to: %s\n", outputFile)
	return nil
}

func (s *GenericSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

// Universal extraction method
func (s *GenericSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     s.config.ScrapingConfig.Brand,
		SiteName:  s.config.ScrapingConfig.SiteName,
		Country:   s.config.ScrapingConfig.Country,
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
		Currency:  s.config.ScrapingConfig.CurrencyFallback,
	}

	// Universal extraction using multiple selectors
	product.Title = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Title, "content", "text")
	product.Description = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Description, "content", "text")

	// Enhanced image extraction with more fallback options
	product.MainImage = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.MainImage, "content", "src", "data-src", "href", "data-image", "data-zoom-image")

	product.SKU = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.SKU, "content", "text", "data-sku")
	product.Category = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Category, "text", "content")

	// Extract currency
	if currency := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Currency, "content", "text"); currency != "" {
		product.Currency = currency
	}

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Price, "content", "text", "data-price"); priceStr != "" {
		product.Price = s.cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr)
	}

	// Extract sale price
	if salePriceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.SalePrice, "content", "text", "data-sale-price"); salePriceStr != "" {
		product.SalePrice = s.cleanAndParsePrice(salePriceStr)
	}

	// Extract sizes
	product.Sizes = s.extractSizes(doc)

	// Check availability
	product.Availability = s.checkAvailability(doc)

	// Extract collection from URL
	if s.config.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL != "" {
		if parts := strings.Split(url, s.config.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL); len(parts) > 1 {
			product.Collection = strings.Split(parts[1], "/")[0]
		}
	}

	// JSON-LD fallback extraction (includes images, prices, SKU)
	if s.config.FallbackExtraction.EnableJSONLD {
		s.extractFromJSONLD(doc, product)
	}

	// Debug logging for images
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		fmt.Printf("WARNING: No image found for %s\n", url)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f, Image: %s)\n", url, product.Price, product.MainImage)
	return product
}

// Helper method to try multiple selectors
func (s *GenericSpider) extractWithSelectors(doc *goquery.Document, selectors []string, attrs ...string) string {
	for _, selector := range selectors {
		if selector == "" {
			continue
		}

		selection := doc.Find(selector)
		if selection.Length() > 0 {
			// Try each attribute
			for _, attr := range attrs {
				var value string
				if attr == "text" {
					value = strings.TrimSpace(selection.First().Text())
				} else {
					value = selection.First().AttrOr(attr, "")
				}
				if value != "" {
					return value
				}
			}
		}
	}
	return ""
}

func (s *GenericSpider) cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr string) float64 {
	// Clean price string
	for _, char := range s.config.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.RemoveChars {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, char, "")
	}

	priceStr = strings.TrimSpace(priceStr)

	if s.config.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.ParseAsFloat {
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			return price
		}
	}
	return 0.0
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractSizes(doc *goquery.Document) []string {
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)

	for _, selector := range s.config.Selectors.Sizes {
		doc.Find(selector).Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) {
			size := strings.TrimSpace(sel.Text())
			if size != "" {
				// Filter out common non-size text
				isValidSize := true
				for _, filter := range s.config.ExtractionRules.SizeFilters {
					if strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), strings.ToLower(filter)) {
						isValidSize = false
						break
					}
				}
				if isValidSize {
					sizeMap[size] = true
				}
			}
		})
	}

	var sizes []string
	for size := range sizeMap {
		sizes = append(sizes, size)
	}
	return sizes
}

func (s *GenericSpider) checkAvailability(doc *goquery.Document) bool {
	for _, selector := range s.config.Selectors.Availability {
		element := doc.Find(selector)
		if element.Length() > 0 {
			text := strings.ToLower(element.Text())
			for _, keyword := range s.config.ExtractionRules.AvailabilityKeywords {
				if strings.Contains(text, strings.ToLower(keyword)) {
					return false
				}
			}
			return true
		}
	}
	return true // Default to available if can't determine
}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractFromJSONLD(doc *goquery.Document, product *ProductItem) {
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := sel.Text()
		if strings.Contains(jsonData, "Product") || strings.Contains(jsonData, "\"@type\":\"Product\"") {
			var schemaData map[string]interface{}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil {
				// Extract image if not found yet
				if product.MainImage == "" {
					if image, ok := schemaData["image"].(string); ok {
						product.MainImage = image
					} else if images, ok := schemaData["image"].([]interface{}); ok && len(images) > 0 {
						if imageStr, ok := images[0].(string); ok {
							product.MainImage = imageStr
						} else if imageObj, ok := images[0].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
							if url, ok := imageObj["url"].(string); ok {
								product.MainImage = url
							}
						}
					}
				}

				// Extract offers (price, SKU)
				if offers, ok := schemaData["offers"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
					if price, ok := offers["price"].(string); ok && product.Price == 0 {
						if priceFloat, err := strconv.ParseFloat(price, 64); err == nil {
							product.Price = priceFloat
						}
					} else if priceFloat, ok := offers["price"].(float64); ok && product.Price == 0 {
						product.Price = priceFloat
					}

					if sku, ok := offers["sku"].(string); ok && product.SKU == "" {
						product.SKU = sku
					}
				} else if offers, ok := schemaData["offers"].([]interface{}); ok && len(offers) > 0 {
					if offer, ok := offers[0].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
						if price, ok := offer["price"].(string); ok && product.Price == 0 {
							if priceFloat, err := strconv.ParseFloat(price, 64); err == nil {
								product.Price = priceFloat
							}
						} else if priceFloat, ok := offer["price"].(float64); ok && product.Price == 0 {
							product.Price = priceFloat
						}

						if sku, ok := offer["sku"].(string); ok && product.SKU == "" {
							product.SKU = sku
						}
					}
				}

				// Extract SKU from top level if not found
				if product.SKU == "" {
					if sku, ok := schemaData["sku"].(string); ok {
						product.SKU = sku
					}
				}
			}
		}
	})
}

func LoadConfig(configPath string) (*Config, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(configPath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	var config Config
	decoder := json.NewDecoder(file)
	err = decoder.Decode(&config)
	return &config, err
}


// LoadURLsFromSQLite loads URLs from sqlite database, table & field name provided as arguments
func LoadURLsFromSQLite(dbPath, table, field string) ([]string, error) {
    db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dbPath)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer db.Close()
    rows, err := db.Query("SELECT " + field + " FROM " + table)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer rows.Close()
    var urls []string
    for rows.Next() {
        var url string
        if err := rows.Scan(&url); err == nil && strings.TrimSpace(url) != "" {
            urls = append(urls, url)
        }
    }
    return urls, nil
}

File: main.go

package main

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/url"
	"os"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/gocolly/colly"
)

type SiteItem struct {
	SiteName  string
	SiteURL   string
	Timestamp time.Time
}

type URLData struct {
	URL       string
	Type      string
	ParentURL string
}

func main() {
	allowedDomains := []string{"www.westside.com"}
	startURLs := []string{"https://www.westside.com"}

	var siteItem SiteItem
	siteItem.SiteName = allowedDomains[0]
	siteItem.SiteURL = startURLs[0]
	siteItem.Timestamp = time.Now()

	// Create collectors pool for concurrent scraping
	collectors := make([]*colly.Collector, 8) // Increase number of collectors
	for i := range collectors {
		collectors[i] = colly.NewCollector(
			colly.AllowedDomains(allowedDomains...),
			colly.MaxDepth(10),
			colly.Async(true),
		)

		// Increase limits significantly
		collectors[i].Limit(&colly.LimitRule{
			DomainGlob:  "*",
			Parallelism: 16,
			RandomDelay: 500 * time.Millisecond,
		})
	}

	// Create buffered channels
	urlChan := make(chan URLData, 10000)
	saveChan := make(chan []string, 10000)

	// Create a map to store visited URLs with a custom mutex for better performance
	var visitedURLs sync.Map

	// Start CSV writer goroutine
	go saveToCSV(saveChan)

	// Start URL processor goroutines
	var wg sync.WaitGroup
	for i := 0; i < 4; i++ { // Multiple URL processors
		wg.Add(1)
		go processURLs(urlChan, saveChan, &wg)
	}

	// Configure collectors
	for _, c := range collectors {
		// Handle all links on the page
		c.OnHTML("a[href]", func(e *colly.HTMLElement) {
			link := e.Attr("href")
			if link == "" {
				return
			}

			absoluteURL := e.Request.AbsoluteURL(link)
			if absoluteURL == "" {
				return
			}

			cleanURL := cleanupURL(absoluteURL)
			if cleanURL == "" {
				return
			}

			// Use LoadOrStore for atomic check-and-set
			if _, exists := visitedURLs.LoadOrStore(cleanURL, true); !exists {
				urlChan <- URLData{
					URL:       cleanURL,
					Type:      categorizeURL(cleanURL),
					ParentURL: e.Request.URL.String(),
				}

				// Visit the URL if it belongs to allowed domains
				if isAllowedDomain(cleanURL, allowedDomains) {
					// Use random collector from pool
					collectors[fastrand(len(collectors))].Visit(cleanURL)
				}
			}
		})

		c.OnError(func(r *colly.Response, err error) {
			log.Printf("Error visiting %s: %v", r.Request.URL, err)
		})
	}

	// Start crawling with multiple collectors
	for _, url := range startURLs {
		for _, c := range collectors {
			c.Visit(url)
		}
	}

	// Wait for all collectors
	for _, c := range collectors {
		c.Wait()
	}

	// Close channels and wait for goroutines
	close(urlChan)
	wg.Wait()
	close(saveChan)

	// Save site information
	saveSiteInfo(siteItem)
}

func processURLs(urlChan chan URLData, saveChan chan []string, wg *sync.WaitGroup) {
	defer wg.Done()
	for urlData := range urlChan {
		saveChan <- []string{urlData.URL, urlData.Type, urlData.ParentURL}
	}
}

func saveToCSV(saveChan chan []string) {
	file, err := os.Create(fmt.Sprintf("site_urls_%s.csv", time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	writer.Write([]string{"url", "type", "parent_url"})

	// Buffer for batch writing
	buffer := make([][]string, 0, 1000)
	for data := range saveChan {
		buffer = append(buffer, data)

		if len(buffer) >= 1000 {
			writer.WriteAll(buffer)
			buffer = buffer[:0]
		}
	}

	// Write remaining data
	if len(buffer) > 0 {
		writer.WriteAll(buffer)
	}
}

// Fast random number generator for collector selection
func fastrand(n int) int {
	return int(time.Now().UnixNano()/1000) % n
}

// Rest of the helper functions remain the same
// cleanupURL, categorizeURL, isAllowedDomain...
func cleanupURL(urlStr string) string {
	// Parse the URL
	parsedURL, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	if err != nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Remove fragments
	parsedURL.Fragment = ""

	// Remove certain query parameters if needed
	query := parsedURL.Query()
	// Add any query parameters you want to remove
	// query.Del("utm_source")
	parsedURL.RawQuery = query.Encode()

	return parsedURL.String()
}

func categorizeURL(urlStr string) string {
	lowercaseURL := strings.ToLower(urlStr)
	switch {
	case strings.Contains(lowercaseURL, "/collections/"):
		return "collection"
	case strings.Contains(lowercaseURL, "/products/"):
		return "product"
	case strings.Contains(lowercaseURL, "/pages/"):
		return "page"
	case strings.Contains(lowercaseURL, "/blogs/"):
		return "blog"
	default:
		return "other"
	}
}

func isAllowedDomain(urlStr string, allowedDomains []string) bool {
	parsedURL, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	if err != nil {
		return false
	}

	for _, domain := range allowedDomains {
		if parsedURL.Hostname() == domain {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}
func saveSiteInfo(siteItem SiteItem) {
	infoFile, err := os.Create(fmt.Sprintf("site_info_%s.csv", time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")))
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	defer infoFile.Close()

	infoWriter := csv.NewWriter(infoFile)
	defer infoWriter.Flush()

	infoWriter.Write([]string{"site_name", "site_url", "timestamp"})
	infoWriter.Write([]string{siteItem.SiteName, siteItem.SiteURL, siteItem.Timestamp.Format(time.RFC3339)})
}

File: main.go

package main

import (
	"bufio"
	"crawlerindexer/internal/spiders"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"os"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"
)

type Spider interface {
	Start() error
}

type SpiderEntry struct {
	Name   string
	Spider Spider
}

func getSpiderList() []SpiderEntry {
	return []SpiderEntry{
		{"Montecarlo", spiders.NewMontecarloSpider()},
		{"Raymond", spiders.NewRaymondSpider()},
		{"Levi", spiders.NewLeviSpider()},
		{"USPolo", spiders.NewUSPoloSpider()},
		{"Duke", spiders.NewDukeSpider()},
		// {"Spykar", spiders.NewSpykarSpider()},
		{"Blackberrys", spiders.NewBlackberrysSpider()},
		{"Jockey", spiders.NewJockeySpider()},
		{"Wrogn", spiders.NewWrognSpider()},
		{"RedTape", spiders.NewRedTapeSpider()},
		{"Westside", spiders.NewWestsideSpider()},
	}
}

func runSpider(name string, spider Spider, wg *sync.WaitGroup, errorChan chan<- error) {
	defer wg.Done()

	fmt.Printf("\nStarting %s spider...\n", name)
	start := time.Now()

	if err := spider.Start(); err != nil {
		errorChan <- fmt.Errorf("%s spider error: %v", name, err)
		return
	}

	duration := time.Since(start)
	fmt.Printf("✓ %s spider completed successfully (took %v)\n", name, duration)
}

func showMenu() {
	fmt.Println("\n=== Spider Crawler Menu ===")
	fmt.Println("1. Run all spiders")
	fmt.Println("2. Select specific spiders")
	fmt.Println("3. Exit")
	fmt.Print("\nEnter your choice (1-3): ")
}

func getSelectedSpiders(allSpiders []SpiderEntry) map[string]Spider {
	fmt.Println("\nAvailable spiders:")
	for i, entry := range allSpiders {
		fmt.Printf("%d. %s\n", i+1, entry.Name)
	}

	fmt.Print("\nEnter spider numbers (comma-separated) or 'all': ")
	reader := bufio.NewReader(os.Stdin)
	input, _ := reader.ReadString('\n')
	input = strings.TrimSpace(strings.ToLower(input))

	selectedSpiders := make(map[string]Spider)

	if input == "all" {
		for _, entry := range allSpiders {
			selectedSpiders[entry.Name] = entry.Spider
		}
		return selectedSpiders
	}

	numbers := strings.Split(input, ",")
	for _, numStr := range numbers {
		numStr = strings.TrimSpace(numStr)
		if num, err := strconv.Atoi(numStr); err == nil && num > 0 && num <= len(allSpiders) {
			entry := allSpiders[num-1]
			selectedSpiders[entry.Name] = entry.Spider
		}
	}

	return selectedSpiders
}

func main() {
	allSpiders := getSpiderList()
	reader := bufio.NewReader(os.Stdin)

	for {
		showMenu()
		choice, _ := reader.ReadString('\n')
		choice = strings.TrimSpace(choice)

		var selectedSpiders map[string]Spider

		switch choice {
		case "1":
			// Run all spiders
			selectedSpiders = make(map[string]Spider)
			for _, entry := range allSpiders {
				selectedSpiders[entry.Name] = entry.Spider
			}
		case "2":
			// Select specific spiders
			selectedSpiders = getSelectedSpiders(allSpiders)
		case "3":
			fmt.Println("Exiting...")
			return
		default:
			fmt.Println("Invalid choice. Please try again.")
			continue
		}

		if len(selectedSpiders) == 0 {
			fmt.Println("No spiders selected. Please try again.")
			continue
		}

		// Setup logging
		logFile, err := os.OpenFile("crawler.log", os.O_CREATE|os.O_WRONLY|os.O_APPEND, 0666)
		if err != nil {
			log.Fatalf("Error opening log file: %v", err)
		}
		defer logFile.Close()
		log.SetOutput(logFile)

		// Create error channel and wait group
		errorChan := make(chan error, len(selectedSpiders))
		var wg sync.WaitGroup

		fmt.Printf("\nStarting crawler with %d spiders\n", len(selectedSpiders))
		startTime := time.Now()

		// Run selected spiders
		for name, spider := range selectedSpiders {
			wg.Add(1)
			go runSpider(name, spider, &wg, errorChan)
			time.Sleep(2 * time.Second)
		}

		// Wait for completion
		go func() {
			wg.Wait()
			close(errorChan)
		}()

		// Collect errors
		var errors []error
		for err := range errorChan {
			errors = append(errors, err)
			log.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
		}

		// Print summary
		duration := time.Since(startTime)
		fmt.Printf("\nCrawl completed in %v\n", duration)
		fmt.Printf("Total spiders: %d\n", len(selectedSpiders))
		fmt.Printf("Successful: %d\n", len(selectedSpiders)-len(errors))
		fmt.Printf("Failed: %d\n", len(errors))

		if len(errors) > 0 {
			fmt.Println("\nErrors encountered:")
			for _, err := range errors {
				fmt.Printf("- %v\n", err)
			}
		}

		fmt.Print("\nPress Enter to continue...")
		reader.ReadString('\n')
	}
}
