File: crawler.go

package main

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"net/url"
	"os"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/gocolly/colly/v2"
)

var STARTURL string

// const STARTURL = "levi.in"
// const STARTURL = "westside.com"

type URLData struct {
	SiteName  string
	URL       string
	ParentURL string
	TimeStamp time.Time
}

// BatchWriter handles writing data in batches
type BatchWriter struct {
	results     []URLData
	batchSize   int
	mu          sync.Mutex
	fileCounter int
	baseDir     string
	siteName    string // Add this new field

}

func NewBatchWriter(batchSize int, siteName string) *BatchWriter {
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	baseDir := fmt.Sprintf("data/urls/%s/%s_%s", siteName, siteName, timestamp)
	err := os.MkdirAll(baseDir, 0755)
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("Error creating directory: %v\n", err)
	}
	return &BatchWriter{
		results:     make([]URLData, 0, batchSize),
		batchSize:   batchSize,
		baseDir:     baseDir,
		fileCounter: 0,
		siteName:    siteName,
	}
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Add(data URLData) {
	bw.mu.Lock()
	defer bw.mu.Unlock()

	bw.results = append(bw.results, data)
	if len(bw.results) >= bw.batchSize {
		bw.writeBatch()
	}
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) writeBatch() {
	if len(bw.results) == 0 {
		return
	}

	filename := fmt.Sprintf("%s/batch%d.csv", bw.baseDir, bw.fileCounter)
	log.Printf("Writing batch %d with %d URLs\n", bw.fileCounter, len(bw.results))

	if err := writeToCSV(filename, bw.results); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Error writing batch: %v\n", err)
		return
	}

	bw.fileCounter++
	bw.results = make([]URLData, 0, bw.batchSize)
}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Flush() {
	bw.mu.Lock()
	defer bw.mu.Unlock()
	bw.writeBatch()
}

func main() {
	if len(os.Args) != 2 {
		fmt.Printf("Usage: %s <domain>\n", os.Args[0])
		fmt.Println("Example: go run main.go bbc.com")
		os.Exit(1)
	}

	// Set the global STARTURL from command line argument
	STARTURL = strings.TrimPrefix(os.Args[1], "www.")
	STARTURL = strings.TrimPrefix(STARTURL, "https://")
	STARTURL = strings.TrimPrefix(STARTURL, "http://")

	log.SetOutput(os.Stdout)
	log.SetFlags(log.LstdFlags | log.Lshortfile)

	c := colly.NewCollector(
		colly.AllowedDomains("www."+STARTURL, STARTURL),
		colly.MaxDepth(15),
		colly.Async(true),
		colly.IgnoreRobotsTxt(),
		colly.UserAgent("Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36"),
	)

	err := c.Limit(&colly.LimitRule{
		DomainGlob:  "*",
		Parallelism: 2,
		Delay:       500 * time.Millisecond,
		RandomDelay: 500 * time.Millisecond,
	})
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal("Error setting rate limit:", err)
	}

	visited := make(map[string]bool)
	var mu sync.Mutex
	batchWriter := NewBatchWriter(400, STARTURL) // Write in batches of 400

	count := 0
	var countMu sync.Mutex

	// Periodic flush every minute
	go func() {
		ticker := time.NewTicker(1 * time.Minute)
		for range ticker.C {
			batchWriter.Flush()
		}
	}()

	c.OnRequest(func(r *colly.Request) {
		countMu.Lock()
		count++
		log.Printf("Visiting URL #%d: %s\n", count, r.URL)
		countMu.Unlock()
	})

	c.OnResponse(func(r *colly.Response) {
		log.Printf("Finished URL: %s (Status: %d)\n", r.Request.URL, r.StatusCode)
	})

	c.OnHTML("a[href]", func(e *colly.HTMLElement) {
		link := e.Request.AbsoluteURL(e.Attr("href"))
		if link == "" || !isValidURL(link) {
			return
		}

		cleanedURL := cleanURL(link)
		if cleanedURL == "" {
			return
		}

		mu.Lock()
		isNewURL := !visited[cleanedURL]
		if isNewURL {
			visited[cleanedURL] = true
		}
		mu.Unlock()

		if isNewURL {
			batchWriter.Add(URLData{
				URL:       cleanedURL,
				ParentURL: e.Request.URL.String(),
				SiteName:  STARTURL,
				TimeStamp: time.Now(),
			})

			if strings.Contains(cleanedURL, STARTURL) {
				err := e.Request.Visit(cleanedURL)
				if err != nil {
					log.Printf("Error visiting %s: %v\n", cleanedURL, err)
				}
			}
		}
	})

	c.OnError(func(r *colly.Response, err error) {
		log.Printf("Error visiting %s: %v (Status: %d)\n", r.Request.URL, err, r.StatusCode)
	})

	startURL := "https://www." + STARTURL
	log.Printf("Starting crawl at %s\n", startURL)

	if err := c.Visit(startURL); err != nil {
		log.Fatal("Error starting crawl:", err)
	}

	// Wait with timeout
	done := make(chan bool)
	go func() {
		c.Wait()
		done <- true
	}()

	select {
	case <-done:
		log.Println("Crawl completed normally")
	case <-time.After(5 * time.Minute):
		log.Println("Crawl timed out after 5 minutes")
	}

	// Final flush of any remaining data
	batchWriter.Flush()
	log.Printf("Crawl finished. Check the results directory for CSV files.")
}

func writeToCSV(filename string, results []URLData) error {
	file, err := os.Create(filename)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create file: %v", err)
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Updated headers to match URLData struct
	if err := writer.Write([]string{"SiteName", "URL", "Parent URL", "Timestamp"}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write header: %v", err)
	}

	for _, result := range results {
		if err := writer.Write([]string{
			result.SiteName,
			result.URL,
			result.ParentURL,
			result.TimeStamp.Format(time.RFC3339),
		}); err != nil {
			return fmt.Errorf("failed to write row: %v", err)
		}
	}

	return nil
}

func isValidURL(urlStr string) bool {
	u, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	if err != nil {
		return false
	}
	return u.Scheme == "http" || u.Scheme == "https"
}

func cleanURL(urlStr string) string {
	u, err := url.Parse(urlStr)
	if err != nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Clean the URL
	u.Fragment = ""
	u.RawQuery = ""

	// Normalize the path
	path := strings.TrimSpace(u.Path)
	path = strings.TrimRight(path, "/")
	if path == "" {
		path = "/"
	}
	u.Path = path

	return u.String()
}

File: main.go

// main.go
package main

import (
	"crawlerindexer/internal/insertintodb/db"
	"database/sql"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"path/filepath"
)

func main() {
	database, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", "products.db")
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	defer database.Close()

	if err := db.InitDB(database); err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}

	// Process files from specific brands
	brands := []string{
		"blackberrys", "jockey", "montecarlo", "redtape",
		"westside", "duke", "levi", "raymond", "uspoloassn",
		"spykar", "wrogn",
	}

	for _, brand := range brands {
		pattern := fmt.Sprintf("data/products/%s/*.csv", brand)
		files, err := filepath.Glob(pattern)
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("Error finding files for %s: %v\n", brand, err)
			continue
		}

		for _, file := range files {
			fmt.Printf("Processing %s file: %s\n", brand, file)
			if err := db.ImportCSV(database, file); err != nil {
				log.Printf("Error processing %s: %v\n", file, err)
			}
		}
	}

	fmt.Println("Import completed successfully")
}

File: db.go

package db

import (
	"database/sql"
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"strconv"
	"strings"

	_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"
)

type Product struct {
	URL          string
	Title        string
	Description  string
	Price        float64
	SalePrice    float64
	Currency     string
	ImageURL     string
	Sizes        string
	Availability bool
	Brand        string
	SiteName     string
	Country      string
	Collection   string
	Timestamp    string
	SKU          string
	Category     string
}

func InitDB(db *sql.DB) error {
	schema := `
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS products (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        url TEXT UNIQUE,
        title TEXT,
        description TEXT,
        price REAL,
        sale_price REAL,
        currency TEXT,
        image_url TEXT,
        sizes TEXT,
        availability BOOLEAN,
        brand TEXT,
        site_name TEXT,
        country TEXT,
        collection TEXT,
        timestamp TEXT,
        sku TEXT,
        category TEXT
    );
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_products_brand ON products(brand);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_products_site_name ON products(site_name);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_products_category ON products(category);
    `
	_, err := db.Exec(schema)
	return err
}

func ImportCSV(db *sql.DB, filepath string) error {
	file, err := os.Open(filepath)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	// Read header to determine column positions
	headers, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	// Map column indices
	colMap := make(map[string]int)
	for i, header := range headers {
		header = strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(header))
		colMap[header] = i
	}

	stmt, err := db.Prepare(`
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO products (
            url, title, description, price, sale_price, currency,
            image_url, sizes, availability, brand, site_name,
            country, collection, timestamp, sku, category
        ) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer stmt.Close()

	tx, err := db.Begin()
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err != nil {
			break
		}

		// Get values using column map, with fallbacks
		getValue := func(key string) string {
			if idx, ok := colMap[key]; ok && idx < len(record) {
				return strings.TrimSpace(record[idx])
			}
			return ""
		}

		price, _ := strconv.ParseFloat(getValue("price"), 64)
		salePrice, _ := strconv.ParseFloat(getValue("sale_price"), 64)
		availability := strings.ToLower(getValue("availability")) == "true"

		// Handle image_url vs main_image
		imageURL := getValue("image_url")
		if imageURL == "" {
			imageURL = getValue("main_image")
		}

		_, err = tx.Stmt(stmt).Exec(
			getValue("url"),
			getValue("title"),
			getValue("description"),
			price,
			salePrice,
			getValue("currency"),
			imageURL,
			getValue("sizes"),
			availability,
			getValue("brand"),
			getValue("site_name"),
			getValue("country"),
			getValue("collection"),
			getValue("timestamp"),
			getValue("sku"),
			getValue("category"),
		)

		if err != nil {
			tx.Rollback()
			return fmt.Errorf("error inserting record: %v", err)
		}
	}

	return tx.Commit()
}

File: blackberrys_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type BlackberrysSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewBlackberrysSpider() *BlackberrysSpider {
	return &BlackberrysSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://blackberrys.com",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/blackberrys",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *BlackberrysSpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	return nil
}

func (s *BlackberrysSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/blackberrys.com"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("blackberrys.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string
	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := 20

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}
		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *BlackberrysSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Blackberrys",
		SiteName:  "blackberrys.com",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").First().AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price from meta tag
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='product:price:amount']").First().AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract sizes and availability from KiwiSizing data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "KiwiSizing.data") {
			if variantsData := strings.Split(s.Text(), "variants:")[1]; len(variantsData) > 0 {
				var variants []struct {
					Title     string  `json:"title"`
					Available bool    `json:"available"`
					Price     float64 `json:"price"`
					SKU       string  `json:"sku"`
				}
				if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(variantsData), &variants); err == nil {
					for _, variant := range variants {
						if variant.Available {
							product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, variant.Title)
							product.SKU = variant.SKU
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract currency
	product.Currency = "INR"

	// Extract category and collection from URL path
	paths := strings.Split(url, "/")
	if len(paths) > 2 {
		if paths[1] == "collections" {
			product.Collection = paths[2]
		}
		if len(paths) > 4 && paths[3] == "products" {
			product.Category = paths[2]
		}
	}

	// Check availability
	product.Availability = len(product.Sizes) > 0

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price)
	return product
}

func (s *BlackberrysSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *BlackberrysSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		if len(record) > urlIndex {
			productURL := record[urlIndex]
			if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
				urls = append(urls, productURL)
			}
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

File: duke_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type KiwiSizingData struct {
	Title    string `json:"title"`
	Variants []struct {
		Available bool    `json:"available"`
		SKU       string  `json:"sku"`
		Price     float64 `json:"price"`
		Option1   string  `json:"option1"`
		Option2   string  `json:"option2"`
		Option3   string  `json:"option3"`
	} `json:"variants"`
	Images []string `json:"images"`
}

type DukeSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewDukeSpider() *DukeSpider {
	return &DukeSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://www.dukeindia.com",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/duke",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *DukeSpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	return nil
}

func (s *DukeSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Duke",
		SiteName:  "dukeindia.com",
		Country:   "India",
		Currency:  "INR",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract title - priority to meta tags
	if title := doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:title']").AttrOr("content", ""); title != "" {
		product.Title = strings.TrimSpace(title)
	} else if title := doc.Find("title").Text(); title != "" {
		product.Title = strings.TrimSpace(title)
	}

	// Extract description - priority to twitter description as it's more complete
	if desc := doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:description']").AttrOr("content", ""); desc != "" {
		product.Description = strings.TrimSpace(desc)
	} else if desc := doc.Find("meta[name='description']").AttrOr("content", ""); desc != "" {
		product.Description = strings.TrimSpace(desc)
	}

	// Extract price from twitter meta
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:data1']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.TrimSpace(strings.ReplaceAll(strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, "₹", ""), ",", ""))
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract main image from twitter meta
	if mainImg := doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:image']").AttrOr("content", ""); mainImg != "" {
		product.MainImage = getLargeImageURL(mainImg)
	}

	if product.MainImage == "" {
		if mainImg := doc.Find(".fancybox-image").AttrOr("src", ""); mainImg != "" {
			product.MainImage = getLargeImageURL(mainImg)
		}
	}

	if salePriceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='product:sale_price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); salePriceStr != "" {
		salePriceStr = strings.TrimSpace(strings.ReplaceAll(strings.ReplaceAll(salePriceStr, "₹", ""), ",", ""))
		if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(salePriceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.SalePrice = salePrice
		}
	}
	// Extract SKU and variants from KiwiSizing data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "KiwiSizing.data") {
			var kiwiData KiwiSizingData
			startIndex := strings.Index(s.Text(), "KiwiSizing.data = ") + len("KiwiSizing.data = ")
			endIndex := strings.LastIndex(s.Text(), ";")
			if startIndex > -1 && endIndex > startIndex {
				jsonData := s.Text()[startIndex:endIndex]
				if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &kiwiData); err == nil {
					// Extract sizes and check availability
					sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)
					for _, variant := range kiwiData.Variants {
						if variant.Available {
							product.Availability = true
							if variant.Option1 != "" {
								sizeMap[variant.Option1] = true
							}
						}
					}
					for size := range sizeMap {
						product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
					}

					// Extract SKU from first variant
					if len(kiwiData.Variants) > 0 {
						product.SKU = kiwiData.Variants[0].SKU
					}

					// Extract secondary images
					if len(kiwiData.Images) > 1 {
						for i := 1; i < len(kiwiData.Images) && i <= 4; i++ {
							imgURL := "https:" + kiwiData.Images[i]
							switch i {
							case 1:
								product.SecondaryImage1 = imgURL
							case 2:
								product.SecondaryImage2 = imgURL
							case 3:
								product.SecondaryImage3 = imgURL
							case 4:
								product.SecondaryImage4 = imgURL
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract category from URL
	urlParts := strings.Split(url, "/")
	for i, part := range urlParts {
		if part == "collections" && i+1 < len(urlParts) {
			product.Category = urlParts[i+1]
			product.Collection = urlParts[i+1]
			break
		}
	}

	// Check availability through Add to Cart button if not determined from variants
	if !product.Availability {
		addToCartBtn := doc.Find("input#product-add-to-cart")
		if addToCartBtn.Length() > 0 {
			_, disabled := addToCartBtn.Attr("disabled")
			product.Availability = !disabled
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (SKU: %s)\n", url, product.SKU)
	return product
}
func (s *DukeSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/dukeindia.com"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("dukeindia.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string

	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			fmt.Printf("Found file: %s\n", path)
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
			fmt.Printf("Collected %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), path)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("Total product URLs found: %d\n", len(allProductURLs))

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	// Create output file and writer
	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Write header
	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "secondary_image1", "secondary_image2",
		"secondary_image3", "secondary_image4", "sizes", "availability",
		"brand", "site_name", "country", "collection", "timestamp",
		"sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	// Process URLs in batches
	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}

		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		s.processBatch(batch, writer)

		fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *DukeSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	// Read header to find URL column index
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error reading line: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			fmt.Printf("Line %d: Invalid record length: %d\n", lineCount, len(record))
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}

func (s *DukeSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit // Rate limiting

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			if product := s.scrapeProduct(url); product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice), // Added sale_price here

			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

// Image handling function to convert URLs to larger format
func getLargeImageURL(imgURL string) string {
	// Return empty if no URL
	if imgURL == "" {
		return ""
	}

	// Add https: if URL starts with //
	if strings.HasPrefix(imgURL, "//") {
		imgURL = "https:" + imgURL
	}

	// Replace medium or small image size with larger size
	imgURL = strings.Replace(imgURL, "_medium.", "_1024x1024.", -1)
	imgURL = strings.Replace(imgURL, "_small.", "_1024x1024.", -1)

	return imgURL
}

File: helpers.go

package spiders

import (
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

// Helper function to check if slice contains string
func contains(slice []string, str string) bool {
	for _, v := range slice {
		if v == str {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

// Helper function to count non-empty secondary images
func countSecondaryImages(p *ProductItem) int {
	count := 0
	if p.SecondaryImage1 != "" {
		count++
	}
	if p.SecondaryImage2 != "" {
		count++
	}
	if p.SecondaryImage3 != "" {
		count++
	}
	if p.SecondaryImage4 != "" {
		count++
	}
	return count
}

// Helper function to remove duplicate images and low-quality variants
func removeDuplicateImages(images []string) []string {
	seen := make(map[string]bool)
	result := []string{}

	for _, img := range images {
		// Remove width parameter for comparison
		baseURL := strings.Split(img, "?")[0]
		if !seen[baseURL] {
			seen[baseURL] = true
			result = append(result, img)
		}
	}
	return result
}

// Helper function to clean and normalize URLs
func normalizeURL(url string) string {
	if !strings.HasPrefix(url, "http") {
		if strings.HasPrefix(url, "//") {
			url = "https:" + url
		} else {
			url = "https://" + url
		}
	}
	return url
}

func cleanDescription(desc string) string {
	// Remove special symbols and extra spaces
	desc = strings.ReplaceAll(desc, "|", "")
	desc = strings.ReplaceAll(desc, "-", "")
	desc = strings.ReplaceAll(desc, "•", "")
	desc = strings.TrimSpace(desc)

	// Remove multiple spaces
	desc = regexp.MustCompile(`\s+`).ReplaceAllString(desc, " ")

	return desc
}

File: jockey_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type JockeySpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewJockeySpider() *JockeySpider {
	return &JockeySpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://www.jockey.in",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/jockey",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *JockeySpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	return nil
}

func (s *JockeySpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/jockey.in"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("jockey.in_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string
	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := 20

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}
		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *JockeySpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Jockey",
		SiteName:  "jockey.in",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract main image
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract currency
	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "INR")

	// Extract category from MP_CONFIG data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "window.__MP_CONFIG__") {
			if categoryData := strings.Split(s.Text(), "category:"); len(categoryData) > 1 {
				product.Category = strings.Split(strings.Split(categoryData[1], ",")[0], "\"")[1]
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract collection IDs
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "collection_ids:") {
			if collectionData := strings.Split(s.Text(), "collection_ids:"); len(collectionData) > 1 {
				product.Collection = strings.Split(strings.Split(collectionData[1], ",")[0], "'")[1]
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract SKU from URL
	if parts := strings.Split(url, "-"); len(parts) > 0 {
		product.SKU = strings.TrimSpace(parts[len(parts)-1])
	}

	// Extract sizes from variant data
	doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
		}
	})

	// Check availability based on add to cart button
	product.Availability = doc.Find("button[name='add']").Length() > 0

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price)
	return product
}

func (s *JockeySpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *JockeySpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		if len(record) > urlIndex {
			productURL := record[urlIndex]
			if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
				urls = append(urls, productURL)
			}
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

File: levi_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type LeviSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewLeviSpider() *LeviSpider {
	return &LeviSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://levi.in",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/levi",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *LeviSpider) Start() error {

func (s *LeviSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	// Extract SKU from URL
	sku := ""
	if parts := strings.Split(url, "/products/"); len(parts) > 1 {
		skuParts := strings.Split(parts[1], "-")
		sku = skuParts[len(skuParts)-1]
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Levi's",
		SiteName:  "levi.in",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
		SKU:       sku,
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}
	// Extract sale price after the regular price extraction
	if salePriceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='product:sale_price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); salePriceStr != "" {
		salePriceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(salePriceStr, ",", "")
		if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(salePriceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.SalePrice = salePrice
		}
	}
	// Extract main image
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	// Extract secondary images
	var allImages []string

	doc.Find(".splide__slide:not(.splide__slide--clone) .global-media-settings").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		// Get high quality image URL from srcset
		srcset := s.AttrOr("srcset", "")
		if srcset != "" {
			srcsetParts := strings.Split(srcset, ",")
			for _, part := range srcsetParts {
				part = strings.TrimSpace(part)
				if strings.Contains(part, "1034w") { // Get highest resolution
					urlPart := strings.Split(part, " ")[0]
					imageURL := normalizeURL(urlPart)
					allImages = append(allImages, imageURL)
					break
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Remove duplicates and assign images
	uniqueImages := removeDuplicateImages(allImages)

	if len(uniqueImages) > 0 {
		product.MainImage = uniqueImages[0]

		// Assign secondary images if available
		for i := 1; i < len(uniqueImages) && i <= 4; i++ {
			switch i {
			case 1:
				product.SecondaryImage1 = uniqueImages[i]
			case 2:
				product.SecondaryImage2 = uniqueImages[i]
			case 3:
				product.SecondaryImage3 = uniqueImages[i]
			case 4:
				product.SecondaryImage4 = uniqueImages[i]
			}
		}
	}
	// Extract sizes
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)
	doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option, .single-option-selector-product option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			sizeMap[size] = true
		}
	})

	for size := range sizeMap {
		product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
	}

	// Extract category
	doc.Find(".breadcrumb__item").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if i == 1 { // Usually second breadcrumb is the category
			product.Category = strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		}
	})

	// Check availability
	addToCart := doc.Find("button[name='add']").Text()
	product.Availability = !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "sold out") &&
		!strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "out of stock")

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (SKU: %s, Images: Main + %d secondary)\n",
		url, product.SKU, countSecondaryImages(product))
	return product
}

func (s *LeviSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}

func (s *LeviSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			if product := s.scrapeProduct(url); product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),  // Added sale_price

			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

File: montecarlo_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)


type MontecarloSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewMontecarloSpider() *MontecarloSpider {
	return &MontecarloSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://www.montecarlo.in",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/montecarlo",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(200 * time.Millisecond), // 1 request per 200 milisecond
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *MontecarloSpider) Start() error {
	// Create output directory
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)

	// Process cleaned URLs
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}

	// Wait for all goroutines to finish
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)

	return nil
}

// ---------------

func (s *MontecarloSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/montecarlo.in"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("montecarlo.in_%s.csv", timestamp))

	// First, collect all product URLs
	var allProductURLs []string

	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	// Walk through all directories
	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			fmt.Printf("Found file: %s\n", path)
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
			fmt.Printf("Collected %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), path)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("Total product URLs found: %d\n", len(allProductURLs))

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	// Create output file and writer
	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Write header
	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	// Process URLs in batches of 20
	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}

		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		// Process batch
		s.processBatch(batch, writer)

		fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *MontecarloSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	// Read header to find URL column index
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	// Find URL column index
	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Processing file: %s (URL column index: %d)\n", filePath, urlIndex)

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error reading line: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			fmt.Printf("Line %d: Invalid record length: %d\n", lineCount, len(record))
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}
func (s *MontecarloSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	// Start a goroutine for each URL in the batch
	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit // Rate limiting

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	// Wait for all goroutines in this batch to complete
	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	// Write results as they come in
	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			// fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			"",
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *MontecarloSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Monte Carlo",
		SiteName:  "montecarlo.in",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata

	// Fix image URL extraction
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='product:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")
	doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='product:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price - handle comma-separated values
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='product:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		// Remove commas and convert to float
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64)
		if err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract sale price from schema data
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := s.Text()
		if strings.Contains(jsonData, "Product") {
			var schemaData struct {
				Offers []struct {
					Price float64 `json:"price"`
				} `json:"offers"`
			}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil {
				if len(schemaData.Offers) > 0 {
					product.SalePrice = schemaData.Offers[0].Price
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract sizes from schema data and options
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool) // Use map to avoid duplicates

	// From schema data
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := s.Text()
		if strings.Contains(jsonData, "Product") {
			var schemaData struct {
				Offers []struct {
					Name string `json:"name"`
				} `json:"offers"`
			}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil {
				for _, offer := range schemaData.Offers {
					size := strings.TrimSpace(offer.Name)
					if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
						sizeMap[size] = true
					}
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// From size selector
	doc.Find("select[name='options[Size]'] option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			sizeMap[size] = true
		}
	})

	// Convert size map to slice
	for size := range sizeMap {
		product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
	}

	// Extract SKU from schema data
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := s.Text()
		if strings.Contains(jsonData, "Product") {
			var schemaData struct {
				Offers []struct {
					SKU string `json:"sku"`
				} `json:"offers"`
			}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil {
				if len(schemaData.Offers) > 0 {
					product.SKU = schemaData.Offers[0].SKU
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Check availability
	addToCart := doc.Find("button#AddToCart .loader-button__text").Text()
	product.Availability = !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "sold out") &&
		!strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "out of stock")

	// Extract collection from URL
	if parts := strings.Split(url, "/collections/"); len(parts) > 1 {
		product.Collection = strings.Split(parts[1], "/")[0]
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f, Sale Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price, product.SalePrice)
	return product
}

File: productItems.go

package spiders

// ProductItem represents the scraped product data
type ProductItem struct {
	URL         string
	Title       string
	Description string
	Price       float64
	SalePrice   float64
	Currency    string
    MainImage       string    // Primary product image
    SecondaryImage1 string    // Additional images as separate fields
    SecondaryImage2 string
    SecondaryImage3 string
    SecondaryImage4 string
	Sizes        []string
	Availability bool
	Brand        string
	SiteName     string
	Country      string
	Collection   string
	Timestamp    string
	SKU          string
	Category     string
}

File: raymond_spider.go

	mutex       sync.Mutex

}
