}

func (s *RaymondSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}

func (s *RaymondSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			if product := s.scrapeProduct(url); product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()
	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *RaymondSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	// Extract Shopify data
	var sku, collection, category string
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "ShopifyAnalytics") {
			skuRegex := regexp.MustCompile(`"sku":"([^"]+)"`)
			categoryRegex := regexp.MustCompile(`"category":"([^"]+)"`)

			if match := skuRegex.FindStringSubmatch(s.Text()); len(match) > 1 {
				sku = match[1]
			}
			if match := categoryRegex.FindStringSubmatch(s.Text()); len(match) > 1 {
				category = match[1]
				collection = category // Use category as collection for Raymond
			}
		}
	})

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:        url,
		Brand:      "Raymond",
		SiteName:   "myraymond.com",
		Country:    "India",
		Timestamp:  time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
		SKU:        sku,
		Category:   category,
		Collection: collection,
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Get image URL
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}
	// Extract sale price
	if salePriceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='product:sale_price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); salePriceStr != "" {
		salePriceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(salePriceStr, ",", "")
		if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(salePriceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.SalePrice = salePrice
		}
	} else {
		// Alternative way to find sale price from spans/divs if meta tag not available
		doc.Find(".price.price--on-sale .price__sale").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
			if priceText := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text()); priceText != "" {
				priceStr := strings.ReplaceAll(strings.ReplaceAll(priceText, "₹", ""), ",", "")
				if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
					product.SalePrice = salePrice
				}
			}
		})
	}
	// Extract sizes
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)
	doc.Find("select[name='options[Size]'] option, .single-option-selector option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			sizeMap[size] = true
		}
	})

	var allImages []string

	// Find all product images from splide slides with high quality
	doc.Find(".splide__slide img").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		srcset := s.AttrOr("srcset", "")
		srcsetParts := strings.Split(srcset, ",")

		var highestQualityImage string
		var maxWidth int

		for _, part := range srcsetParts {
			part = strings.TrimSpace(part)
			if strings.Contains(part, "webp") || strings.Contains(part, "jpg") {
				urlParts := strings.Split(part, " ")
				if len(urlParts) > 0 {
					imageURL := strings.TrimPrefix(urlParts[0], "//")
					if !strings.HasPrefix(imageURL, "http") {
						imageURL = "https://" + imageURL
					}

					// Prefer images without width parameter or highest width
					if !strings.Contains(imageURL, "width=") {
						highestQualityImage = imageURL
						break
					} else if strings.Contains(urlParts[1], "w") {
						widthStr := strings.TrimSuffix(urlParts[1], "w")
						if w, err := strconv.Atoi(widthStr); err == nil && w > maxWidth {
							maxWidth = w
							highestQualityImage = imageURL
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if highestQualityImage != "" && !contains(allImages, highestQualityImage) {
			allImages = append(allImages, highestQualityImage)
		}
	})

	// Also check global-media-settings for additional images
	doc.Find(".global-media-settings").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		srcset := s.AttrOr("srcset", "")
		if src := s.AttrOr("src", ""); src != "" && !contains(allImages, src) {
			imageURL := strings.TrimPrefix(src, "//")
			if !strings.HasPrefix(imageURL, "http") {
				imageURL = "https://" + imageURL
			}
			allImages = append(allImages, imageURL)
		}

		// Process srcset for high-quality versions
		srcsetParts := strings.Split(srcset, ",")
		for _, part := range srcsetParts {
			if strings.Contains(part, "webp") && strings.Contains(part, "600w") {
				urlParts := strings.Split(strings.TrimSpace(part), " ")
				if len(urlParts) > 0 {
					imageURL := strings.TrimPrefix(urlParts[0], "//")
					if !strings.HasPrefix(imageURL, "http") {
						imageURL = "https://" + imageURL
					}
					if !contains(allImages, imageURL) {
						allImages = append(allImages, imageURL)
					}
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Deduplicate and assign images
	uniqueImages := removeDuplicateImages(allImages)

	if len(uniqueImages) > 0 {
		product.MainImage = uniqueImages[0]

		// Assign up to 4 secondary images
		if len(uniqueImages) > 1 {
			product.SecondaryImage1 = uniqueImages[1]
		}
		if len(uniqueImages) > 2 {
			product.SecondaryImage2 = uniqueImages[2]
		}
		if len(uniqueImages) > 3 {
			product.SecondaryImage3 = uniqueImages[3]
		}
		if len(uniqueImages) > 4 {
			product.SecondaryImage4 = uniqueImages[4]
		}
	}

	for size := range sizeMap {
		product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
	}

	// Check availability
	addToCart := doc.Find("button[name='add'], .add-to-cart-button").Text()
	product.Availability = !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "sold out") &&
		!strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(addToCart), "out of stock")

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (SKU: %s, Images: Main + %d secondary)\n",
		url, product.SKU, countSecondaryImages(product))
	return product
}

File: redtape_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type RedTapeSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewRedTapeSpider() *RedTapeSpider {
	return &RedTapeSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://redtape.com",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/redtape",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second),
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *RedTapeSpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	return nil
}

func (s *RedTapeSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Red Tape",
		SiteName:  "redtape.com",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract sale price
	if salePriceStr := doc.Find("[data-product-price]").AttrOr("data-product-price", ""); salePriceStr != "" {
		salePriceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(salePriceStr, ",", "")
		if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(salePriceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.SalePrice = salePrice
		}
	}

	// Extract currency
	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "INR")

	// Extract images
	var images []string
	doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		imgURL := s.AttrOr("content", "")
		if imgURL != "" {
			images = append(images, imgURL)
		}
	})

	// Assign images
	if len(images) > 0 {
		product.MainImage = images[0]
		if len(images) > 1 {
			product.SecondaryImage1 = images[1]
		}
		if len(images) > 2 {
			product.SecondaryImage2 = images[2]
		}
		if len(images) > 3 {
			product.SecondaryImage3 = images[3]
		}
		if len(images) > 4 {
			product.SecondaryImage4 = images[4]
		}
	}

	// Extract sizes
	doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option, .variant-option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
		}
	})

	// Extract SKU from URL or product reference
	if sku := doc.Find("[data-product-sku]").AttrOr("data-product-sku", ""); sku != "" {
		product.SKU = sku
	} else if parts := strings.Split(url, "-"); len(parts) > 0 {
		product.SKU = strings.TrimSpace(parts[len(parts)-1])
	}

	// Check availability from add-to-cart button state
	product.Availability = !doc.Find("button[name='add']").HasClass("sold-out")

	// Extract category from breadcrumb or URL path
	if category := doc.Find(".breadcrumb__item--current").Text(); category != "" {
		product.Category = strings.TrimSpace(category)
	} else if paths := strings.Split(url, "/"); len(paths) > 2 {
		product.Category = paths[len(paths)-2]
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price)
	return product
}

func (s *RedTapeSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/redtape.com"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("redtape.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string
	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "secondary_image1", "secondary_image2", "secondary_image3", "secondary_image4",
		"sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}
		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))
		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *RedTapeSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *RedTapeSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		if len(record) > urlIndex {
			productURL := record[urlIndex]
			if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
				urls = append(urls, productURL)
			}
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

File: spykey_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type SpykarSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewSpykarSpider() *SpykarSpider {
	return &SpykarSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://spykar.com",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/spykar",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *SpykarSpider) Start() error {
	// Create output directory
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)

	// Process cleaned URLs
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}

	// Wait for all goroutines to finish
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)

	return nil
}

func (s *SpykarSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/spykar.com"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("spykar.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string

	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			fmt.Printf("Found file: %s\n", path)
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
			fmt.Printf("Collected %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), path)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("Total product URLs found: %d\n", len(allProductURLs))

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}

		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		s.processBatch(batch, writer)

		fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *SpykarSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	// Read header to find URL column index
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Processing file: %s (URL column index: %d)\n", filePath, urlIndex)

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error reading line: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			fmt.Printf("Line %d: Invalid record length: %d\n", lineCount, len(record))
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}

func (s *SpykarSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	// Start a goroutine for each URL in the batch
	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit // Rate limiting

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	// Wait for all goroutines in this batch to complete
	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	// Write results as they come in
	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *SpykarSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Spykar",
		SiteName:  "spykar.com",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract image URL
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	// Extract price from JSON-LD
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		jsonData := s.Text()
		if strings.Contains(jsonData, "Product") {
			var schemaData struct {
				Offers struct {
					Price         string `json:"price"`
					PriceCurrency string `json:"priceCurrency"`
				} `json:"offers"`
				SKU string `json:"sku"`
			}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil {
				if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(schemaData.Offers.Price, 64); err == nil {
					product.Price = price
				}
				product.Currency = schemaData.Offers.PriceCurrency
				product.SKU = schemaData.SKU
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract sale price if available
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "window.ad_product") {
			if priceStr := strings.Split(s.Text(), "price\": \"")[1]; len(priceStr) > 0 {
				if salePrice, err := strconv.ParseFloat(strings.Split(priceStr, "\"")[0], 64); err == nil {
					product.SalePrice = salePrice
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract sizes
	var sizes []string
	doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			sizes = append(sizes, size)
		}
	})
	product.Sizes = sizes

	// Check availability
	product.Availability = doc.Find("button.product-form__add-button").AttrOr("disabled", "") != "disabled"

	// Extract category and collection
	if paths := strings.Split(url, "/collections/"); len(paths) > 1 {
		if collection := strings.Split(paths[1], "/")[0]; collection != "products" {
			product.Collection = collection
		}
	}

	// Extract category from product data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "window.ad_product") {
			if category := strings.Split(s.Text(), "category\": \"")[1]; len(category) > 0 {
				product.Category = strings.Split(category, "\"")[0]
			}
		}
	})

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f, Sale Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price, product.SalePrice)
	return product
}

File: uspolo_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type USPoloSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewUSPoloSpider() *USPoloSpider {
	return &USPoloSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://uspoloassn.in",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/uspolo",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second), // 1 request per second
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *USPoloSpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)

	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}

	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)

	return nil
}

func (s *USPoloSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	// Initialize product with basic info
	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "U.S. Polo Assn.",
		SiteName:  "U.S. Polo Assn. India",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract title
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.Title == "" {
		product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	// Extract description
	description := doc.Find("meta[name='twitter:description']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if description == "" {
		description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}
	product.Description = cleanDescription(description)

	// Extract price from sale price span
	if priceStr := doc.Find("span.price-item.price-item--sale[data-sale-price]").Text(); priceStr != "" {
		// Clean the price string
		priceStr = strings.TrimSpace(priceStr)
		// Remove the ₹ symbol and any spaces
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, "₹", "")
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, " ", "")
		// Remove commas if present
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")

		// Convert to float
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
			product.Currency = "INR" // Set currency since we found the ₹ symbol
		}
	}
	// Fallback to schema.org data if direct price not found
	if product.Price == 0 {
		doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
			if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "Product") {
				var schemaData struct {
					Offers []struct {
						Price string `json:"price"`
					} `json:"offers"`
				}
				if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(s.Text()), &schemaData); err == nil {
					if len(schemaData.Offers) > 0 {
						priceStr := strings.ReplaceAll(schemaData.Offers[0].Price, ",", "")
						if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
							product.Price = price
						}
					}
				}
			}
		})
	}

	// Extract main image
	product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").AttrOr("content", "")
	if product.MainImage == "" {
		product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image']").AttrOr("content", "")
	}

	// Extract SKU from schema.org data
	doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "Product") {
			var schemaData struct {
				SKU string `json:"sku"`
			}
			if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(s.Text()), &schemaData); err == nil {
				product.SKU = schemaData.SKU
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract category from URL
	urlParts := strings.Split(url, "/")
	for i, part := range urlParts {
		if part == "products" && i+1 < len(urlParts) {
			categories := strings.Split(urlParts[i+1], "-")
			if len(categories) > 0 {
				product.Category = categories[0]
			}
			break
		}
	}

	// Extract sizes and availability from schema.org data
	// Check availability based on Add to Cart button
	addToCartBtn := doc.Find("input#addToCart")
	if addToCartBtn.Length() > 0 {
		// Check if the Add to Cart button exists and is not disabled
		_, disabled := addToCartBtn.Attr("disabled")
		product.Availability = !disabled && addToCartBtn.HasClass("AddtoCart")
	}

	// Additional check for quantity selector
	qtyInput := doc.Find("input.js-qty-input.quantity")
	if qtyInput.Length() > 0 {
		// If quantity input exists and has a min value of 1, product is likely available
		minVal, exists := qtyInput.Attr("min")
		if exists && minVal == "1" {
			// Cross-reference with hidden product ID
			productID, exists := doc.Find("input[name='product-id']").Attr("value")
			if exists && productID != "" {
				product.Availability = true
			}
		}
	}

	// Double check with quantity controls
	qtyControls := doc.Find(".quantity-control-up, .quantity-control-down")
	if qtyControls.Length() == 0 {
		// If quantity controls are not present, product might be out of stock
		product.Availability = false
	}
	// Extract sizes from size selector
	sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)
	doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option, .single-option-selector option").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			sizeMap[size] = true
		}
	})

	// Convert size map to slice
	for size := range sizeMap {
		product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
	}

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (SKU: %s)\n", url, product.SKU)
	return product
}

func (s *USPoloSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/uspoloassn.in"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("uspoloassn.in_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string

	fmt.Println("Scanning U.S. Polo directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}

		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			fmt.Printf("Found file: %s\n", path)
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
			fmt.Printf("Collected %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), path)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	fmt.Printf("Total U.S. Polo product URLs found: %d\n", len(allProductURLs))

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	// Create output file and writer
	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	// Write headers
	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "currency",
		"image_url", "secondary_image1", "secondary_image2",
		"secondary_image3", "secondary_image4", "sizes", "availability",
		"brand", "site_name", "country", "collection", "timestamp",
		"sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	// Process URLs in batches of 20
	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}

		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

		s.processBatch(batch, writer)

		fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *USPoloSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)

	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	lineCount := 0
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		lineCount++
		if len(record) <= urlIndex {
			continue
		}

		productURL := record[urlIndex]
		if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
			urls = append(urls, productURL)
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs out of %d lines in %s\n", len(urls), lineCount, filePath)
	return urls, nil
}

func (s *USPoloSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			if product := s.scrapeProduct(url); product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

File: westside_spider.go

package spiders

import (
	"encoding/csv"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type WestsideSpider struct {
	client      *http.Client
	baseURL     string
	outputDir   string
	wg          sync.WaitGroup
	mutex       sync.Mutex
	rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
	productChan chan ProductItem
}

func NewWestsideSpider() *WestsideSpider {
	return &WestsideSpider{
		client: &http.Client{
			Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
		},
		baseURL:     "https://www.westside.com",
		outputDir:   "./data/products/westside",
		rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second),
		productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
	}
}

func (s *WestsideSpider) Start() error {
	os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
	err := s.processCleanedURLs()
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
	}
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(s.productChan)
	return nil
}

func (s *WestsideSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
	resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}
	defer resp.Body.Close()

	doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
		return nil
	}

	product := &ProductItem{
		URL:       url,
		Brand:     "Westside",
		SiteName:  "westside.com",
		Country:   "India",
		Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	}

	// Extract metadata
	product.Title = doc.Find("meta[property='og:title']").AttrOr("content", "")
	product.Description = doc.Find("meta[property='og:description']").AttrOr("content", "")

	// Extract price
	if priceStr := doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:amount']").AttrOr("content", ""); priceStr != "" {
		priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, ",", "")
		if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
			product.Price = price
		}
	}

	// Extract currency
	product.Currency = doc.Find("meta[property='og:price:currency']").AttrOr("content", "INR")

	// Extract images
	var images []string
	doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		imgURL := s.AttrOr("content", "")
		if imgURL != "" {
			images = append(images, imgURL)
		}
	})

	// Assign images
	if len(images) > 0 {
		product.MainImage = images[0]
		if len(images) > 1 {
			product.SecondaryImage1 = images[1]
		}
		if len(images) > 2 {
			product.SecondaryImage2 = images[2]
		}
		if len(images) > 3 {
			product.SecondaryImage3 = images[3]
		}
		if len(images) > 4 {
			product.SecondaryImage4 = images[4]
		}
	}

	// Extract vendor/brand from moeApp data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "moeApp.product") {
			if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "vendor:") {
				vendor := strings.Split(s.Text(), "vendor: \"")[1]
				vendor = strings.Split(vendor, "\"")[0]
				if vendor != "" {
					product.Brand = vendor
				}
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract sizes
	doc.Find("select[name='options[Size]'] option, .swatch-element").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
		if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
			product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
		}
	})

	// Extract SKU from URL
	if parts := strings.Split(url, "-"); len(parts) > 0 {
		product.SKU = strings.TrimSpace(parts[len(parts)-1])
	}

	// Check availability from moeApp data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "moeApp.product") {
			if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "available: \"true\"") {
				product.Availability = true
			}
		}
	})

	// Extract category/product type from moeApp data
	doc.Find("script").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
		if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "moeApp.product") {
			if strings.Contains(s.Text(), "product_type:") {
				category := strings.Split(s.Text(), "product_type: \"")[1]
				category = strings.Split(category, "\"")[0]
				if category != "" {
					product.Category = category
				}
			}
		}
	})

	fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price)
	return product
}

func (s *WestsideSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
	cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/westside.com"
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
	outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("westside.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

	var allProductURLs []string
	fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

	err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil {
			return err
		}
		if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
			urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
				return nil
			}
			allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
		}
		return nil
	})

	if err != nil {
		return err
	}

	if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
	}

	file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
	defer writer.Flush()

	headers := []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "secondary_image1", "secondary_image2", "secondary_image3", "secondary_image4",
		"sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
	writer.Write(headers)

	batchSize := 20
	totalBatches := (len(allProductURLs) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

	for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
		end := i + batchSize
		if end > len(allProductURLs) {
			end = len(allProductURLs)
		}
		batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
		batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
		fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))
		s.processBatch(batch, writer)
	}

	return nil
}

func (s *WestsideSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
	resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

	for _, url := range urls {
		s.wg.Add(1)
		go func(url string) {
			defer s.wg.Done()
			<-s.rateLimit

			fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
			product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
			if product != nil {
				resultChan <- *product
			}
		}(url)
	}

	go func() {
		s.wg.Wait()
		close(resultChan)
	}()

	for product := range resultChan {
		record := []string{
			product.URL,
			product.Title,
			product.Description,
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
			fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
			product.Currency,
			product.MainImage,
			product.SecondaryImage1,
			product.SecondaryImage2,
			product.SecondaryImage3,
			product.SecondaryImage4,
			strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
			fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
			product.Brand,
			product.SiteName,
			product.Country,
			product.Collection,
			product.Timestamp,
			product.SKU,
			product.Category,
		}

		s.mutex.Lock()
		writer.Write(record)
		writer.Flush()
		s.mutex.Unlock()
	}
}

func (s *WestsideSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
	file, err := os.Open(filePath)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	defer file.Close()

	reader := csv.NewReader(file)
	header, err := reader.Read()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	urlIndex := -1
	for i, column := range header {
		if column == "URL" {
			urlIndex = i
			break
		}
	}

	if urlIndex == -1 {
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
	}

	var urls []string
	for {
		record, err := reader.Read()
		if err == io.EOF {
			break
		}
		if err != nil {
			continue
		}

		if len(record) > urlIndex {
			productURL := record[urlIndex]
			if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
				urls = append(urls, productURL)
			}
		}
	}

	return urls, nil
}

File: wrogn_spider.go

package spiders

import (
    "encoding/csv"
    "encoding/json"
    "fmt"
    "io"
    "net/http"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "strconv"
    "strings"
    "sync"
    "time"

    "github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
)

type WrognSpider struct {
    client      *http.Client
    baseURL     string
    outputDir   string
    wg          sync.WaitGroup
    mutex       sync.Mutex
    rateLimit   <-chan time.Time
    productChan chan ProductItem
}


func NewWrognSpider() *WrognSpider {
    return &WrognSpider{
        client: &http.Client{
            Timeout: 30 * time.Second,
        },
        baseURL:     "https://wrogn.com",
        outputDir:   "./data/products/wrogn",
        rateLimit:   time.Tick(time.Second),
        productChan: make(chan ProductItem, 100),
    }
}

func (s *WrognSpider) Start() error {
    os.MkdirAll(s.outputDir, 0755)
    err := s.processCleanedURLs()
    if err != nil {
        return fmt.Errorf("error processing cleaned URLs: %v", err)
    }
    s.wg.Wait()
    close(s.productChan)
    return nil
}

func (s *WrognSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem {
    resp, err := s.client.Get(url)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error fetching %s: %v\n", url, err)
        return nil
    }
    defer resp.Body.Close()

    doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
        return nil
    }

    product := &ProductItem{
        URL:       url,
        Brand:     "Wrogn",
        SiteName:  "wrogn.com",
        Country:   "India",
        Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
    }

    // Extract from schema.org data
    doc.Find("script[type='application/ld+json']").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
        jsonText := s.Text()
        if strings.Contains(jsonText, "Product") {
            var schemaData struct {
                Name            string `json:"name"`
                Description     string `json:"description"`
                AggregateRating struct {
                    RatingValue string `json:"ratingValue"`
                    RatingCount string `json:"ratingCount"`
                } `json:"aggregateRating"`
                Offers struct {
                    Price        string `json:"price"`
                    PriceCurrency string `json:"priceCurrency"`
                    Availability string `json:"availability"`
                } `json:"offers"`
            }
            if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonText), &schemaData); err == nil {
                product.Title = schemaData.Name
                product.Description = schemaData.Description
                
           
           
                
                if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(schemaData.Offers.Price, 64); err == nil {
                    product.Price = price
                }
                product.Currency = schemaData.Offers.PriceCurrency
                product.Availability = strings.Contains(schemaData.Offers.Availability, "InStock")
            }
        }
    })


    // Extract main image
    product.MainImage = doc.Find("meta[property='og:image:secure_url']").First().AttrOr("content", "")

    // Extract sizes
    doc.Find("select[name='Size'] option, .single-option-selector__radio").Each(func(i int, s *goquery.Selection) {
        size := strings.TrimSpace(s.Text())
        if size != "" && !strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), "select") {
            product.Sizes = append(product.Sizes, size)
        }
    })

    // Extract category from URL structure
    paths := strings.Split(url, "/")
    if len(paths) > 2 {
        product.Category = paths[len(paths)-2]
    }

    fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price)
    return product
}

func (s *WrognSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) {
    resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

    for _, url := range urls {
        s.wg.Add(1)
        go func(url string) {
            defer s.wg.Done()
            <-s.rateLimit
            
            fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
            product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
            if product != nil {
                resultChan <- *product
            }
        }(url)
    }

    go func() {
        s.wg.Wait()
        close(resultChan)
    }()

    for product := range resultChan {
        record := []string{
            product.URL,
            product.Title,
            product.Description,
            fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
            fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
            product.Currency,
            product.MainImage,
            strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
            fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
            product.Brand,
            product.SiteName,
            product.Country,
            product.Collection,
            product.Timestamp,
            product.SKU,
            product.Category,
        
        }

        s.mutex.Lock()
        writer.Write(record)
        writer.Flush()
        s.mutex.Unlock()
    }
}

func (s *WrognSpider) processCleanedURLs() error {
    cleanedDir := "./data/cleaned/urls/wrogn.com"
    timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
    outputFile := filepath.Join(s.outputDir, fmt.Sprintf("wrogn.com_%s.csv", timestamp))

    var allProductURLs []string
    fmt.Println("Scanning directories for cleaned URL files...")

    err := filepath.Walk(cleanedDir, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
        if err != nil {
            return err
        }
        if !info.IsDir() && strings.HasPrefix(info.Name(), "cleaned_urls_") {
            urls, err := s.collectURLsFromFile(path)
            if err != nil {
                fmt.Printf("Error reading file %s: %v\n", path, err)
                return nil
            }
            allProductURLs = append(allProductURLs, urls...)
        }
        return nil
    })

    if err != nil {
        return err
    }

    if len(allProductURLs) == 0 {
        return fmt.Errorf("no product URLs found")
    }

    file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    defer file.Close()

    writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
    defer writer.Flush()

    headers := []string{
        "url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
        "image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
        "collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category", 
    }
    writer.Write(headers)

    batchSize := 20

    for i := 0; i < len(allProductURLs); i += batchSize {
        end := i + batchSize
        if end > len(allProductURLs) {
            end = len(allProductURLs)
        }
        batch := allProductURLs[i:end]
        s.processBatch(batch, writer)
    }

    return nil
}

func (s *WrognSpider) collectURLsFromFile(filePath string) ([]string, error) {
    file, err := os.Open(filePath)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    defer file.Close()

    reader := csv.NewReader(file)
    header, err := reader.Read()
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }

    urlIndex := -1
    for i, column := range header {
        if column == "URL" {
            urlIndex = i
            break
        }
    }

    if urlIndex == -1 {
        return nil, fmt.Errorf("URL column not found in header: %v", header)
    }

    var urls []string
    for {
        record, err := reader.Read()
        if err == io.EOF {
            break
        }
        if err != nil {
            continue
        }

        if len(record) > urlIndex {
            productURL := record[urlIndex]
            if strings.Contains(productURL, "/products/") {
                urls = append(urls, productURL)
            }
        }
    }

    return urls, nil
}

File: main.go

package main

import (
    "encoding/csv"
    "fmt"
    "io"
    "os"
    "path/filepath"
    "regexp"
    "strings"
    "time"
)

func main() {
    baseDir := "./data/urls"
    cleanedBaseDir := "./data/cleaned/urls"
    
    // Create cleaned base directory if it doesn't exist
    os.MkdirAll(cleanedBaseDir, 0755)
    
    // Compile regex patterns for valid product URLs
    productPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`^https?://[^/]+/products/[^/\s]+$`)
    collectionProductPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`^https?://[^/]+/collections/[^/]+/products/[^/\s]+$`)
    
    // Process each website folder
    websites, _ := os.ReadDir(baseDir)
    for _, website := range websites {
        if !website.IsDir() {
            continue
        }
        
        websitePath := filepath.Join(baseDir, website.Name())
        cleanedWebsitePath := filepath.Join(cleanedBaseDir, website.Name())
        
        // Create cleaned website directory
        os.MkdirAll(cleanedWebsitePath, 0755)
        
        // Process dated folders within website folder
        dateFolders, _ := os.ReadDir(websitePath)
        for _, dateFolder := range dateFolders {
            if !dateFolder.IsDir() {
                continue
            }
            
            batchPath := filepath.Join(websitePath, dateFolder.Name())
            cleanedDatePath := filepath.Join(cleanedWebsitePath, dateFolder.Name())
            
            // Create cleaned date directory
            os.MkdirAll(cleanedDatePath, 0755)
            
            // Process and merge batch files
            uniqueRows := make(map[string][]string)
            processBatchFolder(batchPath, productPattern, collectionProductPattern, uniqueRows)
            
            // Generate timestamp for cleaned file
            timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
            cleanedFileName := fmt.Sprintf("cleaned_urls_%s.csv", timestamp)
            cleanedFilePath := filepath.Join(cleanedDatePath, cleanedFileName)
            
            // Write cleaned data
            writeOutput(cleanedFilePath, uniqueRows)
        }
    }
}

func processBatchFolder(folderPath string, productPattern, collectionProductPattern *regexp.Regexp, uniqueRows map[string][]string) {
    files, _ := os.ReadDir(folderPath)
    for _, file := range files {
        if !strings.HasPrefix(file.Name(), "batch") || !strings.HasSuffix(file.Name(), ".csv") {
            continue
        }
        
        filePath := filepath.Join(folderPath, file.Name())
        processFile(filePath, productPattern, collectionProductPattern, uniqueRows)
    }
}

func processFile(filepath string, productPattern, collectionProductPattern *regexp.Regexp, uniqueRows map[string][]string) {
    file, err := os.Open(filepath)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error opening file %s: %v\n", filepath, err)
        return
    }
    defer file.Close()
    
    reader := csv.NewReader(file)
    
    // Read header
    header, err := reader.Read()
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error reading header from %s: %v\n", filepath, err)
        return
    }
    
    // Find URL column index
    urlIndex := -1
    for i, col := range header {
        if col == "URL" {
            urlIndex = i
            break
        }
    }
    
    if urlIndex == -1 {
        fmt.Printf("No URL column found in %s\n", filepath)
        return
    }
    
    // Store header in uniqueRows if not already present
    if len(uniqueRows) == 0 {
        uniqueRows["header"] = header
    }
    
    // Process each row
    for {
        row, err := reader.Read()
        if err == io.EOF {
            break
        }
        if err != nil {
            continue
        }
        
        if len(row) != len(header) {
            continue
        }
        
        url := row[urlIndex]
        // Check if URL matches either product pattern
        if productPattern.MatchString(url) || collectionProductPattern.MatchString(url) {
            key := strings.Join(row, "|")
            uniqueRows[key] = row
        }
    }
}

func writeOutput(outputFile string, uniqueRows map[string][]string) {
    file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
    if err != nil {
        fmt.Printf("Error creating output file: %v\n", err)
        return
    }
    defer file.Close()
    
    writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
    defer writer.Flush()
    
    // Write header first
    if header, ok := uniqueRows["header"]; ok {
        writer.Write(header)
        delete(uniqueRows, "header")
    }
    
    // Write data rows
    for _, row := range uniqueRows {
        writer.Write(row)
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("Successfully processed and wrote %d unique product URLs to %s\n", len(uniqueRows), outputFile)
}

🐛 Troubleshooting

Frontend doesn’t connect to API

  • Check backend is running on port 8080
  • Check API_BASE_URL in api.js
  • Check browser console for CORS errors

Components not rendering

  • Check all component files are loaded in index.html
  • Check browser console for JavaScript errors
  • Verify component names in app.js

Styling issues

  • Clear browser cache
  • Check Bootstrap CSS is loaded
  • Verify custom CSS path

package main

import ( “log” “net/http” “os”

"github.com/gorilla/mux"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/handlers"
collectionModels "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/models"
collectionRepo "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/repository"
collectionService "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/service"
productHandlers "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/handlers"
productModels "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/models"
productRepo "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/repository"
productService "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/service"
searchHandlers "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/handlers"
searchModels "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/models"
searchRepo "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/repository"
searchService "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/service"
siteHandlers "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/handlers"
siteModels "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/models"
siteRepo "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/repository"
siteService "github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/service"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/internal/config"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/internal/database"

)

func main() { // Load configuration cfg := config.Load()

// Ensure data directory exists
if err := os.MkdirAll("./data", 0755); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("Failed to create data directory:", err)
}

// Connect to database
if err := database.Connect(cfg.DatabasePath); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("Failed to connect to database:", err)
}

// Auto migrate all models
db := database.GetDB()
if err := db.AutoMigrate(
	&productModels.Product{},
	&productModels.Brand{},
	&siteModels.Site{},
	&collectionModels.Collection{},
	&collectionModels.CollectionItem{},
	&searchModels.Page{},
	&searchModels.Image{},
); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("Failed to migrate database:", err)
}

log.Println("Database migration completed successfully")

// Initialize repositories
productRepository := productRepo.NewProductRepository(db)
brandRepository := productRepo.NewBrandRepository(db)
siteRepository := siteRepo.NewSiteRepository(db)
collectionRepository := collectionRepo.NewCollectionRepository(db)
searchRepository := searchRepo.NewSearchRepository(db)
// Initialize services
productSvc := productService.NewProductService(productRepository, brandRepository)
siteSvc := siteService.NewSiteService(siteRepository)
collectionSvc := collectionService.NewCollectionService(collectionRepository)
searchSvc := searchService.NewSearchService(searchRepository)

// Initialize handlers
productHandler := productHandlers.NewProductHandler(productSvc)
siteHandler := siteHandlers.NewSiteHandler(siteSvc)
collectionHandler := handlers.NewCollectionHandler(collectionSvc)
searchHandler := searchHandlers.NewSearchHandler(searchSvc)

// Setup router
router := mux.NewRouter()

// CORS middleware
router.Use(func(next http.Handler) http.Handler {
	return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
		w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Methods", "GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS")
		w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Headers", "Content-Type, Authorization")

		if r.Method == "OPTIONS" {
			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
			return
		}

		next.ServeHTTP(w, r)
	})
})

// Register routes
productHandler.RegisterRoutes(router)
siteHandler.RegisterRoutes(router)
collectionHandler.RegisterRoutes(router)
searchHandler.RegisterRoutes(router)

// Health check endpoint
router.HandleFunc("/health", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
	w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
	w.Write([]byte(`{"status":"ok"}`))
}).Methods("GET")

// Root endpoint with API info
router.HandleFunc("/", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
	w.Write([]byte(`{
		"name": "Unified Search API",
		"version": "1.0.0",
		"features": [
			"Product Search Engine",
			"Site Directory",
			"Collections",
			"Web Search",
			"Crawler"
		],
		"endpoints": {
			"products": "/api/products",
			"brands": "/api/brands",
			"sites": "/api/sites",
			"collections": "/api/collections",
			"search": "/api/search",
			"crawler": "/api/crawler"
		}
	}`))
}).Methods("GET")

// Start server
serverAddr := ":" + cfg.ServerPort
log.Printf("Starting server on %s", serverAddr)
log.Printf("Environment: %s", cfg.Environment)
log.Printf("Database: %s", cfg.DatabasePath)
log.Println("API Documentation: http://localhost:" + cfg.ServerPort + "/")

if err := http.ListenAndServe(serverAddr, router); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("Server failed to start:", err)
}

}



### File: collection_handlers.go

package handlers

import ( “encoding/json” “net/http” “strconv”

"github.com/gorilla/mux"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/models"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/collections/service"

)

type CollectionHandler struct { service *service.CollectionService }

func NewCollectionHandler(service *service.CollectionService) *CollectionHandler { return &CollectionHandler{service: service} }

func (h *CollectionHandler) RegisterRoutes(router *mux.Router) { router.HandleFunc("/api/collections", h.GetAllCollections).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/public", h.GetPublicCollections).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/{id}", h.GetCollectionByID).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections", h.CreateCollection).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/{id}", h.UpdateCollection).Methods(“PUT”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/{id}", h.DeleteCollection).Methods(“DELETE”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/{id}/items", h.GetCollectionItems).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/{id}/items", h.AddItemToCollection).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/collections/items/{itemId}", h.RemoveItemFromCollection).Methods(“DELETE”) }

func (h *CollectionHandler) GetAllCollections(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { collections, err := h.service.GetAllCollections() if err != nil { http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError) return }

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(collections)

}

func (h *CollectionHandler) GetPublicCollections(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { collections, err := h.service.GetPublicCollections() if err != nil { http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError) return }

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")

package handlers

import ( “encoding/json” “net/http” “strconv”

"github.com/gorilla/mux"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/models"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/repository"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/service"

)

type ProductHandler struct { service *service.ProductService }

func NewProductHandler(service *service.ProductService) *ProductHandler { return &ProductHandler{service: service} }

func (h *ProductHandler) RegisterRoutes(router *mux.Router) { router.HandleFunc("/api/products", h.GetProducts).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/{id}", h.GetProductByID).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/slug/{slug}", h.GetProductBySlug).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products", h.CreateProduct).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/{id}", h.UpdateProduct).Methods(“PUT”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/{id}", h.DeleteProduct).Methods(“DELETE”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/{id}/related", h.GetRelatedProducts).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/products/filters/options", h.GetFilterOptions).Methods(“GET”)

// Brand routes
router.HandleFunc("/api/brands", h.GetAllBrands).Methods("GET")
router.HandleFunc("/api/brands/{name}", h.GetBrandByName).Methods("GET")
router.HandleFunc("/api/brands/{name}/categories", h.GetBrandCategories).Methods("GET")
router.HandleFunc("/api/brands", h.CreateBrand).Methods("POST")

}

func (h *ProductHandler) GetProducts(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { query := r.URL.Query()

page, _ := strconv.Atoi(query.Get("page"))
if page < 1 {
	page = 1
}

limit, _ := strconv.Atoi(query.Get("limit"))
if limit < 1 {
	limit = 50
}

filters := repository.ProductFilters{
	Search:       query.Get("search"),
	Category:     query.Get("category"),
	Subcategory:  query.Get("subcategory"),
	Brand:        query.Get("brand"),
	Country:      query.Get("country"),
	Collection:   query.Get("collection"),
	Availability: query.Get("availability"),
}

if minPrice := query.Get("min_price"); minPrice != "" {
	if val, err := strconv.ParseFloat(minPrice, 64); err == nil {
		filters.MinPrice = &val
	}
}

if maxPrice := query.Get("max_price"); maxPrice != "" {
	if val, err := strconv.ParseFloat(maxPrice, 64); err == nil {
		filters.MaxPrice = &val
	}
}

if featured := query.Get("featured"); featured != "" {
	val := featured == "true"
	filters.IsFeatured = &val
}

products, total, err := h.service.GetProducts(filters, page, limit)
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

response := map[string]interface{}{
	"data":  products,
	"total": total,
	"page":  page,
	"limit": limit,
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)

}

func (h *ProductHandler) GetProductByID(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid product ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

product, err := h.service.GetProductByID(uint(id))
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, "Product not found", http.StatusNotFound)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(product)

}

### File: product_repository.go

package repository

import ( “fmt”

"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/models"
"gorm.io/gorm"

)

type ProductRepository struct { db *gorm.DB }

func NewProductRepository(db *gorm.DB) *ProductRepository { return &ProductRepository{db: db} }

type ProductFilters struct { Search string Category string Subcategory string Brand string Country string Collection string MinPrice *float64 MaxPrice *float64 Availability string IsFeatured *bool Tags []string }

func (r *ProductRepository) GetProducts(filters ProductFilters, page, limit int) ([]models.Product, int64, error) { var products []models.Product var total int64

query := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Where("is_active = ?", true)

// Apply filters
if filters.Search != "" {
	query = query.Where("title LIKE ? OR description LIKE ? OR brand LIKE ?",
		"%"+filters.Search+"%", "%"+filters.Search+"%", "%"+filters.Search+"%")
}
if filters.Category != "" {
	query = query.Where("category = ?", filters.Category)
}
if filters.Subcategory != "" {
	query = query.Where("subcategory = ?", filters.Subcategory)
}
if filters.Brand != "" {
	query = query.Where("brand = ?", filters.Brand)
}
if filters.Country != "" {
	query = query.Where("country = ?", filters.Country)
}
if filters.Collection != "" {
	query = query.Where("collection = ?", filters.Collection)
}
if filters.MinPrice != nil {
	query = query.Where("price >= ?", *filters.MinPrice)
}
if filters.MaxPrice != nil {
	query = query.Where("price <= ?", *filters.MaxPrice)
}
if filters.Availability != "" {
	query = query.Where("availability = ?", filters.Availability)
}
if filters.IsFeatured != nil {
	query = query.Where("is_featured = ?", *filters.IsFeatured)
}

// Count total
if err := query.Count(&total).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

// Get paginated results
offset := (page - 1) * limit
if err := query.Offset(offset).Limit(limit).Order("created_at DESC").Find(&products).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

return products, total, nil

}

func (r *ProductRepository) GetProductByID(id uint) (*models.Product, error) { var product models.Product if err := r.db.First(&product, id).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &product, nil }

func (r *ProductRepository) GetProductBySlug(slug string) (*models.Product, error) { var product models.Product if err := r.db.Where(“slug = ?”, slug).First(&product).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &product, nil }

func (r *ProductRepository) GetProductBySKU(sku string) (*models.Product, error) { var product models.Product if err := r.db.Where(“sku = ?”, sku).First(&product).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &product, nil }

func (r *ProductRepository) CreateProduct(product *models.Product) error { return r.db.Create(product).Error }

func (r *ProductRepository) UpdateProduct(product *models.Product) error { return r.db.Save(product).Error }

func (r *ProductRepository) DeleteProduct(id uint) error { return r.db.Delete(&models.Product{}, id).Error }

func (r *ProductRepository) GetRelatedProducts(productID uint, category, brand string, limit int) ([]models.Product, error) { var products []models.Product query := r.db.Where(“is_active = ? AND id != ?”, true, productID)

if category != "" && brand != "" {
	query = query.Where("(category = ? OR brand = ?)", category, brand)
} else if category != "" {
	query = query.Where("category = ?", category)
} else if brand != "" {
	query = query.Where("brand = ?", brand)
}

if err := query.Limit(limit).Order("RANDOM()").Find(&products).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, err
}
return products, nil

}

func (r *ProductRepository) GetFilterOptions() (map[string]interface{}, error) { options := make(map[string]interface{})

var categories []string
if err := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Distinct("category").Where("is_active = ? AND category != ''", true).Pluck("category", &categories).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get categories: %w", err)
}
options["categories"] = categories

var brands []string
if err := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Distinct("brand").Where("is_active = ? AND brand != ''", true).Pluck("brand", &brands).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get brands: %w", err)
}
options["brands"] = brands

var countries []string
if err := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Distinct("country").Where("is_active = ? AND country != ''", true).Pluck("country", &countries).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get countries: %w", err)
}
options["countries"] = countries

var collections []string
if err := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Distinct("collection").Where("is_active = ? AND collection != ''", true).Pluck("collection", &collections).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get collections: %w", err)
}
options["collections"] = collections

return options, nil

}

func (r *ProductRepository) GetTotalCount() (int64, error) { var count int64 if err := r.db.Model(&models.Product{}).Where(“is_active = ?”, true).Count(&count).Error; err != nil { return 0, err } return count, nil }



### File: product_service.go

package service

import ( “github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/models” “github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/products/repository” )

type ProductService struct { productRepo *repository.ProductRepository brandRepo *repository.BrandRepository }

### File: search_handlers.go

package handlers

import ( “encoding/json” “net/http” “strconv”

"github.com/gorilla/mux"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/models"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/service"

)

type SearchHandler struct { service *service.SearchService }

func NewSearchHandler(service *service.SearchService) *SearchHandler { return &SearchHandler{service: service} }

func (h *SearchHandler) RegisterRoutes(router *mux.Router) { router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages", h.SearchPages).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images", h.SearchImages).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages/{id}", h.GetPageByID).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}", h.GetImageByID).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages", h.CreatePage).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images", h.CreateImage).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages/{id}", h.UpdatePage).Methods(“PUT”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}", h.UpdateImage).Methods(“PUT”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages/{id}", h.DeletePage).Methods(“DELETE”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}", h.DeleteImage).Methods(“DELETE”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages/{id}/click", h.IncrementPageClicks).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}/click", h.IncrementImageClicks).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/pages/{id}/vote", h.VotePage).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}/vote", h.VoteImage).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/search/images/{id}/broken", h.MarkImageBroken).Methods(“POST”) }

func (h *SearchHandler) SearchPages(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { query := r.URL.Query().Get(“q”)

page, _ := strconv.Atoi(r.URL.Query().Get("page"))
if page < 1 {
	page = 1
}

limit, _ := strconv.Atoi(r.URL.Query().Get("limit"))
if limit < 1 {
	limit = 20
}

pages, total, err := h.service.SearchPages(query, page, limit)
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

response := map[string]interface{}{
	"data":  pages,
	"total": total,
	"page":  page,
	"limit": limit,
	"query": query,
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)

}

func (h *SearchHandler) SearchImages(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { query := r.URL.Query().Get(“q”)

page, _ := strconv.Atoi(r.URL.Query().Get("page"))
if page < 1 {
	page = 1
}

limit, _ := strconv.Atoi(r.URL.Query().Get("limit"))
if limit < 1 {
	limit = 20
}

images, total, err := h.service.SearchImages(query, page, limit)
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

response := map[string]interface{}{
	"data":  images,
	"total": total,
	"page":  page,
	"limit": limit,
	"query": query,
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)

}

func (h *SearchHandler) GetPageByID(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid page ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

page, err := h.service.GetPageByID(uint(id))
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, "Page not found", http.StatusNotFound)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(page)

}

func (h *SearchHandler) GetImageByID(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid image ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

image, err := h.service.GetImageByID(uint(id))
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, "Image not found", http.StatusNotFound)

}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")

if err := h.service.CreatePage(&page); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
w.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(page)

}

package models

import ( “time” )

type Page struct { ID uint gorm:"primaryKey" json:"id" Title string gorm:"size:512;not null" json:"title" URL string gorm:"size:1024;not null;uniqueIndex" json:"url" Description string gorm:"type:text" json:"description" Content string gorm:"type:text" json:"content" VoteCount int gorm:"default:0" json:"vote_count" Clicks int gorm:"default:0" json:"clicks" CreatedAt time.Time json:"created_at" }

type Image struct { ID uint gorm:"primaryKey" json:"id" Title string gorm:"size:512;not null" json:"title" URL string gorm:"size:1024;not null" json:"url" ImageURL string gorm:"size:1024;not null;uniqueIndex" json:"image_url" Description string gorm:"type:text" json:"description" AltText string gorm:"size:512" json:"alt_text" Width int gorm:"default:0" json:"width" Height int gorm:"default:0" json:"height" VoteCount int gorm:"default:0" json:"vote_count" Broken bool gorm:"default:false" json:"broken" Clicks int gorm:"default:0" json:"clicks" CreatedAt time.Time json:"created_at" }



### File: search_repository.go

package repository

import ( “github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/search/models” “gorm.io/gorm” )

type SearchRepository struct { db *gorm.DB }

func NewSearchRepository(db *gorm.DB) *SearchRepository { return &SearchRepository{db: db} }

func (r *SearchRepository) SearchPages(query string, page, limit int) ([]models.Page, int64, error) { var pages []models.Page var total int64

dbQuery := r.db.Model(&models.Page{})

if query != "" {
	dbQuery = dbQuery.Where("title LIKE ? OR description LIKE ? OR content LIKE ?",
		"%"+query+"%", "%"+query+"%", "%"+query+"%")
}

// Count total
if err := dbQuery.Count(&total).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

// Get paginated results with ranking
offset := (page - 1) * limit
if err := dbQuery.Order("vote_count DESC, clicks DESC, created_at DESC").
	Offset(offset).Limit(limit).Find(&pages).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

return pages, total, nil

}

func (r *SearchRepository) SearchImages(query string, page, limit int) ([]models.Image, int64, error) { var images []models.Image var total int64

dbQuery := r.db.Model(&models.Image{}).Where("broken = ?", false)

if query != "" {
	dbQuery = dbQuery.Where("title LIKE ? OR description LIKE ? OR alt_text LIKE ?",
		"%"+query+"%", "%"+query+"%", "%"+query+"%")
}

// Count total
if err := dbQuery.Count(&total).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

// Get paginated results with ranking
offset := (page - 1) * limit
if err := dbQuery.Order("vote_count DESC, clicks DESC, created_at DESC").
	Offset(offset).Limit(limit).Find(&images).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

return images, total, nil

}

func (r *SearchRepository) GetPageByID(id uint) (*models.Page, error) { var page models.Page if err := r.db.First(&page, id).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &page, nil }

func (r *SearchRepository) GetImageByID(id uint) (*models.Image, error) { var image models.Image if err := r.db.First(&image, id).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &image, nil }

func (r *SearchRepository) CreatePage(page *models.Page) error { return r.db.Create(page).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) CreateImage(image *models.Image) error { return r.db.Create(image).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) UpdatePage(page *models.Page) error { return r.db.Save(page).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) UpdateImage(image *models.Image) error { return r.db.Save(image).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) DeletePage(id uint) error { return r.db.Delete(&models.Page{}, id).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) DeleteImage(id uint) error { return r.db.Delete(&models.Image{}, id).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) IncrementPageClicks(pageID uint) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Page{}).Where(“id = ?”, pageID).UpdateColumn(“clicks”, gorm.Expr(“clicks + ?”, 1)).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) IncrementImageClicks(imageID uint) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Image{}).Where(“id = ?”, imageID).UpdateColumn(“clicks”, gorm.Expr(“clicks + ?”, 1)).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) VotePage(pageID uint, voteType int) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Page{}).Where(“id = ?”, pageID). UpdateColumn(“vote_count”, gorm.Expr(“vote_count + ?”, voteType)).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) VoteImage(imageID uint, voteType int) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Image{}).Where(“id = ?”, imageID). UpdateColumn(“vote_count”, gorm.Expr(“vote_count + ?”, voteType)).Error }

func (r *SearchRepository) MarkImageBroken(imageID uint) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Image{}).Where(“id = ?”, imageID).Update(“broken”, true).Error }
