### File: site_handlers.go

package handlers

import ( “encoding/json” “net/http” “strconv”

"github.com/gorilla/mux"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/models"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/repository"
"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/service"

)

type SiteHandler struct { service *service.SiteService }

func NewSiteHandler(service *service.SiteService) *SiteHandler { return &SiteHandler{service: service} }

func (h *SiteHandler) RegisterRoutes(router *mux.Router) { router.HandleFunc("/api/sites", h.GetSites).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/{id}", h.GetSiteByID).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites", h.CreateSite).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/{id}", h.UpdateSite).Methods(“PUT”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/{id}", h.DeleteSite).Methods(“DELETE”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/{id}/vote", h.VoteSite).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/{id}/click", h.IncrementClicks).Methods(“POST”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/categories", h.GetAllCategories).Methods(“GET”) router.HandleFunc("/api/sites/tags", h.GetAllTags).Methods(“GET”) }

func (h *SiteHandler) GetSites(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { query := r.URL.Query()

page, _ := strconv.Atoi(query.Get("page"))
if page < 1 {
	page = 1
}

limit, _ := strconv.Atoi(query.Get("limit"))
if limit < 1 {
	limit = 50
}

filters := repository.SiteFilters{
	Search:   query.Get("search"),
	Category: query.Get("category"),
	Tag:      query.Get("tag"),
	OrderBy:  query.Get("order_by"), // popular, recent, random
}

sites, total, err := h.service.GetSites(filters, page, limit)
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

response := map[string]interface{}{
	"data":  sites,
	"total": total,
	"page":  page,
	"limit": limit,
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(response)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) GetSiteByID(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid site ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

site, err := h.service.GetSiteByID(uint(id))
if err != nil {
	http.Error(w, "Site not found", http.StatusNotFound)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(site)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) CreateSite(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { var site models.Site if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&site); err != nil { http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest) return }

if err := h.service.CreateSite(&site); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
w.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(site)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) UpdateSite(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid site ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

var site models.Site
if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&site); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
	return
}

site.ID = uint(id)
if err := h.service.UpdateSite(&site); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(site)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) DeleteSite(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid site ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

if err := h.service.DeleteSite(uint(id)); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) VoteSite(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid site ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

var req struct {
	VoteType int `json:"vote_type"` // 1 for upvote, -1 for downvote
}
if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
	return
}

if err := h.service.VoteSite(uint(id), req.VoteType); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{"message": "Vote recorded"})

}

func (h *SiteHandler) IncrementClicks(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { vars := mux.Vars(r) id, err := strconv.ParseUint(vars[“id”], 10, 32) if err != nil { http.Error(w, “Invalid site ID”, http.StatusBadRequest) return }

if err := h.service.IncrementClicks(uint(id)); err != nil {
	http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
	return
}

w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{"message": "Click recorded"})

}

func (h *SiteHandler) GetAllCategories(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { categories, err := h.service.GetAllCategories() if err != nil { http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError) return }

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(categories)

}

func (h *SiteHandler) GetAllTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) { tags, err := h.service.GetAllTags() if err != nil { http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError) return }

w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(tags)

}

package models

import ( “time” )

type Site struct { ID uint gorm:"primaryKey" json:"id" Title string gorm:"size:512;not null" json:"title" URL string gorm:"size:1024;not null" json:"url" Description string gorm:"type:text" json:"description" Category string gorm:"size:100;index" json:"category" Tags string gorm:"type:text" json:"tags" // comma-separated Logo string gorm:"size:1024;default:'default-logo.png'" json:"logo" Upvotes int gorm:"default:0" json:"upvotes" Downvotes int gorm:"default:0" json:"downvotes" Clicks int gorm:"default:0" json:"clicks" CreatedAt time.Time json:"created_at" }



### File: site_repository.go

package repository

import ( “strings”

"github.com/yourusername/unified-search-api/features/sites/models"
"gorm.io/gorm"

)

type SiteRepository struct { db *gorm.DB }

func NewSiteRepository(db *gorm.DB) *SiteRepository { return &SiteRepository{db: db} }

type SiteFilters struct { Search string Category string Tag string OrderBy string // popular, recent, random }

func (r *SiteRepository) GetSites(filters SiteFilters, page, limit int) ([]models.Site, int64, error) { var sites []models.Site var total int64

query := r.db.Model(&models.Site{})

// Apply filters
if filters.Search != "" {
	query = query.Where("title LIKE ? OR description LIKE ? OR url LIKE ?",
		"%"+filters.Search+"%", "%"+filters.Search+"%", "%"+filters.Search+"%")
}
if filters.Category != "" {
	query = query.Where("category = ?", filters.Category)
}
if filters.Tag != "" {
	query = query.Where("tags LIKE ?", "%"+filters.Tag+"%")
}

// Count total
if err := query.Count(&total).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

// Apply ordering
switch filters.OrderBy {
case "popular":
	query = query.Order("(upvotes - downvotes) DESC, clicks DESC")
case "random":
	query = query.Order("RANDOM()")
default: // recent
	query = query.Order("created_at DESC")
}

// Get paginated results
offset := (page - 1) * limit
if err := query.Offset(offset).Limit(limit).Find(&sites).Error; err != nil {
	return nil, 0, err
}

return sites, total, nil

}

func (r *SiteRepository) GetSiteByID(id uint) (*models.Site, error) { var site models.Site if err := r.db.First(&site, id).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return &site, nil }

func (r *SiteRepository) CreateSite(site *models.Site) error { return r.db.Create(site).Error }

func (r *SiteRepository) UpdateSite(site *models.Site) error { return r.db.Save(site).Error }

func (r *SiteRepository) DeleteSite(id uint) error { return r.db.Delete(&models.Site{}, id).Error }

func (r *SiteRepository) VoteSite(siteID uint, voteType int) error { site, err := r.GetSiteByID(siteID) if err != nil { return err }

if voteType > 0 {
	site.Upvotes++
} else {
	site.Downvotes++
}

return r.UpdateSite(site)

}

func (r *SiteRepository) IncrementClicks(siteID uint) error { return r.db.Model(&models.Site{}).Where(“id = ?”, siteID).UpdateColumn(“clicks”, gorm.Expr(“clicks + ?”, 1)).Error }

func (r *SiteRepository) GetAllCategories() ([]string, error) { var categories []string if err := r.db.Model(&models.Site{}). Distinct(“category”). Where(“category != ‘’”). Pluck(“category”, &categories).Error; err != nil { return nil, err } return categories, nil }

func (r *SiteRepository) GetAllTags() ([]string, error) { var sites []models.Site if err := r.db.Select(“tags”).Find(&sites).Error; err != nil { return nil, err }

tagMap := make(map[string]bool)
for _, site := range sites {
	if site.Tags != "" {
		tags := strings.Split(site.Tags, ",")
		for _, tag := range tags {
			trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(tag)
			if trimmed != "" {
				tagMap[trimmed] = true
			}
		}
	}
}

tags := make([]string, 0, len(tagMap))
for tag := range tagMap {
	tags = append(tags, tag)
}

return tags, nil

}

### File: config.go

package config

import ( “os” )

type Config struct { DatabasePath string ServerPort string Environment string }

func Load() *Config { return &Config{ DatabasePath: getEnv(“DATABASE_PATH”, “./data/unified.db”), ServerPort: getEnv(“SERVER_PORT”, “8080”), Environment: getEnv(“ENVIRONMENT”, “development”), } }

func getEnv(key, defaultValue string) string { if value := os.Getenv(key); value != "" { return value } return defaultValue }

package database

import ( “log”

"gorm.io/driver/sqlite"
"gorm.io/gorm"
"gorm.io/gorm/logger"

)

var DB *gorm.DB

func Connect(databasePath string) error { var err error

DB, err = gorm.Open(sqlite.Open(databasePath), &gorm.Config{
	Logger: logger.Default.LogMode(logger.Info),
})

if err != nil {
	return err
}

log.Println("Database connected successfully")
return nil

}

func GetDB() *gorm.DB { return DB }

func AutoMigrate(models …interface{}) error { return DB.AutoMigrate(models…) }

package main

import ( “context” “database/sql” “encoding/csv” “encoding/json” “fmt” “log” “net/url” “os” “path/filepath” “strings” “sync” “sync/atomic” “time”

"github.com/gocolly/colly"
_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"

)

var STARTURL string

type Config struct { CrawlerName string json:"crawler_name" DatabaseName string json:"database_name" // “data.csv” for CSV or “data.db” for SQLite MaxDepth int json:"max_depth" WritePath string json:"write_path" Async bool json:"async" Parallelism int json:"parallelism" DelayMS int json:"delay_ms" RandomDelayMS int json:"random_delay_ms" BatchSize int json:"batch_size" UserAgent string json:"user_agent" TimeoutMinutes int json:"timeout_minutes" // New performance settings MaxOpenConns int json:"max_open_conns" MaxIdleConns int json:"max_idle_conns" WriteBufferSize int json:"write_buffer_size" }

func generateDefaultConfig() error { config := Config{ CrawlerName: “web_crawler”, DatabaseName: “data.csv”, // Use “data.db” for SQLite, “data.csv” for CSV MaxDepth: 10, WritePath: “data/urls”, Async: true, Parallelism: 4, DelayMS: 500, RandomDelayMS: 500, BatchSize: 200, UserAgent: “Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36”, TimeoutMinutes: 5, MaxOpenConns: 20, MaxIdleConns: 10, WriteBufferSize: 1000, }

data, err := json.MarshalIndent(config, "", "  ")
if err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to marshal config: %w", err)
}

return os.WriteFile("crawlerconfig.json", data, 0644)

}

type URLData struct { URL string TimeStamp time.Time SiteName string }

// Performance monitoring type CrawlStats struct { URLsProcessed int64 URLsWritten int64 ErrorCount int64 StartTime time.Time mu sync.RWMutex errors []string }

func NewCrawlStats() *CrawlStats { return &CrawlStats{ StartTime: time.Now(), errors: make([]string, 0), } }

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementProcessed() { atomic.AddInt64(&cs.URLsProcessed, 1) }

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementWritten() { atomic.AddInt64(&cs.URLsWritten, 1) }

func (cs *CrawlStats) IncrementErrors() { atomic.AddInt64(&cs.ErrorCount, 1) }

func (cs *CrawlStats) AddError(err string) { cs.mu.Lock() defer cs.mu.Unlock() cs.errors = append(cs.errors, fmt.Sprintf("[%s] %s", time.Now().Format(“15:04:05”), err)) if len(cs.errors) > 100 { // Keep only last 100 errors cs.errors = cs.errors[1:] } }

func (cs *CrawlStats) GetStats() (int64, int64, int64, time.Duration, []string) { cs.mu.RLock() defer cs.mu.RUnlock() return atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.URLsProcessed), atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.URLsWritten), atomic.LoadInt64(&cs.ErrorCount), time.Since(cs.StartTime), append([]string{}, cs.errors…) }

func (cs *CrawlStats) PrintStats() { processed, written, errorCount, duration, errors := cs.GetStats() log.Printf("=== CRAWL STATISTICS ===") log.Printf(“URLs Processed: %d”, processed) log.Printf(“URLs Written: %d”, written) log.Printf(“Error Count: %d”, errorCount) log.Printf(“Duration: %v”, duration.Truncate(time.Second)) if processed > 0 { log.Printf(“Processing Rate: %.2f URLs/second”, float64(processed)/duration.Seconds()) } if len(errors) > 0 { log.Printf(“Recent Errors:”) for i, err := range errors { if i >= 10 { // Show only last 10 errors log.Printf("… and %d more errors", len(errors)-10) break } log.Printf(" %s", err) } } log.Printf("========================") }

// Enhanced BatchWriter with better error handling type BatchWriter struct { results []URLData batchSize int mu sync.Mutex fileCounter int baseDir string siteName string stats *CrawlStats }

// List of non-HTML extensions (expand as needed) var blockedExtensions = []string{".jpg", “.jpeg”, “.png”, “.gif”, “.webp”, “.bmp”, “.svg”, “.ico”, “.css”, “.js”, “.json”, “.pdf”, “.mp4”, “.avi”, “.mov”, “.zip”, “.rar”, “.woff”, “.ttf”}

// List of path segments or patterns typical to asset CDNs var blockedPathPatterns = []string{ “/image/upload/”, “/images/”, “/static/”, “/assets/”, “/media/”, “/fonts/”, “/js/”, “/css/”, }

// List of blocked host substrings (expand as needed) var blockedHostKeywords = []string{ “cdn.”, “assets.”, “media.”, }

// Returns true if the URL is likely to be an asset, NOT an HTML page. func isAssetURL(u string) bool { parsed, err := url.Parse(u) if err != nil { return false // If we can’t parse, let other logic handle it. }

urlLower := strings.ToLower(u)
// Extension block
for _, ext := range blockedExtensions {
	if strings.HasSuffix(urlLower, ext) {
		return true
	}
}
// Path pattern block
for _, pattern := range blockedPathPatterns {
	if strings.Contains(parsed.Path, pattern) {
		return true
	}
}
// Host block
hostLower := strings.ToLower(parsed.Hostname())
for _, kw := range blockedHostKeywords {
	if strings.Contains(hostLower, kw) {
		return true
	}
}
return false

}

// Helper to check if a URL has a blocked extension func hasBlockedExtension(u string) bool { lower := strings.ToLower(u) for _, ext := range blockedExtensions { if strings.HasSuffix(lower, ext) { return true } } return false }

func NewBatchWriter(siteName string, config *Config, stats *CrawlStats) (*BatchWriter, error) { timestamp := time.Now().Format(“20060102_150405”) baseDir := filepath.Join(config.WritePath, config.CrawlerName, siteName, fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s", siteName, timestamp))

if err := os.MkdirAll(baseDir, 0755); err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to create directory %s: %w", baseDir, err)
}

return &BatchWriter{
	results:   make([]URLData, 0, config.BatchSize),
	batchSize: config.BatchSize,
	baseDir:   baseDir,
	siteName:  siteName,
	stats:     stats,
}, nil

}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Add(data URLData) { bw.mu.Lock() defer bw.mu.Unlock() bw.results = append(bw.results, data) bw.stats.IncrementProcessed() if len(bw.results) >= bw.batchSize { bw.writeBatch() } }

func (bw *BatchWriter) writeBatch() { if len(bw.results) == 0 { return }

filename := fmt.Sprintf("%s/batch%d.csv", bw.baseDir, bw.fileCounter)
log.Printf("Writing batch %d with %d URLs", bw.fileCounter, len(bw.results))

if err := writeToCSV(filename, bw.results); err != nil {
	errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Error writing CSV batch %d: %v", bw.fileCounter, err)
	log.Printf(errMsg)
	bw.stats.AddError(errMsg)
	bw.stats.IncrementErrors()
	return
}

bw.stats.IncrementWritten()
bw.fileCounter++
bw.results = make([]URLData, 0, bw.batchSize)

}

func (bw *BatchWriter) Flush() { bw.mu.Lock() defer bw.mu.Unlock() bw.writeBatch() }

func (bw *BatchWriter) Close() error { bw.Flush() return nil }

// Enhanced AsyncSQLiteWriter with channels and goroutines type AsyncSQLiteWriter struct { db *sql.DB ctx context.Context cancel context.CancelFunc dataChan chan URLData flushChan chan chan struct{} closeChan chan chan error wg sync.WaitGroup batchSize int siteName string tableName string stats *CrawlStats writeBuffer []URLData bufferMu sync.Mutex }

func NewAsyncSQLiteWriter(siteName string, config *Config, stats *CrawlStats) (*AsyncSQLiteWriter, error) { dbDir := filepath.Join(config.WritePath, config.CrawlerName) if err := os.MkdirAll(dbDir, 0755); err != nil { return nil, fmt.Errorf(“failed to create directory %s: %w”, dbDir, err) }

dbFileName := strings.TrimSuffix(config.DatabaseName, ".db")
dbPath := filepath.Join(dbDir, fmt.Sprintf("%s.db", dbFileName))

// Enhanced SQLite connection string with performance optimizations
dsn := fmt.Sprintf("%s?_journal_mode=WAL&_synchronous=NORMAL&_cache_size=100000&_temp_store=memory&_mmap_size=268435456", dbPath)
db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dsn)
if err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to open database: %w", err)
}

// Enhanced connection pool settings
db.SetMaxOpenConns(config.MaxOpenConns)
db.SetMaxIdleConns(config.MaxIdleConns)
db.SetConnMaxLifetime(time.Hour)

// Test connection
if err := db.Ping(); err != nil {
	db.Close()
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to ping database: %w", err)
}

ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())

tableName := fmt.Sprintf("urls_%s", strings.ReplaceAll(config.CrawlerName, "-", "_"))

writer := &AsyncSQLiteWriter{
	db:          db,
	ctx:         ctx,
	cancel:      cancel,
	dataChan:    make(chan URLData, config.WriteBufferSize),
	flushChan:   make(chan chan struct{}, 1),
	closeChan:   make(chan chan error, 1),
	batchSize:   config.BatchSize,
	siteName:    siteName,
	tableName:   tableName,
	stats:       stats,
	writeBuffer: make([]URLData, 0, config.BatchSize),
}

// Create table and indexes
if err := writer.initializeDatabase(); err != nil {
	writer.Close()
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize database: %w", err)
}

// Start async writer goroutine
writer.wg.Add(1)
go writer.writeWorker()

return writer, nil

}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) initializeDatabase() error { // Create table with better schema createTableSQL := fmt.Sprintf(CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS %s ( id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, url TEXT NOT NULL, timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL, site_name TEXT NOT NULL, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, UNIQUE(url) );, asw.tableName)

if _, err := asw.db.ExecContext(asw.ctx, createTableSQL); err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to create table: %w", err)
}

// Create performance indexes
indexes := []string{
	fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_url ON %s(url);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
	fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_site_name ON %s(site_name);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
	fmt.Sprintf("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_%s_timestamp ON %s(timestamp);", asw.tableName, asw.tableName),
}

for _, indexSQL := range indexes {
	if _, err := asw.db.ExecContext(asw.ctx, indexSQL); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Warning: Failed to create index: %v", err)
	}
}

// Optimize SQLite settings
optimizations := []string{
	"PRAGMA optimize;",
	"PRAGMA analysis_limit=1000;",
	"PRAGMA cache_size=100000;",
}

for _, pragma := range optimizations {
	if _, err := asw.db.ExecContext(asw.ctx, pragma); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Warning: Failed to execute pragma %s: %v", pragma, err)
	}
}

return nil

}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) writeWorker() { defer asw.wg.Done() ticker := time.NewTicker(5 * time.Second) // Periodic flush defer ticker.Stop()

for {
	select {
	case <-asw.ctx.Done():
		asw.flushBuffer()
		return

	case data := <-asw.dataChan:
		asw.bufferMu.Lock()
		asw.writeBuffer = append(asw.writeBuffer, data)
		shouldFlush := len(asw.writeBuffer) >= asw.batchSize
		asw.bufferMu.Unlock()

		if shouldFlush {
			asw.flushBuffer()
		}

	case respChan := <-asw.flushChan:
		asw.flushBuffer()
		respChan <- struct{}{}

	case respChan := <-asw.closeChan:
		asw.flushBuffer()
		respChan <- nil
		return

	case <-ticker.C:
		asw.bufferMu.Lock()
		hasData := len(asw.writeBuffer) > 0
		asw.bufferMu.Unlock()
		if hasData {
			asw.flushBuffer()
		}
	}
}

}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) flushBuffer() { asw.bufferMu.Lock() if len(asw.writeBuffer) == 0 { asw.bufferMu.Unlock() return }

batch := make([]URLData, len(asw.writeBuffer))
copy(batch, asw.writeBuffer)
asw.writeBuffer = asw.writeBuffer[:0]
asw.bufferMu.Unlock()

if err := asw.writeBatch(batch); err != nil {
	errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Failed to write batch to SQLite: %v", err)
	log.Printf(errMsg)
	asw.stats.AddError(errMsg)
	asw.stats.IncrementErrors()
	return
}

asw.stats.IncrementWritten()
log.Printf("Wrote batch of %d URLs to SQLite (Total processed: %d)",
	len(batch), atomic.LoadInt64(&asw.stats.URLsProcessed))

}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) writeBatch(batch []URLData) error { if len(batch) == 0 { return nil }

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(asw.ctx, 30*time.Second)
defer cancel()

tx, err := asw.db.BeginTx(ctx, &sql.TxOptions{
	Isolation: sql.LevelReadCommitted,
})
if err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to begin transaction: %w", err)
}

insertSQL := fmt.Sprintf("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO %s (url, timestamp, site_name) VALUES (?, ?, ?)", asw.tableName)
stmt, err := tx.PrepareContext(ctx, insertSQL)
if err != nil {
	tx.Rollback()
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to prepare statement: %w", err)
}
defer stmt.Close()

for _, data := range batch {
	if _, err := stmt.ExecContext(ctx, data.URL, data.TimeStamp, data.SiteName); err != nil {
		log.Printf("Warning: Failed to insert URL %s: %v", data.URL, err)
	}
}

if err := tx.Commit(); err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to commit transaction: %w", err)
}

return nil

}

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Add(data URLData) { asw.stats.IncrementProcessed() select { case asw.dataChan <- data: // Successfully queued case <-asw.ctx.Done(): // Context cancelled, skip default: // Channel full, try to write anyway but log warning log.Printf(“Warning: Write buffer full, may be blocking”) select { case asw.dataChan <- data: case <-asw.ctx.Done(): } } }

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Flush() { respChan := make(chan struct{}) select { case asw.flushChan <- respChan: <-respChan case <-time.After(10 * time.Second): log.Printf(“Warning: Flush timeout”) } }

func (asw *AsyncSQLiteWriter) Close() error { asw.cancel()

respChan := make(chan error)
select {
case asw.closeChan <- respChan:
	err := <-respChan
	asw.wg.Wait()
	asw.db.Close()
	return err
case <-time.After(30 * time.Second):
	log.Printf("Warning: Close timeout, forcing shutdown")
	asw.wg.Wait()
	return asw.db.Close()
}

}

type Writer interface { Add(URLData) Flush() Close() error }

func printHelp() { fmt.Printf(“Usage: %s <config.json> \n”, os.Args[0]) fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Example:”) fmt.Println(" go run main.go news_crawler.json bbc.com") fmt.Println(" go run main.go ecommerce_crawler.json https://nyandcompany.com") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Description:”) fmt.Println(" This tool crawls all links from the given domain and saves them.") fmt.Println(" Output format is determined by ‘database_name’ field in config:") fmt.Println(" - *.db files = SQLite database") fmt.Println(" - *.csv files = CSV format") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Options:”) fmt.Println(" -h, –help Show this help message") fmt.Println(" –generate-config Generate a default crawlerconfig.json") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Config Examples:”) fmt.Println(" For CSV: "database_name": "news_data.csv"") fmt.Println(" For SQLite: "database_name": "news_data.db"") fmt.Println("") }

func main() { if len(os.Args) < 2 { fmt.Printf(“Usage: %s <config.json> \n”, os.Args[0]) os.Exit(1) }

// Handle flags first
if os.Args[1] == "--help" || os.Args[1] == "-h" {
	printHelp()
	os.Exit(0)
}

if os.Args[1] == "--generate-config" {
	if err := generateDefaultConfig(); err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error generating config: %v\n", err)
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	fmt.Println("Default crawlerconfig.json generated successfully.")
	fmt.Println("Edit 'database_name' field:")
	fmt.Println("  - Use 'data.csv' for CSV output")
	fmt.Println("  - Use 'data.db' for SQLite output")
	os.Exit(0)
}

// Now require two arguments for normal operation
if len(os.Args) < 3 {
	fmt.Printf("Usage: %s <config.json> <domain>\n", os.Args[0])
	os.Exit(1)
}

// Load config
configFile := os.Args[1]
config, err := loadConfig(configFile)
if err != nil {
	log.Fatalf("Failed to load config: %v", err)
}

// Validate and set defaults for new config fields
if config.MaxOpenConns <= 0 {
	config.MaxOpenConns = 20
}
if config.MaxIdleConns <= 0 {
	config.MaxIdleConns = 10
}
if config.WriteBufferSize <= 0 {
	config.WriteBufferSize = 1000
}

// Validate required config fields
if config.CrawlerName == "" {
	log.Fatalf("crawler_name is required in config")
}
if config.DatabaseName == "" {
	log.Fatalf("database_name is required in config")
}

// Normalize URL
rawInput := os.Args[2]
if !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "http://") && !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "https://") {
	rawInput = "https://" + rawInput
}

parsed, err := url.Parse(rawInput)
if err != nil {
	log.Fatalf("Invalid domain: %v", err)
}

STARTURL = strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")

// Initialize statistics
stats := NewCrawlStats()

// Create collector from config
c := colly.NewCollector(
	colly.MaxDepth(config.MaxDepth),
	colly.Async(config.Async),
	colly.IgnoreRobotsTxt(),
	colly.UserAgent(config.UserAgent),
)

if err := c.Limit(&colly.LimitRule{
	DomainGlob:  "*",
	Parallelism: config.Parallelism,
	Delay:       time.Duration(config.DelayMS) * time.Millisecond,
	RandomDelay: time.Duration(config.RandomDelayMS) * time.Millisecond,
}); err != nil {
	log.Fatalf("Error setting rate limit: %v", err)
}

siteName := strings.Split(STARTURL, ".")[0]

// Choose writer based on database_name extension
var writer Writer
if isSQLiteDatabase(config.DatabaseName) {
	sqliteWriter, err := NewAsyncSQLiteWriter(siteName, config, stats)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create async SQLite writer: %v", err)
	}
	writer = sqliteWriter
	log.Printf("Using Async SQLite database for storage - Crawler: %s, Database: %s", config.CrawlerName, config.DatabaseName)
} else {
	csvWriter, err := NewBatchWriter(siteName, config, stats)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create CSV writer: %v", err)
	}
	writer = csvWriter
	log.Printf("Using CSV files for storage - Crawler: %s, Database: %s", config.CrawlerName, config.DatabaseName)
}
defer writer.Close()

visited := &sync.Map{}

// Enhanced error handling for HTTP requests
c.OnError(func(r *colly.Response, err error) {
	errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Request error for %s: %v", r.Request.URL, err)
	log.Printf("%s", errMsg)
	stats.AddError(errMsg)
	stats.IncrementErrors()
})

// Performance monitoring
go func() {
	ticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)
	defer ticker.Stop()
	for range ticker.C {
		stats.PrintStats()
	}
}()

// Enhanced OnHTML callback with better error handling
c.OnHTML("a[href]", func(e *colly.HTMLElement) {
	link := e.Request.AbsoluteURL(e.Attr("href"))
	if link == "" || !isValidURL(link) {
		return
	}

	if isAssetURL(link) {
		return // Skip asset/media URLs
	}
	cleanLink := cleanURL(link)
	if cleanLink == "" {
		return
	}
	if hasBlockedExtension(cleanLink) {
		return // Skip assets
	}
	// Use sync.Map for thread-safe operations
	if _, exists := visited.LoadOrStore(cleanLink, true); exists {
		return
	}

	writer.Add(URLData{
		URL:       cleanLink,
		TimeStamp: time.Now(),
		SiteName:  siteName,
	})

	if strings.Contains(cleanLink, STARTURL) {
		if err := e.Request.Visit(cleanLink); err != nil {
			errMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Failed to visit %s: %v", cleanLink, err)
			stats.AddError(errMsg)
		}
	}
})

log.Printf("Starting crawl for %s using crawler '%s'", STARTURL, config.CrawlerName)

if err := c.Visit(parsed.String()); err != nil {
	log.Fatalf("Error starting crawl: %v", err)
}

done := make(chan bool)
go func() {
	c.Wait()
	done <- true
}()

select {
case <-done:
	log.Println("Crawl completed normally")
case <-time.After(time.Duration(config.TimeoutMinutes) * time.Minute):
	log.Println("Crawl timed out")
}

writer.Flush()
stats.PrintStats()

log.Println("Crawl finished successfully")

}

func isSQLiteDatabase(databaseName string) bool { return strings.HasSuffix(strings.ToLower(databaseName), “.db”) }

func loadConfig(path string) (*Config, error) { file, err := os.Open(path) if err != nil { return nil, fmt.Errorf(“failed to open config file: %w”, err) } defer file.Close()

var cfg Config
if err := json.NewDecoder(file).Decode(&cfg); err != nil {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to decode config JSON: %w", err)
}
return &cfg, nil

}

func writeToCSV(filename string, results []URLData) error { file, err := os.Create(filename) if err != nil { return fmt.Errorf(“failed to create CSV file: %w”, err) } defer file.Close()

writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
defer writer.Flush()

if err := writer.Write([]string{"URL", "Timestamp", "SiteName"}); err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("failed to write CSV header: %w", err)
}

for _, r := range results {
	if err := writer.Write([]string{r.URL, r.TimeStamp.Format(time.RFC3339), r.SiteName}); err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write CSV row: %w", err)
	}
}
return nil

}

func isValidURL(urlStr string) bool { u, err := url.Parse(urlStr) return err == nil && (u.Scheme == “http” || u.Scheme == “https”) && u.Host != "" }

func cleanURL(urlStr string) string { u, err := url.Parse(urlStr) if err != nil { return "" } u.Fragment = "" // Remove # anchors only return u.String() }

package main

import ( “database/sql” “encoding/csv” “fmt” “log” “os” “path/filepath”

_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"

)

func main() { // Get arguments args := os.Args if len(args) < 2 { fmt.Println(“Usage: go run main.go <folder_path> [dbname]”) return }

root := args[1]
dbname := "justdata.db"
if len(args) > 2 {
	dbname = args[2]
}

// Open SQLite DB
db, err := sql.Open("sqlite3", dbname)
if err != nil {
	log.Fatal(err)
}
defer db.Close()

// Create table if not exists
createTable := `
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS urls (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	url TEXT,
	timestamp TEXT
);`
_, err = db.Exec(createTable)
if err != nil {
	log.Fatal(err)
}

// Walk through all folders for CSV
err = filepath.Walk(root, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
	if !info.IsDir() && filepath.Ext(path) == ".csv" {
		fmt.Println("Processing:", path)
		if err := processCSV(db, path); err != nil {
			log.Println("Error processing", path, ":", err)
		}
	}
	return nil
})
if err != nil {
	log.Fatal(err)
}

}

func processCSV(db *sql.DB, filename string) error { file, err := os.Open(filename) if err != nil { return err } defer file.Close()

reader := csv.NewReader(file)

records, err := reader.ReadAll()
if err != nil {
	return err
}

for i, row := range records {
	if i == 0 {
		continue // skip header
	}
	if len(row) < 2 {
		continue
	}
	url := row[0]
	timestamp := row[1]

	_, err := db.Exec("INSERT INTO urls (url, timestamp) VALUES (?, ?)", url, timestamp)
	if err != nil {
		return err
	}
}
return nil

}

package main

import ( “encoding/csv” “encoding/json” “fmt” “log” “net/http” “net/url” “os” “path/filepath” “strconv” “strings” “sync” “time”

"github.com/PuerkitoBio/goquery"
"database/sql"
_ "github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3"

)

func printHelp() { fmt.Println(“Usage:”) fmt.Println(" scraper [urlfile]") fmt.Println(" scraper –genconfig ") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Example:”) fmt.Println(" scraper nyandcompany.com nyandcompanyconfig.json urls.txt") fmt.Println(" scraper –genconfig nyandcompany.com") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“If [urlfile] is not given, scraper will look for:”) fmt.Println(" _urls.txt") fmt.Println(" _urls.csv") fmt.Println(" urls.txt") fmt.Println(" urls.csv") fmt.Println("") fmt.Println(“Options:”) fmt.Println(" -h, –help Show this help message") fmt.Println(" –genconfig Generate a default config file for a site") }

var STARTURL string var AllowedDomains []string

func genScraperConfig(siteURL string) error { // Parse the URL to get domain parsed, err := url.Parse(siteURL) if err != nil { return fmt.Errorf(“invalid URL: %v”, err) }

domain := strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")

// Create config with default values
config := Config{
	SpiderConfig: SpiderConfig{
		Name:           strings.ReplaceAll(domain, ".", "_") + "_scraper",
		BaseURL:        "",
		OutputDir:      "./output",
		RateLimitMs:    500,
		BatchSize:      10,
		TimeoutSeconds: 30,
		ChannelBuffer:  100,
	},
	ScrapingConfig: ScrapingConfig{
		Brand:            "Generic Brand",
		SiteName:         domain,
		Country:          "Global",
		CurrencyFallback: "INR",
	},
	Selectors: Selectors{
		Title:        []string{"meta[property='og:title']", "meta[name='title']", "title", "h1"},
		Description:  []string{"meta[property='og:description']", "meta[name='description']", ".product-description", ".description"},
		MainImage:    []string{"meta[property='og:image:secure_url']", "meta[property='og:image']", ".product-image img", ".main-image img", "img[data-main-image]"},
		Price:        []string{"meta[property='product:price:amount']", ".price", ".current-price", "[data-price]"},
		Currency:     []string{"meta[property='product:price:currency']", "[data-currency]"},
		SalePrice:    []string{".sale-price", ".discounted-price", "[data-sale-price]"},
		Sizes:        []string{"select[name*='size'] option", "select[name*='Size'] option", ".size-selector option", ".sizes .size"},
		Availability: []string{"button[id*='AddToCart']", ".add-to-cart", ".buy-now"},
		SKU:          []string{"[data-sku]", ".sku"},
		Category:     []string{".breadcrumbs a:last-child", ".category"},
	},
	ExtractionRules: ExtractionRules{
		CollectionPaths:      []string{"/collections/", "/category/"},
		ProductPaths:         []string{"/products/", "/item/"},
		CollectionFromURL:    "/collections/",
		ProductURLFilter:     "/products/",
		AvailabilityKeywords: []string{"sold out", "out of stock", "unavailable"},
		SizeFilters:          []string{"select size", "choose size", "pick size"},
		PriceCleanup: struct {
			RemoveChars  []string `json:"remove_chars"`
			ParseAsFloat bool     `json:"parse_as_float"`
		}{
			RemoveChars:  []string{",", "$", "₹", "€", "£"},
			ParseAsFloat: true,
		},
	},
	FallbackExtraction: FallbackExtraction{
		EnableJSONLD:         true,
		EnableMicrodata:      true,
		EnableTextExtraction: true,
	},
}

// Generate filename
filename := strings.ReplaceAll(domain, ".", "_") + "_config.json"

// Convert to JSON with proper indentation
jsonData, err := json.MarshalIndent(config, "", "  ")
if err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("error marshaling config: %v", err)
}

// Write to file
err = os.WriteFile(filename, jsonData, 0644)
if err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("error writing config file: %v", err)
}

fmt.Printf("Generated config file: %s\n", filename)
return nil

}

func main() { if len(os.Args) < 2 { printHelp() os.Exit(1) }

// Help flag
if strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "-h") || strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "--help") {
	printHelp()
	return
}
// Generate config flag
if strings.EqualFold(os.Args[1], "--genconfig") {
	if len(os.Args) < 3 {
		log.Fatal("Error: --genconfig requires a site URL")
	}
	rawInput := os.Args[2]
	if !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "http://") && !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "https://") {
		rawInput = "https://" + rawInput
	}
	err := genScraperConfig(rawInput)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
	return
}

if len(os.Args) < 3 {
	log.Fatal("Error: Missing arguments. Run with --help for usage.")
}

// Normalize input URL
rawInput := os.Args[1]
if !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "http://") && !strings.HasPrefix(rawInput, "https://") {
	rawInput = "https://" + rawInput
}

parsed, err := url.Parse(rawInput)
if err != nil {
	log.Fatalf("Invalid URL: %v", err)
}

// Extract clean domain
host := strings.TrimPrefix(parsed.Host, "www.")

// Store for scraper
STARTURL = rawInput
AllowedDomains = []string{host, "www." + host}

log.Printf("Scraping site: %s (allowed domains: %v)\n", STARTURL, AllowedDomains)

// Remaining arguments
configFile := os.Args[2]
var urlFile string
if len(os.Args) >= 4 {
	urlFile = os.Args[3]
}

err = RunScraper(STARTURL, configFile, urlFile) // pass normalized URL
if err != nil {
	log.Fatal(err)
}

} func RunScraper(siteName, configFile, urlFile string) error { fmt.Println(“Starting scraper for”, siteName, “with config”, configFile)

// Load config
config, err := LoadConfig(configFile)
if err != nil {
	return fmt.Errorf("error loading config: %v", err)
}

fmt.Printf("Loaded config for: %s\n", config.SpiderConfig.Name)

// Load URLs
var urls []string
if urlFile != "" {
	urls, err = LoadURLsFromFile(urlFile)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("error loading URLs from %s: %v", urlFile, err)
	}
} else {
	defaultFiles := []string{
		fmt.Sprintf("%s_urls.txt", siteName),
		fmt.Sprintf("%s_urls.csv", siteName),
		"urls.txt",
		"urls.csv",
	}
	for _, f := range defaultFiles {
		if fileUrls, err := LoadURLsFromFile(f); err == nil && len(fileUrls) > 0 {
			urls = fileUrls
			fmt.Printf("Loaded %d URLs from %s\n", len(urls), f)
			break
		}
	}
}

if len(urls) == 0 {
	return fmt.Errorf("no URLs found. Provide a file or create one like %s_urls.txt", siteName)
}

// Filter product URLs
var productURLs []string
for _, url := range urls {
	if len(config.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths) > 0 {
		for _, path := range config.ExtractionRules.ProductPaths {
			if strings.Contains(url, path) {
				productURLs = append(productURLs, url)
				break
			}
		}
	} else if config.ExtractionRules.ProductURLFilter != "" {
		if strings.Contains(url, config.ExtractionRules.ProductURLFilter) {
			productURLs = append(productURLs, url)
		}
	}
}

if len(productURLs) == 0 {
	return fmt.Errorf("no valid product URLs found")
}

fmt.Printf("Found %d product URLs\n", len(productURLs))
fmt.Printf("Starting scraping with rate limit: %dms, batch size: %d\n",
	config.SpiderConfig.RateLimitMs, config.SpiderConfig.BatchSize)

spider := NewGenericSpider(config)
return spider.ScrapeURLs(productURLs)

}

func LoadURLsFromFile(path string) ([]string, error) { f, err := os.Open(path) if err != nil { return nil, err } defer f.Close()

var urls []string
if strings.HasSuffix(strings.ToLower(path), ".csv") {
	r := csv.NewReader(f)
	records, err := r.ReadAll()
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	for _, rec := range records {
		if len(rec) > 0 && strings.TrimSpace(rec[0]) != "" {
			urls = append(urls, strings.TrimSpace(rec[0]))
		}
	}
} else {
	buf, err := os.ReadFile(path)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	lines := strings.Split(string(buf), "\n")
	for _, line := range lines {
		if trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(line); trimmed != "" {
			urls = append(urls, trimmed)
		}
	}
}
return urls, nil

}

// Helper function func contains(s, substr string) bool { if substr == "" { return true } for i := 0; i <= len(s)-len(substr); i++ { if s[i:i+len(substr)] == substr { return true } } return false }

// scraper code starts from here //

// Updated structs to support arrays of selectors type Selectors struct { Title []string json:"title" Description []string json:"description" MainImage []string json:"main_image" Price []string json:"price" Currency []string json:"currency" SalePrice []string json:"sale_price" Sizes []string json:"sizes" Availability []string json:"availability" SKU []string json:"sku" Category []string json:"category" }

type ExtractionRules struct { CollectionPaths []string json:"collection_paths" ProductPaths []string json:"product_paths" CollectionFromURL string json:"collection_from_url" ProductURLFilter string json:"product_url_filter" AvailabilityKeywords []string json:"availability_keywords" SizeFilters []string json:"size_filters" PriceCleanup struct { RemoveChars []string json:"remove_chars" ParseAsFloat bool json:"parse_as_float" } json:"price_cleanup" }

type FallbackExtraction struct { EnableJSONLD bool json:"enable_json_ld" EnableMicrodata bool json:"enable_microdata" EnableTextExtraction bool json:"enable_text_extraction" }

type Config struct { SpiderConfig SpiderConfig json:"spider_config" ScrapingConfig ScrapingConfig json:"scraping_config" Selectors Selectors json:"selectors" ExtractionRules ExtractionRules json:"extraction_rules" OutputFormat OutputFormat json:"output_format" FallbackExtraction FallbackExtraction json:"fallback_extraction" }

// Rest of the structs remain the same… type SpiderConfig struct { Name string json:"name" BaseURL string json:"base_url" OutputDir string json:"output_dir" RateLimitMs int json:"rate_limit_ms" BatchSize int json:"batch_size" TimeoutSeconds int json:"timeout_seconds" ChannelBuffer int json:"channel_buffer" }

type ScrapingConfig struct { Brand string json:"brand" SiteName string json:"site_name" Country string json:"country" CurrencyFallback string json:"currency_fallback" }

type OutputFormat struct { Headers []string json:"headers" }

type ProductItem struct { URL string Title string Description string Price float64 SalePrice float64 Currency string MainImage string Sizes []string Availability bool Brand string SiteName string Country string Collection string Timestamp string SKU string Category string }

type GenericSpider struct { client *http.Client config *Config rateLimit <-chan time.Time productChan chan ProductItem wg sync.WaitGroup mutex sync.Mutex }

func NewGenericSpider(config *Config) *GenericSpider { return &GenericSpider{ client: &http.Client{ Timeout: time.Duration(config.SpiderConfig.TimeoutSeconds) * time.Second, }, config: config, rateLimit: time.Tick(time.Duration(config.SpiderConfig.RateLimitMs) * time.Millisecond), productChan: make(chan ProductItem, config.SpiderConfig.ChannelBuffer), } }

func (s *GenericSpider) ScrapeURLs(urls []string) error { os.MkdirAll(s.config.SpiderConfig.OutputDir, 0755)

timestamp := time.Now().Format("20060102_150405")
outputFile := filepath.Join(s.config.SpiderConfig.OutputDir, fmt.Sprintf("%s_%s.csv", s.config.SpiderConfig.Name, timestamp))

file, err := os.Create(outputFile)
if err != nil {
	return err
}
defer file.Close()

writer := csv.NewWriter(file)
defer writer.Flush()

// Default headers if not specified
headers := s.config.OutputFormat.Headers
if len(headers) == 0 {
	headers = []string{
		"url", "title", "description", "price", "sale_price", "currency",
		"image_url", "sizes", "availability", "brand", "site_name", "country",
		"collection", "timestamp", "sku", "category",
	}
}
writer.Write(headers)

batchSize := s.config.SpiderConfig.BatchSize
totalBatches := (len(urls) + batchSize - 1) / batchSize

for i := 0; i < len(urls); i += batchSize {
	end := i + batchSize
	if end > len(urls) {
		end = len(urls)
	}

	batch := urls[i:end]
	batchNum := (i / batchSize) + 1
	fmt.Printf("Processing batch %d of %d (%d URLs)\n", batchNum, totalBatches, len(batch))

	s.processBatch(batch, writer)
	fmt.Printf("Completed batch %d of %d\n", batchNum, totalBatches)
}

s.wg.Wait()
close(s.productChan)
fmt.Printf("Output saved to: %s\n", outputFile)
return nil

}

func (s *GenericSpider) processBatch(urls []string, writer *csv.Writer) { resultChan := make(chan ProductItem, len(urls))

for _, url := range urls {
	s.wg.Add(1)
	go func(url string) {
		defer s.wg.Done()
		<-s.rateLimit

		fmt.Printf("Scraping URL: %s\n", url)
		product := s.scrapeProduct(url)
		if product != nil {
			resultChan <- *product
		}
	}(url)
}

go func() {
	s.wg.Wait()
	close(resultChan)
}()

for product := range resultChan {
	record := []string{
		product.URL,
		product.Title,
		product.Description,
		fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.Price),
		fmt.Sprintf("%.2f", product.SalePrice),
		product.Currency,
		product.MainImage,
		strings.Join(product.Sizes, ", "),
		fmt.Sprintf("%v", product.Availability),
		product.Brand,
		product.SiteName,
		product.Country,
		product.Collection,
		product.Timestamp,
		product.SKU,
		product.Category,
	}

	s.mutex.Lock()
	writer.Write(record)
	writer.Flush()
	s.mutex.Unlock()
}

}

// Universal extraction method func (s *GenericSpider) scrapeProduct(url string) *ProductItem { resp, err := s.client.Get(url) if err != nil { fmt.Printf(“Error fetching %s: %v\n”, url, err) return nil } defer resp.Body.Close()

doc, err := goquery.NewDocumentFromReader(resp.Body)
if err != nil {
	fmt.Printf("Error parsing %s: %v\n", url, err)
	return nil
}

product := &ProductItem{
	URL:       url,
	Brand:     s.config.ScrapingConfig.Brand,
	SiteName:  s.config.ScrapingConfig.SiteName,
	Country:   s.config.ScrapingConfig.Country,
	Timestamp: time.Now().Format(time.RFC3339),
	Currency:  s.config.ScrapingConfig.CurrencyFallback,
}

// Universal extraction using multiple selectors
product.Title = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Title, "content", "text")
product.Description = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Description, "content", "text")
product.MainImage = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.MainImage, "content", "src", "data-src")
product.SKU = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.SKU, "content", "text", "data-sku")
product.Category = s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Category, "text", "content")

// Extract currency
if currency := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Currency, "content", "text"); currency != "" {
	product.Currency = currency
}

// Extract price
if priceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.Price, "content", "text", "data-price"); priceStr != "" {
	product.Price = s.cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr)
}

// Extract sale price
if salePriceStr := s.extractWithSelectors(doc, s.config.Selectors.SalePrice, "content", "text", "data-sale-price"); salePriceStr != "" {
	product.SalePrice = s.cleanAndParsePrice(salePriceStr)
}

// Extract sizes
product.Sizes = s.extractSizes(doc)

// Check availability
product.Availability = s.checkAvailability(doc)

// Extract collection from URL
if s.config.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL != "" {
	if parts := strings.Split(url, s.config.ExtractionRules.CollectionFromURL); len(parts) > 1 {
		product.Collection = strings.Split(parts[1], "/")[0]
	}
}

// JSON-LD fallback extraction
if s.config.FallbackExtraction.EnableJSONLD {
	s.extractFromJSONLD(doc, product)
}

fmt.Printf("Successfully scraped: %s (Price: %.2f, Sale Price: %.2f)\n", url, product.Price, product.SalePrice)
return product

}

// Helper method to try multiple selectors func (s *GenericSpider) extractWithSelectors(doc *goquery.Document, selectors []string, attrs …string) string { for _, selector := range selectors { if selector == "" { continue }

	selection := doc.Find(selector)
	if selection.Length() > 0 {
		// Try each attribute
		for _, attr := range attrs {
			var value string
			if attr == "text" {
				value = strings.TrimSpace(selection.First().Text())
			} else {
				value = selection.First().AttrOr(attr, "")
			}
			if value != "" {
				return value
			}
		}
	}
}
return ""

}

func (s *GenericSpider) cleanAndParsePrice(priceStr string) float64 { // Clean price string for _, char := range s.config.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.RemoveChars { priceStr = strings.ReplaceAll(priceStr, char, “”) }

priceStr = strings.TrimSpace(priceStr)

if s.config.ExtractionRules.PriceCleanup.ParseAsFloat {
	if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(priceStr, 64); err == nil {
		return price
	}
}
return 0.0

}

func (s *GenericSpider) extractSizes(doc *goquery.Document) []string { sizeMap := make(map[string]bool)

for _, selector := range s.config.Selectors.Sizes {
	doc.Find(selector).Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) {
		size := strings.TrimSpace(sel.Text())
		if size != "" {
			// Filter out common non-size text
			isValidSize := true
			for _, filter := range s.config.ExtractionRules.SizeFilters {
				if strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(size), strings.ToLower(filter)) {
					isValidSize = false
					break
				}
			}
			if isValidSize {
				sizeMap[size] = true
			}
		}
	})
}

var sizes []string
for size := range sizeMap {
	sizes = append(sizes, size)
}
return sizes

}

func (s *GenericSpider) checkAvailability(doc *goquery.Document) bool { for _, selector := range s.config.Selectors.Availability { element := doc.Find(selector) if element.Length() > 0 { text := strings.ToLower(element.Text()) for _, keyword := range s.config.ExtractionRules.AvailabilityKeywords { if strings.Contains(text, strings.ToLower(keyword)) { return false } } return true } } return true // Default to available if can’t determine }

func (s *GenericSpider) extractFromJSONLD(doc *goquery.Document, product *ProductItem) { doc.Find(“script[type=‘application/ld+json’]”).Each(func(i int, sel *goquery.Selection) { jsonData := sel.Text() if strings.Contains(jsonData, “Product”) { var schemaData map[string]interface{} if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonData), &schemaData); err == nil { // Extract what we can from structured data if offers, ok := schemaData[“offers”].([]interface{}); ok && len(offers) > 0 { if offer, ok := offers[0].(map[string]interface{}); ok { if price, ok := offer[“price”].(float64); ok && product.SalePrice == 0 { product.SalePrice = price } if sku, ok := offer[“sku”].(string); ok && product.SKU == "" { product.SKU = sku } } } } } }) }

func LoadConfig(configPath string) (*Config, error) { file, err := os.Open(configPath) if err != nil { return nil, err } defer file.Close()

var config Config
decoder := json.NewDecoder(file)
err = decoder.Decode(&config)
return &config, err

}

// LoadURLsFromSQLite loads URLs from sqlite database, table & field name provided as arguments func LoadURLsFromSQLite(dbPath, table, field string) ([]string, error) { db, err := sql.Open(“sqlite3”, dbPath) if err != nil { return nil, err } defer db.Close() rows, err := db.Query(“SELECT " + field + " FROM " + table) if err != nil { return nil, err } defer rows.Close() var urls []string for rows.Next() { var url string if err := rows.Scan(&url); err == nil && strings.TrimSpace(url) != "” { urls = append(urls, url) } } return urls, nil }



### File: main.go

package main

import ( “context” “log” “net/http” “strconv” “strings” “time”

"github.com/gin-gonic/gin"
"go.mongodb.org/mongo-driver/bson"
"go.mongodb.org/mongo-driver/bson/primitive"
"go.mongodb.org/mongo-driver/mongo"
"go.mongodb.org/mongo-driver/mongo/options"

)

var collection *mongo.Collection

// Universal Product Structure type Product struct { ID primitive.ObjectID json:"id,omitempty" bson:"_id,omitempty" Name string json:"name" bson:"name" Price float64 json:"price" bson:"price" Category string json:"category" bson:"category" SubCategory string json:"sub_category,omitempty" bson:"sub_category,omitempty" Brand string json:"brand,omitempty" bson:"brand,omitempty" Description string json:"description,omitempty" bson:"description,omitempty" SKU string json:"sku,omitempty" bson:"sku,omitempty" Stock int json:"stock" bson:"stock" Images []string json:"images,omitempty" bson:"images,omitempty" Tags []string json:"tags,omitempty" bson:"tags,omitempty" Currency string json:"currency" bson:"currency" Country string json:"country,omitempty" bson:"country,omitempty" Availability string json:"availability" bson:"availability" // in_stock, out_of_stock, pre_order

// Dynamic fi	elds - This is the key to extensibility
Attributes map[string]interface{} `json:"attributes,omitempty" bson:"attributes,omitempty"`

// Metadata
CreatedAt time.Time `json:"created_at" bson:"created_at"`
UpdatedAt time.Time `json:"updated_at" bson:"updated_at"`

}

// Response structure type Response struct { Data interface{} json:"data" Total int64 json:"total,omitempty" Page int json:"page,omitempty" Limit int json:"limit,omitempty" Pages int64 json:"pages,omitempty" }

func init() { // MongoDB connection clientOptions := options.Client().ApplyURI(“mongodb://localhost:27017”) client, err := mongo.NewClient(clientOptions) if err != nil { log.Fatal(“MongoDB connection error:”, err) }

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10*time.Second)
defer cancel()

if err = client.Connect(ctx); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("MongoDB connection failed:", err)
}

// Test connection
if err = client.Ping(ctx, nil); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("MongoDB ping failed:", err)
}

collection = client.Database("shopdb").Collection("products")
log.Println("Connected to MongoDB successfully")

// Create indexes for better performance

}

// CREATE Product func CreateProduct(c *gin.Context) { var product Product if err := c.ShouldBindJSON(&product); err != nil { c.JSON(http.StatusBadRequest, gin.H{“error”: “Invalid JSON: " + err.Error()}) return }

// Validate required fields
if product.Name == "" || product.Category == "" || product.Price <= 0 {
	c.JSON(http.StatusBadRequest, gin.H{
		"error": "Required fields missing. Name, Category, and Price > 0 are required",
	})
	return
}

// Set defaults
now := time.Now()
product.CreatedAt = now
product.UpdatedAt = now

if product.Currency == "" {
	product.Currency = "USD"
}
if product.Availability == "" {
	product.Availability = "in_stock"
}

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
defer cancel()

result, err := collection.InsertOne(ctx, product)
if err != nil {
	if mongo.IsDuplicateKeyError(err) {
		c.JSON(http.StatusConflict, gin.H{"error": "SKU already exists"})
		return
	}
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Failed to create product: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

c.JSON(http.StatusCreated, gin.H{
	"message": "Product created successfully",
	"id":      result.InsertedID,
	"sku":     product.SKU,
})

}

// READ Products with universal filtering func GetProducts(c *gin.Context) { filter := bson.M{}

// Build filter dynamically from query parameters
buildFilter(c, filter)

// Pagination
page, _ := strconv.Atoi(c.DefaultQuery("page", "1"))
limit, _ := strconv.Atoi(c.DefaultQuery("limit", "20"))
if limit > 100 {
	limit = 100 // Prevent excessive data retrieval
}
skip := (page - 1) * limit

// Sorting
sort := buildSort(c)

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 30*time.Second)
defer cancel()

// Find options
findOptions := options.Find().
	SetSkip(int64(skip)).
	SetLimit(int64(limit)).
	SetSort(sort)

cursor, err := collection.Find(ctx, filter, findOptions)
if err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Query failed: " + err.Error()})
	return
}
defer cursor.Close(ctx)

var products []Product
if err = cursor.All(ctx, &products); err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Failed to decode results: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

// Get total count for pagination
total, _ := collection.CountDocuments(ctx, filter)
pages := (total + int64(limit) - 1) / int64(limit)

response := Response{
	Data:  products,
	Total: total,
	Page:  page,
	Limit: limit,
	Pages: pages,
}

c.JSON(http.StatusOK, response)

}

// Universal filter builder func buildFilter(c *gin.Context, filter bson.M) { // Basic string filters stringFilters := []string{“category”, “sub_category”, “brand”, “country”, “availability”, “currency”} for _, field := range stringFilters { if value := c.Query(field); value != "” { // Case-insensitive partial match filter[field] = primitive.Regex{Pattern: value, Options: “i”} } }

// Exact match filters
if sku := c.Query("sku"); sku != "" {
	filter["sku"] = sku
}

// Price range filters
if minPrice := c.Query("min_price"); minPrice != "" {
	if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(minPrice, 64); err == nil && price >= 0 {
		if existing, ok := filter["price"].(bson.M); ok {
			existing["$gte"] = price
		} else {
			filter["price"] = bson.M{"$gte": price}
		}
	}
}
if maxPrice := c.Query("max_price"); maxPrice != "" {
	if price, err := strconv.ParseFloat(maxPrice, 64); err == nil && price > 0 {
		if existing, ok := filter["price"].(bson.M); ok {
			existing["$lte"] = price
		} else {
			filter["price"] = bson.M{"$lte": price}
		}
	}
}

// Rating filter
if minRating := c.Query("min_rating"); minRating != "" {
	if rating, err := strconv.ParseFloat(minRating, 64); err == nil && rating >= 0 && rating <= 5 {
		filter["rating"] = bson.M{"$gte": rating}
	}
}

// Stock filter
if inStock := c.Query("in_stock"); inStock == "true" {
	filter["stock"] = bson.M{"$gt": 0}
}
if minStock := c.Query("min_stock"); minStock != "" {
	if stock, err := strconv.Atoi(minStock); err == nil && stock >= 0 {
		filter["stock"] = bson.M{"$gte": stock}
	}
}

// Tags filter (array contains)
if tags := c.Query("tags"); tags != "" {
	tagList := strings.Split(tags, ",")
	filter["tags"] = bson.M{"$in": tagList}
}

// Dynamic attribute filters (this is where the magic happens)
// Any query parameter starting with 'attr_' will be treated as an attribute filter
for key, values := range c.Request.URL.Query() {
	if strings.HasPrefix(key, "attr_") {
		attrName := strings.TrimPrefix(key, "attr_")
		filter["attributes."+attrName] = values[0]
	}
}

// Full-text search
if q := c.Query("q"); q != "" {
	filter["$text"] = bson.M{"$search": q}
}

}

// Universal sort builder func buildSort(c *gin.Context) bson.D { sortField := c.DefaultQuery(“sort”, “created_at”) sortOrder := 1 if c.Query(“order”) == “desc” { sortOrder = -1 }

// Validate sort field to prevent injection
validSortFields := []string{
	"name", "price", "category", "sub_category", "brand", "rating",
	"stock", "created_at", "updated_at", "review_count",
}

isValid := false
for _, field := range validSortFields {
	if sortField == field {
		isValid = true
		break
	}
}

if !isValid {
	sortField = "created_at"
}

return bson.D{{Key: sortField, Value: sortOrder}}

}

// READ Single Product func GetProduct(c *gin.Context) { identifier := c.Param(“id”) filter := bson.M{}

// Try to find by ObjectID first, then by SKU
if objID, err := primitive.ObjectIDFromHex(identifier); err == nil {
	filter["_id"] = objID
} else {
	filter["sku"] = identifier
}

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
defer cancel()

var product Product
err := collection.FindOne(ctx, filter).Decode(&product)
if err != nil {
	if err == mongo.ErrNoDocuments {
		c.JSON(http.StatusNotFound, gin.H{"error": "Product not found"})
		return
	}
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Query failed: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

c.JSON(http.StatusOK, Response{Data: product})

}

// PATCH Product (partial update) func PatchProduct(c *gin.Context) { identifier := c.Param(“id”) filter := bson.M{}

if objID, err := primitive.ObjectIDFromHex(identifier); err == nil {
	filter["_id"] = objID
} else {
	filter["sku"] = identifier
}

var patchData map[string]interface{}
if err := c.ShouldBindJSON(&patchData); err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusBadRequest, gin.H{"error": "Invalid JSON: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

if len(patchData) == 0 {
	c.JSON(http.StatusBadRequest, gin.H{"error": "No data provided for update"})
	return
}

// Remove protected fields
delete(patchData, "_id")
delete(patchData, "created_at")

// Set updated timestamp
patchData["updated_at"] = time.Now()

update := bson.M{"$set": patchData}

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
defer cancel()

result, err := collection.UpdateOne(ctx, filter, update)
if err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Patch failed: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

if result.MatchedCount == 0 {
	c.JSON(http.StatusNotFound, gin.H{"error": "Product not found"})
	return
}

c.JSON(http.StatusOK, gin.H{
	"message":  "Product patched successfully",
	"modified": result.ModifiedCount,
})

}

// DELETE Product func DeleteProduct(c *gin.Context) { identifier := c.Param(“id”) filter := bson.M{}

if objID, err := primitive.ObjectIDFromHex(identifier); err == nil {
	filter["_id"] = objID
} else {
	filter["sku"] = identifier
}

ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
defer cancel()

result, err := collection.DeleteOne(ctx, filter)
if err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Delete failed: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

if result.DeletedCount == 0 {
	c.JSON(http.StatusNotFound, gin.H{"error": "Product not found"})
	return
}

c.JSON(http.StatusOK, gin.H{
	"message": "Product deleted successfully",
	"deleted": result.DeletedCount,
})

}

// Get product statistics func GetProductStats(c gin.Context) { ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10time.Second) defer cancel()

// Aggregation pipeline for statistics
pipeline := []bson.M{
	{
		"$group": bson.M{
			"_id":        "$category",
			"count":      bson.M{"$sum": 1},
			"avgPrice":   bson.M{"$avg": "$price"},
			"minPrice":   bson.M{"$min": "$price"},
			"maxPrice":   bson.M{"$max": "$price"},
			"totalStock": bson.M{"$sum": "$stock"},
			"avgRating":  bson.M{"$avg": "$rating"},
		},
	},
	{
		"$sort": bson.M{"count": -1},
	},
}

cursor, err := collection.Aggregate(ctx, pipeline)
if err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Stats query failed: " + err.Error()})
	return
}
defer cursor.Close(ctx)

var stats []bson.M
if err = cursor.All(ctx, &stats); err != nil {
	c.JSON(http.StatusInternalServerError, gin.H{"error": "Failed to decode stats: " + err.Error()})
	return
}

// Get total count
totalCount, _ := collection.CountDocuments(ctx, bson.M{})

c.JSON(http.StatusOK, gin.H{
	"total_products": totalCount,
	"category_stats": stats,
})

}

func main() { r := gin.Default()

// Add CORS middleware for web applications
r.Use(func(c *gin.Context) {
	c.Header("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
	c.Header("Access-Control-Allow-Methods", "GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE, OPTIONS")
	c.Header("Access-Control-Allow-Headers", "Content-Type, Authorization")

	if c.Request.Method == "OPTIONS" {
		c.AbortWithStatus(204)
		return
	}

	c.Next()
})

// Product CRUD routes
r.POST("/products", CreateProduct)
r.GET("/products", GetProducts)
r.GET("/products/:id", GetProduct)
r.PATCH("/products/:id", PatchProduct)
r.DELETE("/products/:id", DeleteProduct)

// Statistics
r.GET("/products/stats", GetProductStats)

// Health check
r.GET("/health", func(c *gin.Context) {
	c.JSON(http.StatusOK, gin.H{
		"status":    "OK",
		"timestamp": time.Now(),
		"service":   "Product Management API",
	})
})

if err := r.Run(":8080"); err != nil {
	log.Fatal("Server failed to start:", err)
}

}



### File: project context.md

E-commerce Product Search Engine Project Overview Project Structure Copysitename/ ├── .htaccess # URL rewriting configuration ├── index.php # Main router file ├── products.db # SQLite database containing product data │ ├── assets/ │ ├── css/ │ │ └── style.css # Main stylesheet │ └── js/ │ └── main.js # JavaScript functionality │ ├── config/ │ ├── config.php # Global configuration settings │ ├── database.php # Database connection and queries │ └── functions.php # Helper functions │ ├── includes/ │ ├── header.php # Site header with navigation │ ├── footer.php # Site footer │ └── sidebar.php # Filter sidebar │ └── pages/ ├── home.php # Homepage with product grid ├── product.php # Product detail page ├── brand.php # Brand-specific product listing ├── contact.php # Contact page (placeholder) └── 404.php # 404 error page Key Features

Clean URL Routing: Uses a simple routing system for clean URLs (/product/123, /brand/nike) Product Filtering: Multi-select filters for brands, categories, countries, etc. Dynamic Search: Search functionality for product titles and descriptions Sticky Sidebar: Sidebar with filters stays visible when scrolling Responsive Design: Mobile-friendly interface using Bootstrap Pagination: Shows 50 products per page with proper pagination Random Products: Shows random products on homepage load for discovery

Main Files and Their Functions

  1. .htaccess - URL Rewriting Routes all non-file/directory requests to index.php for handling clean URLs.
  2. index.php - Main Router Processes URL routes and loads the appropriate pages based on the URL path.
  3. config/config.php - Global Configuration Contains site-wide constants like site name, base URL, and database path.
  4. config/database.php - Database Functions Contains all database interaction functions:

getDbConnection(): Establishes SQLite connection getProducts(): Retrieves filtered products with pagination getRandomProducts(): Gets random product selection getProductById(): Gets single product details getFilterOptions(): Gets all available filter options getRelatedProducts(): Gets products related to current one getBrandCategories(): Gets categories for a specific brand getTotalProductCount(): Gets total number of products getRandomProductsForPage(): Gets random products for current page

  1. config/functions.php - Helper Functions Contains utility functions:

buildUrl(): Constructs URLs with parameters getCurrentFilters(): Gets current filter state from URL getCurrentPage(): Gets current pagination page buildPaginationUrl(): Builds URLs for pagination links escapeHtml(): Sanitizes output for security

  1. includes/header.php Contains the site header, navigation, and search bar.
  2. includes/sidebar.php Contains the filter sidebar with scrollable sections for each filter type.
  3. includes/footer.php Contains the site footer.
  4. pages/home.php Displays product grid with filters and pagination.
  5. pages/product.php Displays detailed product information and related products.
  6. pages/brand.php Shows products filtered by a specific brand with category sub-navigation.
  7. assets/css/style.css Contains custom styling including:

Product card designs Sticky sidebar implementation Filter scrollable areas Responsive adjustments

  1. assets/js/main.js Handles interactive elements:

Filter search functionality Multi-select checkboxes Size selection buttons on product page Wishlist button toggle Price range validation

Database Schema The products.db SQLite database contains a single products table with the following columns:

id: Product ID (INTEGER) url: Product URL (TEXT) title: Product title (TEXT) description: Product description (TEXT) price: Product price (REAL) sale_price: Sale price if applicable (REAL) currency: Currency code (TEXT) image_url: Product image URL (TEXT) sizes: Available sizes (TEXT - comma separated) availability: Stock status (TEXT - “TRUE” or “FALSE”) brand: Brand name (TEXT) site_name: Source website (TEXT) country: Country of origin (TEXT) collection: Product collection (TEXT) timestamp: Last updated timestamp (TEXT) sku: Stock keeping unit (TEXT) category: Product category (TEXT) created_at: Creation timestamp (datetime) updated_at: Update timestamp (datetime) deleted_at: Deletion timestamp (datetime)

Key Implementation Details

Router Implementation: Simple switch-case router that parses the URL and directs to appropriate page templates Filter Sidebar: Implements multi-select filtering with “Select All” functionality and individual scrollable sections for each filter type Sticky Sidebar: Uses CSS position:sticky with proper overflow handling for scrollable filters Product Grid: Responsive grid showing 4 products per row on large screens, 2 on medium, 1 on small Pagination: Shows a reasonable number of page links with previous/next buttons Random Products: Uses a seeded random query to show different products on homepage refresh while maintaining consistency within a single page view

This project provides a solid foundation for an e-commerce product search engine with filter capabilities using PHP, SQLite, and Bootstrap.
